Lch II (1)<extent></extent>
B21.2.1.1.2.
Bald's Leechbook: Cockayne 1864-6, II, 18-156 (Bk I).



 1.1.1. On þissum ærestan læcecræftum gewritene sint
læcedomas wið eallum heafdes untrymnessum.
 1.2.1. Murra hatte wyrt, gegnid on mortere þætte pening
gewege, do steap fulne wines to wose symre þonne þæt heafod mid &
drince on niht nestig.
 1.2.3. Wið heafod wærce genim rudan & wermod, gecnuwa
& meng wiþ eced & ele, aseoh þurh clað, smire mid þæt heafod
oððe clam of þam ilcan wyrc, lege on þæt heafod & besweþe wel
þonne þu to reste wille.
 1.3.1. Wið þon ilcan genim betonican & pipor, gegnid
swiðe togædere, læt ane niht hangian on claðe, smire mid.
 1.3.2. Wið heafod wærce betan wyrttruman gecnuwa wið hunig,
awring, do þæt seaw on neb & ongean sunnan upweard licge &
þæt heafod ho of dune þæt se seaw mæge þæt heafod geond
yrnan.
 1.3.5. Hæbbe him ær on muþe ele oþþe buteran &
þonne uplang aslitte hnigie forð læte flowan of þam nebbe þa
gillistran.
 1.3.6. Do swa gelome oþþæt hit clæne sie.
 1.4.1. Wið heafod wærce genim hamwyrt niþewearde, gecnuwa,
lege on ceald wæter, gnid swiðe oþþæt eall geleþred sie, beþe
mid þæt heafod.
 1.5.1. Wiþ heafod wærce genim heah heoloþan & grunde
swelgean & fencersan & gitrifan, wel on wætere, læt reocan on
þa eagan þonne hit hat sie & ymb þa eagan gnid mid þæm wyrtum
swa hatum.
 1.6.1. Wið heafod ece genim sealh & ele, do ahsan, gewyrc
þonne to slypan, do to hymlican & eofor þrotan & ða readan
netlan, gecnuwa, do þonne on þone slipan, beþe mid.
 1.6.3. Wiþ heafod ece hundes heafod gebærn to ahsan &
snið þæt heafod, lege on.
 1.7.1. Wið heafod wærce genim efelastan, gecnua on ceald
wæter, gnid betweoh handum & gecnuwa clufþung, do þærto, beþe
mid.
 1.7.2. Wiþ heafod ece genim hofan & win & eced, geswet
mid hunige & smire mid.
 1.8.1. Wiþ heafod ece genim diles blostman, seoð on ele, smire
þa þunwangan mid.
 1.8.2. Wiþ þon ilcan genim heorotes hornes ahsan, meng wið
eced & rosan seaw, bind on þæt wænge.
 1.8.3. Wiþ þon ilcan genim fæt ful grenre rudan leafa &
senepes sædes cucler fulne, gegnid togædere, do æges þæt hwite to
cucler fulne þæt sio sealf sie þicce, smire mid feþere on þa healfe
þe sar ne sie.
 1.9.1. Wiþ healfes heafdes ece genim þa readan netlan
anstelede, getrifula, meng wið eced & æges þæt hwite, do eall
togædere, smire mid.
 1.10.1. Wiþ healfes heafdes ece, laures croppan getrifula on eced
mid ele, smyre mid þy þæt wenge.
 1.11.1. Wið þon ilcan genim rudan seaw, wring on þæt
næsþyrel þe on þa saran healfe bið.
 1.12.1. Wiþ healfes heafdes ece genim laures croppan dust &
senep, meng togædere, geot eced on, smire mid þa saran healfe mid þy.
 1.12.2. Oþþe menge wið win þæs laures croppan.
 1.12.3. Oþþe rudan sæd gnid on eced, do bega emfela, gnid
ðon hneccan mid þy.
 1.13.1. Tacnu þære adle.
 1.13.1. Sio adl cymð of yfelre wætan ufan flowendre oþþe
æþme oþþe of bam.
 1.13.2. Þonne sceal mon ærest on ða adle foreweardre blod
lætan of ædre.
 1.13.3. Æfter þon sceal man wyrt drenc sellan & lacnian
siþþan þa saran stowa.
 1.13.4. Gif seo adl sie cumen of micelre hæto þonne sceal man
mid cealdum læcedomum lacnian, gif hio of cealdum intingan cymð þonne
sceal mon mid hatum læcedomum lacnian, gehwæþeres sceal mon nyttian
& miscian þæt þone lichoman hæle & æfer mægen
hæbbe.
 1.13.7. Him deah þæt him mon on eare drype gewlæccedne ele
mid oþrum godum wyrtum.
 1.14.1. Genim wiþ tobrocenum heafde betonican getrifula &
lege on þæt heafod ufan.
 1.14.2. Þonne samnað hio þa wunde & hælð.
 1.14.2. Eft wiþ þon ilcan genim tuncersan sio þe self
weaxeð & mon ne sæwð, do in þa nosu þæt se stenc mæge on
þæt heafod & þæt seaw.
 1.15.1. Wiþ þon ilcan eft genim banwyrt & attorlaþan
& dolhrunan & wudumerce & brunwyrt & betonican, do ealle þa
wyrta to wyrtdrence & menge þærwið þa smalan clifan &
centaurian & wegbrædan, ealra swiþust betonican.
 1.15.3. & gif þæt brægen utsige genim æges þæt
geoluwe & meng lythwon wið hunig & afyl ða wunde & mid acumban
besweðe & forlæt swa þonne.
 1.15.5. & eft ymb þry dagas gespæt þa wunde & gif se
hala ferþe wille habban readne hring ymb þa wunde wite þu þonne
þæt þu hie ne meaht gehælan.
 1.15.7. Wið þon ilcan genim wudurofan & wudu merce &
hofan & wel on buteran & seoh þurh hæwenne clað, do on þæt
heafod.
 1.15.9. Þonne gangaþ þa ban ut.
 1.16.1. Wiþ langum sare þæs heafdes oþþe ðara earena
oððe þara toþa þa þurh horh oððe þurh snofl ut ateo þæt
þær egleþ, geseoþ cerfillan on wætere, sele drincan.
 1.16.3. Þonne atihð þæt þa yfelan wætan ut oþþe
þurh muð oððe þurh nosu.
 1.16.4. Eft þus þu scealt þa yfelan ofsetenan wætan utadon
þurh spatl & hræcean, meng pipor wiþ hwit cwudu, sele to ceowanne
& wyrc him to swillanne þone geagl, genim eced & wæter & senep
& hunig, wyl togædere listum & aseoh, ðonne læt colian, sele
þonne gelome þæt geagl to swillanne þæt he þy sel mæge
þæt yfel utahræcean.
 1.17.1. Wyrc þus swilinge to heafdes clænsunge, genim eft
senepes sædes dæl & næpsædes & cersan sædes, sume men
hatað lambes cersan, & merces sæd & <foreign>XX</foreign> piporcorna, gesamna eall
mid ecede & mid hunige, gehæt on wætere & habbe on muþe lange.
 1.17.4. Þonne yrnð þæt gillister ut.
 1.17.4. Eft oþru swiling on sumere, cærenes godne bollan fulne
& ecedes medmicelne & ysopum hatte wyrt hire leaf & blostman meng
togædere & læt standan neahterne & on morgen on croccan oferwylle
& supe wlæc & þæt geagl swile & þwea his muð.
 1.17.8. To þon ilcan on wintra senepes dustes cucler fulne &
huniges healfne cucler gedo on calic menge, þonne æfter þon wið
wæter & hæte & seoh þurh linenne clað & swile mið
þæt geagl.
 1.17.10. Æfter þam læcedome gelome mid ele swille þa
hracan.
 1.17.11. Eft wiþ þon ilcan genim mealwan, gegnid on wlæc
win, sele to swillanne þæt geagl.
 1.17.12. Wið tobrocenum heafde & sarum, rude getrifeladu mid
sealte & mid hunige, smire þæt heafod foreweard mid þy.
 1.17.14. Se cuþesta læcedom biþ þam þe heafod wylm &
sar þrowiað.
 1.17.15. Wiþ þon ilcan eft gegnid rudan on win, sele drincan
& gemeng eced wiþ rudan & ele, drype on þæt heafod & smire
mid.
 2.1.1. Læcedomas wiþ eagna miste, genim celeþenian seaw
oþþe blostman, gemeng wið dorena hunig, gedo on æren fæt, wlece
listum on wearmum gledum oþþæt hit gesoden sie.
 2.1.3. Þis bið god læcedom wiþ eagna dimnesse.
 2.1.4. Wiþ þon ilcan eft wildre rudan gedeawre &
getrifuladre seaw gemeng wið aseownes huniges em micel, smyre mid þa
eagan.
 2.1.5. Wiþ eagna miste monige men þy læs hiora eagan þa
adle þrowian lociað on ceald wæter & þonne magon fyr geseon, ne
wyrt þæt þa seon.
 2.1.7. Ac micel win gedrinc & oþre geswette drincan &
mettas & þa swiþost þa ðe on ðære uferan wambe gewuniað
& ne magon meltan ac þær yfele wætan wyrceað & þicce, por
& cawel & eal þa þe syn swa afer sind to fleoganne, & þæt
þe mon on bedde dæges upweard ne licge.
 2.1.11. & cyle & wind & rec & dust þas þing
& þisum gelic ælce dæge sceþþað þam eagum.
 2.1.12. Wiþ eagna miste genim grenne finul, gedo on wæter
<foreign>XXX</foreign> nihta on ænne croccan þone þe sie gepicod utan, gefylle þonne
mid ren wætere.
 2.1.14. Æfter þon aweorpe of þone finul & mid þy
wætere ælce dæge þweah þa eagan & ontyne.
 2.1.15. Eft of homena æþme & stieme & of wlætan
cymð eagna mist & sio scearpnes & sogoþa þæt deþ wiþ þon
is þis to donne.
 2.1.17. Wið eagna miste genim cileþonian seawes cucler fulne
oþerne finoles þriddan aprotanan seawes & huniges teares tu cucler
mæl, meng togædere & þonne mid feþere gedo in þa eagan on
morgenne & þonne middæg sie & eft on æfen æfter þon
þonne þæt adrugod sie & togoten.
 2.1.20. For þære sealfe scearpnesse genim wifes meoluc
þæs þe cild hæbbe, do on þa eagan.
 2.2.1. Eft æþele cræft, genim balsami & huniges teares
em micel gemeng togædere & smire mid þy.
 2.3.1. Eft wið þon ilcan celeþonian seaw & sæwæter,
smire mid þa eagan & beðe.
 2.3.2. Biþ þonne selest þæt þu nime þære
celeþonian seaw & mucgwyrte & rudan ealra em fela, do hunig to &
baldsamum gif þu hæbbe, gedo on þæt fæt þe þu hit mæge on
mid gefoge geseoþan & nytta.
 2.3.4. Wel þæt bet.
 2.4.1. Wiþ eagna miste gebærned sealt & gegniden &
wiþ dorena hunig gemenged, smire mid.
 2.5.1. Eft finoles & rosan & rudan seaw & doran hunig
& ticcenes geallan togædere gemenged, smire mid þa eagan.
 2.5.2. Eft grene cellendre gegniden & wiþ wifes meoluc
gemenged alege ofer þa eagan.
 2.6.1. Eft haran geallan genime & smire mid.
 2.7.1. Eft cwice wine winclan gebærnde to ahsan & þa ahsan
gemenge wið dorena hunig.
 2.8.1. Eft ryslas ealra ea fisca on sunnan gemylte & wið
hunig gemengde, smire mid.
 2.9.1. Wið eagna miste eft betonican seaw gebeatenre mid hire
wyrttruman & awrungenre & gearwan seaw & celeþonian em micel
ealra, meng togædere, do on eage.
 2.9.3. Eft finoles wyrttruman gecnuadne gemeng wið huniges seaw,
seoð þonne æt leohtum fyre listelice oþ huniges þicnesse gedo
þonne on ærene ampullan & þonne þearf sie smire mid.
 2.9.5. Þis todrifþ þa eahmistas þeah þe hie þicce
synd.
 2.10.1. Wiþ eagna miste eft celeþonian seaw oþþe þara
blostmena gewring & gemeng wið dorena hunig, gedo on æren fæt,
wlece þonne listum on wearmum gledum oþþe on ahsan oþ þæt hit
gedon sie.
 2.10.3. Þæt bið anspilde lyb wiþ eagena dimnesse.
 2.11.1. Sume þæs seawes anlipiges nyttiað & þa eagan
mid þy smiriað.
 2.11.1. Wiþ eagena miste eft eorðifies seaw & finoles seaw,
gedo begea em fela on ampullan, drige þonne on hatre sunnan & þa eagan
inneweard mid þy smire.
 2.11.4. Wiþ eagena miste eft eorðgeallan seaw þæt is
hyrdewyrt smire on þa eagan.
 2.11.5. Sio syn biþ þy scearpre.
 2.11.5. Gif þu hunig to dest þæt deah.
 2.11.5. Genim þonne þære ilcan wyrte godne gelm, gedo on
ceac fulne wines & geseoþ ofnete ær þry dagas & þonne hio
gesoden sie, awring þa wyrt of & þæs woses geswettes mid hunige
gedrinc ælce dæge neaht nestig bollan fulne.
 2.12.1. Ealdes mannes eagan beoþ unscearpsyno.
 2.12.1. Þonne sceal he þa eagan weccan mid gnidingum, mid
gongum, mid radum oþþe mid þy þe hine mon bere oþþe on wæne
ferige.
 2.12.3. & hy sculan nyttian lytlum & forhtlicum metum &
hiora heafod cemban & wermod drincan ær þon þe hie mete þicgean.
 2.12.4. Þus mon sceal unscearpsynum sealfe wyrcean to eagum,
genim pipor & gebeat & swegles æppel & hwon sealt & win.
 2.12.6. Þæt biþ god sealf.
 2.13.1. Wiþ miclum eagece, manig man hæfþ micelne ece on his
eagum, wyrc him þonne grunde swelgean & bisceop wyrt & finol, wyl
þa wyrta ealle on wætre, meoluc bið selre, læt þæt reocan on
þa eagan.
 2.13.3. Eft celeþonian & wudubindels leaf geaces sure wið
win gemenge.
 2.14.1. Eft to miclum eagece cropleac nioþoweard &
witmæres wyrt nioþoweard cnua on wine.
 2.14.2. Læt standan twa niht.
 2.14.2. Wið flie eagsealf genim, bromes ahsan & bollan fulne
hates wines, geot þriwa lytlum on hate þa ahsan & do þonne on æren
fæt oððe cyperen, do huniges hwon to & meng togædere, do on
þæs untruman mannes eagan & aþweah eft þa eagan on clænum
wylle.
 2.14.6. Wiþ flie haran geallan do wearmne on ymb twa niht flihð
of þam eagum.
 2.14.7. Wiþ flie genim onwære slah, þæt seaw & wring
þurh clað on þæt eage, sona gæð on þrim dagum of gif sio slah
biþ grene.
 2.14.8. Wiþ flie eced & gebærned sealt & beren mela,
gemeng togædere, do on þæt eage, hafa lange hwile þine hand on.
 2.15.1. Wiþ flie eahsealf, celeþonian sæd genim on þam
wyrttruman, gnid on eald win & on hunig, do pipor, to læt standan
neahterne be fyre, nytta þonne þu slapan wille.
 2.15.3. Wiþ flie oxan slyppan niþewearde & alor rinde wylle
on buteran.
 2.16.1. Wiþ þon ðe eagan tyren rudan seaw & gate geallan
& doran hunig ealra em fela.
 2.16.2. Gif eagan tyren, heorotes hornes ahsan do on geswet win.
 2.16.3. Wyrc eagsealfe wiþ wænne, genim cropleac & garleac
begea em fela, gecnuwa wel tosomne, genim win & fearres geallan begea em
fela, gemeng wiþ þy leace, do þonne on arfæt, læt standan nigon
niht on þam arfate, awring þurh claþ & gehlyttre wel, do on horn
& ymb niht do mid feþere on þæt eage, se betsta læcedom.
 2.17.1. Wiþ wenne on eagon genim þa holan cersan, gebræd, do
on þæt eage swa he hatost mæge.
 2.18.1. Wiþ eagece gewyrce him grundswelgean & bisceop wyrt
& beowyrt & finul, wyl þa wyrta ealle on wætere, meoluc biþ
betere.
 2.19.1. Wiþ eagna ece genim þa readan hofan, awyl on surum
swatum oþþe on surum ealað & beþe þa eagan on þam baþe,
betere swa oftor.
 2.20.1. Wiþ eagece genim wiþowindan twigu, gecnuwa, awylle on
buteran, do on þa eagan.
 2.21.1. Wyrc eagsealfe, genim hnutcyrnla & hwæte corn, gnid
togædere, do win to aseoh þurh clað, do þonne on þa eagan.
 2.21.2. Wiþ eagna wærce & ece hwites hlafes cruman &
pipor & eced meng wel, lege on clað, bind on þa eagan nihterne.
 2.21.4. Þus mon sceal eagsealfe wyrcean, genim streawberian wisan
nioþowearde & pipor, gecnuwa wel, do on claþ, bebind fæste, lege on
geswet win, læt gedreopan on þa eagan ænne dropan.
 2.21.6. Wyrc eagsealfe, wudubindes leaf, wudumerce, streawberian
wisan, suþerne wermod, oxna lyb, celeþonian, gecnuwa þa wyrte swiðe,
meng wiþ win, do on cyperen fæt oþþe on ærenum fate hafa, læt
standan seofon niht oþþe ma, awringe þa wyrta swiðe clæne, gedo
pipor on & geswet swiþe leohtlice mid hunige, do siþþan on horn &
mid feþere do on þa eagan ænne dropan.
 2.21.11. Wyrt eagsealfe drige genim swegles æppel & swefl,
crecisc attrum, & gebærned sealt & pipores mæst, gegrind eall to
duste, asift þurh clað, do on næsc, hæbbe him on þy læs hit
þine, do medmicel on þa eagan mid toþ gare.
 2.21.14. Gereste him æfter & slape & þonne aþweah
his eagan mid clæne wætre & on þæt wæter locige.
 2.21.16. Wyrc eagsealfe, cymen & streawbergean wise gecnuwa
swiðe wel & of geot mid geswette wine, do in cyperen fæt oððe on
æren, læt standan fela nihta on, awring þa wyrte þurh clað &
ahluttra swiþe wel, do þonne on þa eagan þonne þu wille restan.
 2.21.19. Gif sio sealf sie to hear geswet mið hunige.
 2.21.20. Wið æsmælum genim attrum, gemeng wið spatl, þa
eagan uteweard nalæs innan.
 2.22.1. Wið æsmælum niþeweard æscþrotu gecowen on
muþe & awringen þurh clað on eage gedon wundorlice hælþ.
 2.22.2. Wiþ þon þe mon surege sie genim agrimonian, welle
swiþe oþ þriddan dæl, þweah gelome þa eagan mid þy.
 2.22.4. Wiþ pocce on eagum genim wad & ribban &
hleomocan, wyl on meolce, on buteran is betere, & wyrc beþinge, wyl
hleomoc & gearwan & wudu cearfillan on meolcum.
 2.23.1. Wiþ wyrmum on eagum genim beolonan sæd, scead on
gleda, do twa bleda fulle wæteres to, sete on twa healfe & site þær
ofer, bræd þonne þæt heafod hider & geond ofer þæt fyr &
þa bleda eac, þonne sceadaþ þa wyrmas on þæt wæter.
 2.23.4. Wiþ þeoradle on eagum, þe mon gefigo hæt, on
læden hatte cimosis, hænne æges geolocan & merces sæd &
attrum & tunmintan.
 2.23.6. Eft wið gefigon sceapes hohscancan unsodenne tobrec, gedo
þæt mearh on þa eagan.
 2.23.7. Wiþ þiccum bræwum genim þreo hand fulla mucwyrte,
þreo sealtes, þreo wapan, wylle þonne oþ þæt sie twæde bewylled
þæs woses, heald þonne on cyperenum fate.
 2.23.9. Þam men þe habbað þicce bræwas genim cyperen
fæt, do þæron lybcorn & sealt gemeng, genim celeþonian &
bisceopwyrt & geaces suran & attorlaþan & springwyrt &
englisce moran & hwon rædices & hrefnes fot, awæsc þonne ealle,
geot þonne win on læt standan, aseoh eft on þæt cyperene fæt,
læt þonne standan fiftyne niht & þa derstan beoþ gode.
 2.23.14. Hafa þe clæne fletan, do on þæt fæt þe þa
derstan on syn swa fela swa þara flietna þær on clifian mæge, screp
þonne of þam fæte.
 2.23.15. Þæt biþ swiðe god sealf þam men þe hæfð
þicce bræwas.
 3.1.1. Læcedomas wið eallum earena sare & ece & wið
earena adeafunge & gif wyrmas on earan synd oþþe earwicga & gif
earan dynien & earsealfa, fiftyne cræftas.
 3.2.1. Wiþ earena sare & ece betonican niwan geworhte þa
leaf self gecnuwa on wearmum wætere, do hwon gerosodes eles to, genim
þæt swa wlacu mid þicre wulle, drype on þæt eare.
 3.2.3. Eft wiþ þon ilcan genim ciepan, geseoþ on ele, drype
on þæt eare þone ele.
 3.2.4. Wiþ earwærce & wið deafe hundes tunge &
fenminte & cellendre gecnuwa on win oþþe on eala, aseoh, do on eare.
 3.2.6. Wiþ þon ilcan genim hænne rysele, gemylte &
þonne gedo wlaco on eare, gedrype on.
 3.2.7. Wiþ þon ilcan genim ele, genim eac gose rysele, geot
on.
 3.2.8. Þonne gewit þæt sar aweg.
 3.3.1. Wiþ þon ilcan genim beolonan seaw, gewlece & þonne
on eare gedryp.
 3.3.2. Þonne þæt sar gestilð.
 3.4.1. Wiþ þon ilcan genim garleac & cipan & gose
rysele, gemylte togædere, wring on eare.
 3.5.1. Wiþ þon ilcan genim æmetan ægru, getrifula, wring
on eare.
 3.5.1. Wið earena sare genim gate geallan, drype on þæt
eare, meng wið cu meoluc gif þu wille.
 3.5.3. Wið earena deafe genim hryþeres geallan wiþ gæten
hland gemenged, gedrype gewleced on þæt eare.
 3.6.1. Wiþ þon ilcan gif earan willen adeafian oþþe yfel
hlyst sie genim eofores geallan, fearres geallan, buccan geallan, gemeng wiþ
hunig ealra em fela, drype on þæt eare.
 3.7.1. Wiþ þon ilcan gif yfelne hlyst hæbbe ifies seaw
þæs þe be eorþan flihð þæt clænoste seaw gemeng wið win,
drype on eare.
 3.8.1. Eft ribban seaw & gewlecedne ele togædere gemenged
drype on, wundorlice hælð.
 3.8.2. Wiþ þon ilcan genim rammes geallan mid his selfes
nihtnestiges migoþan, gemenge wið buteran, geot on eare.
 3.8.3. Eft wiþ þon ilcan hnutbeames rinde seaw gewleced drype
on eare.
 3.9.1. Wiþ ðon ilcan genim celendran seaw grenre meng wiþ
wifes meoluc & huniges dropan & wines gewleht tosamne.
 3.9.2. Wiþ earena adeafunge eft ellencroppan getrifulad, þæt
seaw wring on þæt eare.
 3.9.3. Eft wiþ þon ilcan genim eofores geallan & fearres
& buccan, meng wiþ hunig oþþe on ele, wring on eare.
 3.10.1. Eft wið þon ilcan genim grenne æscenne stæf, lege
on fyr, genim þonne þæt seaw þe him of gæþ, do on þa ilcan
wulle, wring on eare & mid þære ilcan wulle forstoppa þæt eare.
 3.11.1. Wiþ þæt ilce eft genim æmetan hors & cropleac
& neoþowearde ellenrinde oþþe beolonan & ele, gecnuwa tosomne,
wyrme on scille, do þonne on eare þara readena æmetena hors, genim
þonne rædic & eced, cnuwa tosomne, wring on þæt eare.
 3.11.4. Gif wyrmas on earan syn genim eorð geallan grenes seaw
oþþe hunan seaw oþþe wermodes seaw swilc þara an swa þu wille, geot
þæt seaw on þæt eare.
 3.11.6. Þæt tihð þone wyrm ut.
 3.11.6. Wyrc sealfe, gecnuwa sinfullan & leoþowyrt & por,
gedo þonne on glæs fæt mid ecede & þurh clað awring, drype on
þæt eare.
 3.11.8. Wiþ þon gif earan dynien genim ele, do on mid eowocigre
wulle & fordytte þæt eare mid þære wulle þonne þu slapan
wille & do eft of þonne þu onwæcne.
 3.12.1. Eft wiþ þon ilcan wermod gesodenne on wætere on
niwum cytele, do of heorðe, læt reccan þone steam on þæt eare &
fordytte mid þære wyrte siþþan hit ingegan sie.
 3.12.3. Wiþ earwicgan genim þæt micle greate windel streaw
twyecge þæt on worþium wixð, ceow on þæt eare.
 3.12.4. He bið of sona.
 4.1.1. Læcedomas wið healsgunde & þæs tacn,
hwæþer he hit sie, & eac wið gealhswile & þrotan &
wasende, wiþ sweorcoþe, <foreign>XIIII</foreign> cræftas.
 4.2.1. Wiþ healsgunde, þonne ærest onginne se healsgund
wesan smire hine sona mid hryþeres oþþe swiðost mid oxan geallan,
þæt is acunnod.
 4.2.3. Ymb feawa niht bið hal.
 4.2.3. Gif þu wolde witan hwæþer þæt heals gund sie
genim angeltwæccean gehalne lege on þa stowe þær hit aþruten sie
& bewreoh fæste ufan mid leafum.
 4.2.5. Gif hit healsgund bið se wyrm wyrð to eorþan, gif hit
ne biþ he biþ gehal.
 4.2.6. Eft wiþ heals gunde, genim celender & beana
togædere gesodene & alege on.
 4.2.7. Sona tofereþ.
 4.2.7. Eft læcedom wiþ þon ilcan, genim wæterhæfern
gebærnedne & þonne gegniden smale & wiþ hunig gemenged & on
gedon.
 4.2.9. Sona bið sel.
 4.2.9. Wiþ þon ilcan eft, galbanum hatte suþerne wyrt, lege
þa on þone sweorwærc.
 4.2.10. Þonne atihð hio mid ealle þa yfelan wætan ut &
þone gund.
 4.3.1. Wiþ þon ilcan eft, beren melo & hluttor pic &
weax & ele meng tosomne, seoþ, do cnihtes oþþe cildes migeþan to,
to onlegene do on þone gund.
 4.3.3. Wið heals gunde eft, þære readan netelan wyrttruman
gesodenne on ecede & gebeatenne & on weaxhlafes wisan on aled.
 4.3.4. Gif se gund biþ þonne onginnende sio sealf hine
todrifþ, gif he biþ eald hio hine ontynð.
 4.3.5. & swa astihð þæt yfel ut oþ þæt he hal
bið.
 4.4.1. Eft wiþ þon, manigfeald tacn & læcedom wið
healsgunde oþþe geaglswile oððe þrotan oþþe wasende, sio adl is
twegea cynna.
 4.4.2. Oþer is on þam geagle & þonne mon þone muþ
ontynð biþ gehwæþer geswollen & biþ read ymb þa hræctunga
& ne mæg se man eþelice eþian ac biþ asmorod, ne mæg eac naht
forswelgan ne wel sprecan ne stemne næfþ.
 4.4.5. Ne bið þeos adl hwæþere to frecne.
 4.4.6. Oþer is þonne on þære þrotan biþ swyle &
lyssen, se ne mæg naht gecweþan & bið se swile ge on þam sweoran
ge on þære tungan, ne mæg se man wel eþian ne þone sweoran on
cerran ne his heafod forð on hyldan þæt he his nafolan geseon mæge.
 4.4.9. & butan his man raþor tilige he biþ ymb þreo niht
gefaren.
 4.4.10. Gif sie þære adle bryne innan þæs strang þæt
mon ne mæge utan geseon sio biþ ðy frecenre.
 4.4.11. Gif þonne sie on gehwæþere healfe þa ceacan
aswollen & sio þrotu & þu þa tacn geseo þonne sona læt þu
him blod on ædre.
 4.4.13. Gif þu þæt þurhteon ne mæge scearpa him þa
scancan.
 4.4.14. Þæt him deah.
 4.5.1. Sele him scearpne wyrtdrenc, wyrne him metes.
 4.5.1. Æfter þon bewind þone sweoran & lege on
læcedomas þa þe utteon þa yfelan wætan & þæt sar.
 4.5.3. Þonne biþ þær wyrpe wen.
 4.5.3. Wyrc him þa sealfe, genim swines rysle, gesmyre ane brade
pannan innewearde mid þam rysele, wyl, þonne weorp gose scearn to on þa
pannan & gewlece & þonne hit sy gemylt do þonne on linenne clað,
lege on þæt sar & besweþe do, þæt wel oft on on dæg.
 4.5.6. & biþ swa betere swa þu oftor edniwast þa sealfe
& oftor onlegst.
 4.5.7. Sio tihð þæt yfel ut.
 4.6.1. Wiþ healsgunde genim weax & ele, gemeng wiþ rosan
blostman & gemelt togædere, do þær on.
 4.6.2. Wiþ sweorcoþe wyrc on lecgende sealfe, genim fearres
gelyndo & beran smeru & weax, ealra em fela, wyrc to sealfe, smire
mid.
 4.6.4. Eft wiþ þon ilcan, gif þu finde hwitne hundes þost,
adrige þone & gegnid & asyft & geheald þæt wiþ þære
sweorcoþe & þonne þearf sie meng wiþ hunig, smire þone sweoran
mid.
 4.6.6. Þæt biþ strang sealf & god wið swelcre
ablawunge & bruneþan & wiþ þara ceacna geswelle oððe
asmorunge.
 4.6.8. Sceal þeah se hund ban gnagan ær, þy biþ se þost
hwit & micel.
 4.6.8. Gif þu hine nimest & gaderast æt fylne þonne ne
biþ he to unswete to gestincanne.
 4.6.10. Þonne sceal mon þone geagl eac swillan gelome on
þære adle & swolgettan eced wiþ sealt gemenged.
 4.6.11. Eft fifleafan seawes þry bollan fulle lytle sceal
forcuuolstan.
 4.6.12. Wiþ sweorcoðe eft, garleac gegniden on eced þæt
þe sie wiþ wæter gemenged, swille þone geagl mid þy.
 4.6.13. Wiþ sweorcoþe eft, riges sceofoþa seoþ on geswettum
wætere, swille þa ceolan mid þy.
 4.6.14. Gif se sweora sar sie syn eac þa swillinga hwilum hate.
 4.6.15. Þonne is eac to þisse adle geset þæt mon under
þære tungan læte blod oþþe of earme & on morgen on sprenge.
 4.6.17. Gif hit þonne cniht sie læt on þam sweoran.
 4.6.17. & on þære adle is to forwyrnanne wines &
flæsces swiþost þy læs sio ceole sie aswollen.
 5.1.1. Wiþ þon gif mannes muð sar sie genim betonican &
getrifula, lege on þa weolore.
 5.1.2. To muðsealfe & to geblegenadre tungan, fifleafe &
brembelleaf wyl on wætere, hafa lange on muðe & gelome.
 5.1.3. Gif monnes orað sie ful genim beren mela god &
clæne hunig & hwit sealt, gemeng eall tosomne & gnid þa teþ mid
swiðe & gelome.
 6.1.1. Læcedomas wiþ toð wærce & wiþ wyrmum, ge
wiþ þam uferan toðece ge wiþ þam niþeran.
 6.2.1. Wiþ toþ wærce betonican seoð on wine oþ þriddan
dæl, swile þonne geond þone muð lange hwile.
 6.3.1. Wið toþ wærce, gif wyrm ete genim eald holen leaf
& heorot crop neoþeweardne & saluian ufewearde, bewyl twy dæl on
wætre, geot on bollan & geona ymb.
 6.3.3. Þonne feallað þa wyrmas on þone bollan.
 6.3.3. Gif wyrm ete þa teð genim ofer geare holen rinde &
eofor þrotan moran, wel on swa hatum, hafa on muþe swa hat swa þu hatost
mæge.
 6.3.5. Wiþ toðwyrmum genim acmela & beolonan sæd &
weax, ealra em fela, meng tosomne, wyrc to weax candelle & bærn, læt
reocan on þone muð.
 6.3.7. Do blæc hrægl under, þonne feallaþ þa wyrmas
on.
 6.4.1. Wið toþ wærce gebærn hwit sealt & garleac,
berec on gledum, gebræd & berend & pipor & strælwyrt, gegnid
eal tosomne, lege on.
 6.5.1. Wiþ toþ wærce, hrefnes fot wel on wine neoþoweardne
oððe on ecede, sup swa ðu hatost mæge.
 6.5.2. Wiþ toðwærce hnutbeames rinde & þorn rinde
gecnua to duste, adrig on pannan, snið utan þa teþ, scead on gelome.
 6.6.1. Wyrc þus toþsealfe, ofersæwisc rind & hunig &
pipor meng tosomne, lege on.
 6.6.2. Wyrc eac sealfe of wenwyrte on þa ilcan wisan.
 6.7.1. Wiþ þam uferan toþece genim wiþowindan leaf, awring
on þa nosu.
 6.7.2. Wiþ þam niþeran toþece slit mid þe foþorne oþ
þæt hie bleden.
 6.8.1. Eft genim elmes rinde, gebærn to ahsan, gemeng þa ahsan
wiþ wæter & aseoh, hafa þæt wæter lange on muþe.
 6.8.2. Eft genim gearwan, ceow swiþe.
 7.1.1. Gif mon blode hræce genim betonican swilce swa <foreign>III</foreign>
penegas gewegen, gegnid on gæte meolc, sele þry dagas þry bollan fulle
to drincanne.
 8.1.1. Wiþ blæce on andwlitan wyl to bæþe fencersan &
neoþoweardne secg, æscrinde, earfan, wyl on wætere lange, beþe mid.
 8.2.1. To sealfe wiþ blæce on andwlitan, ompran neoþowearde
þa þe swimme, do sealt to & flietan & æg.
 8.2.2. Briw wiþ blæce on andwlitan, gemelte eald spic, briw on
þon, do gegrundenne pipor on & cropleac, hwætenes melwes twy dæl
swilce þæs pipores, awyl hræt hwega, genim þæs þreo snæda,
gerest æfter wearme.
 8.2.5. Wið blæce genim heorotes horn, gebærn to ahsan &
swefl & gebærned sealt & pic to ahsan & swa oster scella &
gecnuwa ompran smale & gemeng eall to briwe & smire mid.
 8.2.7. Eft sealf, wel on aþydum sceapes smeruwe hægþornes
blostman & þa smalan singrenan & wudurofan, meng þonne hwitcwudu
wiþ & hwon buteran.
 9.1.1. Gif men yrne blod of nebbe to swiðe genim grene betonican
& rudan, gecnuwa on eced.
 9.1.2. Gewring tosomne swilce sie an slah, sting on þa nosu.
 9.1.3. Blod seten, bisceop wyrt nioþowearde ete oððe on
meolce drince.
 9.1.3. Blod seten eft, genim hegeclifan, gebinde on sweoran.
 9.2.1. Blod seten eft, spring wyrt do on eare.
 9.3.1. Blod seten eft, wegbrædan do on eare.
 9.4.1. Blod seten eft, gehal beren ear bestinge on eare swa he
nyte.
 9.4.2. Sume þis writað, ge horse ge men blod seten.
 10.1.1. Wiþ gesnote & geposum genim oxna lyb niþeweard,
gecnuwa wel wið wætre, gif hio sie grene ne do þu þær wæter to,
wring þonne on þæt neb.
 11.1.1. Wiþ sarum weolorum gesmire mid hunige þa weoloras,
genim þonne ægerfelman, bescead mid pipore, lege on.
 12.1.1. Wiþ wouum muþe genim ompran & ealdne swines rysle,
wyrc to sealfe, sete on þone won dæl.
 12.1.2. Wiþ ceolan swile wiþ þon, sceal eoforfearn eac swa
& gyþrifan wyl on meolce, sup þonne & gebeþe mid.
 12.1.3. Wiþ ceolan swile bisceop wyrt, aterlaðe niðewearde
& clatan, wyl on ealað.
 13.1.1. Wið hær scearde, hwit cwudu gecnuwa swiðe smale, do
æges þæt hwite to & meng swa þu dest teafor, onsnið mid seaxse
seowa mid seolce fæste smire mid þonne mid þære sealfe utan &
innan ær se seoloc rotige gif tosomne teo rece mid handa smire eft sona.
 14.1.1. Wiþ seaðan, recels lytel, swefl, swegles æppel,
weax, gingifer, þurh horn drince hunan, hafocwyrt on hluttrum ealoð.
 15.1.1. Wiþ hwostan, hu he missenlice on mon becume & hu his
mon tilian scyle.
 15.1.2. Se hwosta hæfð manigfealdne tocyme swa þa spatl
beoð missenlicu, hwilum cymð of ungemetfæstre hæto, hwilum of
ungemetfæstum cyle, hwilum of ungemetlicre drignesse.
 15.2.1. Wyrc drenc wiþ hwostan, genim mucgwyrt, seoþ on
cyperenum citele & wyl oþ þæt hio sie swiþe þicce & hio sie
of hwætenum mealte geworht, genim þonne eoforfearnes mæst, bisceopwyrt,
hind heoloðan, dweorgedwostlan, singrenan, do to eall on fæt, sele drincan
middeldagum & forga sur & sealtes gehwæt.
 15.2.5. Wiþ hwostan eft genim hunan, seoð on wætere, sele
swa wearme drincan.
 15.3.1. Eft genim clifwyrt, sume men hatað foxes clife, sume
eawyrt & hio sy geworht ofer midne sumor, seoþ þa on wætere oþ
þæt driddan dæl þæs woses of sie, sele drincan þriwa on dæg.
 15.4.1. Wið hwostan eft genim sæmintan, wyl on ealaþ, sele
drincan.
 15.4.2. Eft genim spracen berindred, wyl on ealað, sele drincan.
 15.5.1. Eft genim hofan, gearwan, reade netelan, wyl on meolce.
 15.5.1. Eft genim wiþ hwostan & wiþ angbreoste slarian
godne dæl, do bollan fulne wines to, bewyl þriddan dæl on þa wyrte,
supe on niht nestig.
 15.6.1. Est genim marubian, wyl on ealað, do pipor on.
 15.6.1. Eft wiþ angbreoste, gif men sie drige hwosta genim spices
snæde þynne, lege on hatne stan, scead cymed on, sete horn on, drince
þonne smic.
 15.7.1. Wiþ drigum hwostan eft genim eolonan & galluc, ete on
huniges teare.
 16.1.1. Wiþ breost wærce genim þa lytlan culmillan &
cymed, wyl on hluttrum ealaþ, supe & drince.
 16.1.2. Eft genim dweorgedwostlan & gyþrifan, kyncean, welle
on hluttrum ealað, drince scenc fulne on neaht nestig.
 16.2.1. Wyl on ealað wiþ þon ilcan, finul, marubian,
betonican, & drince.
 16.2.2. Wiþ breost wærce genim rudan, hunan & aprotanan,
gegnid tosomne smæle on mortere, meng wið hunig & þry dagas ælce
dæg ær mete þrie cucler fulle geþicge.
 17.1.1. Wiþ heort wærce, rudan gelm seoþ on ele & do
alwan ane yntsan to, smire mid þy.
 17.1.2. Þæt stilð þam sare.
 17.1.2. Wiþ heort ece gif him on innan heard heort wærc sie
þonne him wyxþ wind on þære heortan & hine þegeð þurst &
biþ unmehtiglic.
 17.2.1. Wyrc him þonne stan bæð & on þam ete suþerne
rædic mid sealte þy mæg wesan sio wund gehæled.
 17.2.2. Wiþ heorot ece eft genim giþrifan, seoþ on meolce,
sele drincan <foreign>VI</foreign> dagas.
 17.3.1. Eft nioþeweard eforfearn, geþrifan, wegbrædan wyl
tosomne, sele drincan.
 17.3.2. Wið hiorot ece eft genim pipor & cymen & cost,
gegnid on beor oþþe on wætre, sele drincan.
 18.1.1. Hwonan se micla geoxa cume oþþe hu his mon tilian
scule, se cymð of þam swiðe acolodan magan oþþe of þam to swiðe
ahatodan oððe of to micelre fylle oþþe of to micelre lærnesse
oððe of yfelum wætan slitendum & sceorfendum þone magan.
 18.1.4. Gif þonne se seoca man þurh spiwedrenc aspiwð þone
yfelan bitendan wætan on weg þonne forstent se geohsa.
 18.1.5. Spiwe þa deah þam monnum þe for fylle gihsa, slihð
oððe forþon þe hie innan scyrfð.
 18.1.7. & eac se geohsa se þe of þæs yfelan wætan
micelnysse cymð hæfð þearfe spiwdrinces se wyrcð micelne fnoran eac
& se hine bet.
 18.1.8. Þonne se geohsa of þære idlan wambe cymð & of
þære gelæran ne bet þone se fnora.
 18.1.10. Gif se geohsa of cile cume þonne sceal mon mid wyrmendum
þingum lacnian swile swa pipor is & oþra wermenda wyrta oþþe rudan
gegnide mon, owin selle drincan oþþe merces sæd mid wine oþþe eced
selle drincan oððe mintan broð oþþe moran oððe cymenes oþþe
gingifran, hwilum anlepig swa gerenode, hwilum þa wyrta togædere gedon on
þæt wos selle drincan.
 18.1.14. Gif of hatum wætan yfelum on þone magon gesamnodum se
geohsa cume & he gefele þæt se hine innan sceorfe on þone magan sele
him þonne wlacu wæter drincan swiþe hat, gedo þonne feþere on ele,
stinge him gelome on þa hracan þæt he mage spiwan, sele him wiþ
geohsan ceald wæter & eced drincan & aprotanan gegnidene on wine.
 19.1.1. Wiþ wlættan, þam men þe hine ne lyst his metes ne
liþes oððe on magan untrum sie oþþe bitere hræce, eorðgeallan
& pipor drince on wearmum wætere þry bollan fulle on niht nestig.
 19.1.3. Eft wiþ wlatunge, rudan, wermod, bisceopwyrt, marubian,
wyl on ealað swiþe geswet mid hunige leohtlice, gedrinc swa hates swa þin
blod sie scenc fulne, do swa þonne þe þearf sie.
 20.1.1. Wiþ sculdor wærce, ealdes swines tord þæs þe
feldgangende sie meng wið ealdne rysele, gewyrme, lege on.
 20.1.2. Þæt deah wiþ sculdor wærce ge wið sid wærce,
wið breost wærce & wiþ lendenwærce.
 20.1.3. Eft wyl betonican & neftan on ealoð, sele drincan
gelome & simle æt fyre gesmire mid wenwyrte.
 20.1.5. Eft genim swines scearn þæs þe on dun lande &
wyrtum libbe, mæng wiþ ealdne rysele, lege on & drinc betonican on
geswettum wine.
 20.1.6. Gif fefer habbe drince on wætere.
 21.1.1. Wiþ sidan sare þære swiþran, bogen & redic
& hwite clæfran wyrc to clame & to drence.
 21.1.2. Wiþ þære winestran sidan sare, wudurifan gecnuwa on
eced & wyrc to clame, gebind on þa sidan.
 21.1.3. Eft betonican swilc swa þry penegas gewegen & pipores
seofon & <foreign>XX</foreign> corna tosomne getrifulad, geot ealdes wines þry bollan
fulle to & gewlece, sele nihtnestigum drincan.
 21.1.5. Eft wið sidan sare, rudan wið rysele gemenged &
gebeaten lecge on þa sidan, þæt bet.
 21.1.7. Wiþ sidan sare eft, laures croppan gebeate, drince on
wætere & on þa sidan binde.
 21.1.8. Wið sidan sare eft, caules wyrttruman gebærn to ahsan
& wiþ ealdne rysele gemeng & alege on þa sidan.
 22.1.1. Wiþ lenden ece genim betonican swilce twegen penegas
gewegen, do þærto swetes wines twegen bollan fulle, meng wiþ hat
wæter, sele nihtnestig drincan.
 22.1.3. Eft genim grundeswelgean, gebeat & þæt seaw sele
drincan nihtnestigum.
 22.2.1. Wiþ lenden ece, ealifer hatte wyrt, gnid on ealaþ &
drince þa.
 22.2.2. Wiþ þon ilcan, hundes tunge hatte, wyrt genim þa
leaf, adrig & gegnid to meluwe, genim þonne beren mela gemeng wiþ þa
wyrt & gebring þonne on meolce.
 23.1.1. Wiþ þeoh ece smice mid fearne swiþe þa þeoh.
 23.1.1. Eft to drence pipor, win wealwyrt, hunig.
 23.1.2. Eac to þon apuldor, þorn, æsc, cwicbeam,
eoforþrote, æscþrote, elone, bisceopwyrt, ifig, betonica, ribbe,
rædic, spracen, pipor, hwit cwudu, cost, gingifer, moniaca, netle, blinde
netle, wirc þis to drence.
 23.1.5. Gif þeoh slapan adelf nioþoweardne secg, wyl on
wætere, læt reocan on þæt lim þætte slape, smire mid sealfe
þe mon þus wyrce, of swines smerwe, sceapes smeru, butere, sciptearo,
pipor, hwit cwudu, swegles æppel, swefl, cost, eced, ele, hwerwette,
rædic, eolene, bisceopwyrt, sealt, æsc, apuldre, ac, þorn.
 24.1.1. Wiþ cneow wærce, wuduweaxe & hegerife gecnuwa þa
togædere & do on ealu, læt licgean neahterne, sele him þæt
þonne drincan, beþe mid & lege on.
 24.1.3. Wiþ þon gif cneow sar sie genim wealwyrt &
clufþung, reade netlan, awyl on wætere, beþe mid.
 25.1.1. Gif scancan sare synd genim giþrifan & dolgrunan
& hamor wyrt & betonican & banwyrt & linwyrt & wudu merce
& eorðgeallan & brunwyrt, seoþ on buteran, smire mid.
 25.2.1. Gif scancan synd forode nim banwyrt, gecnuwa, geot æges
þæt hwite, meng tosomne scancforedum men.
 25.2.2. Wið foredum lime lege þas sealfe on þæt forode lim
& forlege mid elmrinde, do spilc to, eft simle niwa oþþæt gehalod
sie.
 25.2.4. Gerendra elm rinde & awyl swiðe, do þonne of þa
rinde, genim linsæd, gegrind briwe wið þam elmes drænce.
 25.2.5. Þæt bið god sealf foredum lime.
 26.1.1. Gif sino gescrince & eft æfter þon swelle genim
gate tord gemeng wið eced smit on sona halað.
 26.1.2. Monegum men gescrincað his fet to his homme wyrc baþo
do earban to & cersan & smale netelan & beowyrt do on troh hate
stanas wel gehætte gebeþe þa hamma mid þam stan baðe þonne hie
sien geswate þonne recce he þa ban swa he swiþost mæge do spelc to
& betere swa mon oftor mid þy beþige.
 26.1.6. Gif sino clæppette mucgwyrt gebeatenu & wiþ ele
gemenged & on aled.
 26.1.7. Mycgwyrte seaw wiþ gerosodne ele gemenged smire mid þy
sona biþ ætstilled sio cwacung.
 27.1.1. Wiþ fot ece, betonican, geormenleaf, finul, ribban, ealra
emfela, gemenge meoluc wiþ wæter & þæt toswollene lim fram
þære uferran healfe beþe þy læs se swile ingewite.
 27.1.3. Genime þonne galluc gesodenne, lege on.
 27.1.4. Wið fota sare oþþe geswelle fram miclum gange,
wegbræde getrifulad & wið eced gemenged.
 27.1.5. Wiþ þon, deah grunde swelge gebeatenu & wið
rysele gemenged.
 27.2.1. Wiþ fotece, gif se fotace ingeswice genim mucgwyrte
wyrtruman, meng wiþ ele, sele etan.
 27.2.2. Wið fot ece eft, hunan seaw wiþ ele gemenged, smire
þa saran fet mid.
 27.3.1. Wiþ fotece genim ellenes leaf & wegbrædan &
mucgwyrt, gecnuwa, lege on & gebind on.
 28.1.1. Wiþ ban ece, tuningwyrt, beolone, wealwyrt, ealde grut
& eced, heorotes smera oþþe gate oþþe gose, meng tosomne, lege
þonne on.
 28.1.2. Wiþ banece eft to drence, elene, cneowholen, wealwyrt,
hune, clufþung, gecnuwa, do on wæter þæt ofer yrne, beþe to fyre
swiðe, þone ece þwea mid þy wætere, do þæt þriwa on dæg.
 28.1.5. Wyrc þonne sealfe of tuning wyrte, of eolonan, of
þunge, of wermode, do ealra emfela, wylle swiðe.
 29.1.1. Gif mannes getawa beoþ sare oððe aþundene,
betonican getrifula on wine, beþe þa saran stowa & þa aþundenan mid
þy.
 29.1.2. Eft gif hie dylstihte sien oððe geborstene genim
saluian, seoð on wætere, beþe mid þa getawa.
 29.2.1. Eft dile gebærned, gemeng wið ahsan hunig, wyrc to
sealfe, aþweah þonne & gebeþe þa wunda ærest mid hate wætere,
æfter þon mid wearme ele ge smire on þam þe wære wir gesoden, lege
þonne þa sealfe on.
 30.1.1. Þis sceal wiþ æcelman & wið þon þe men
acale þæt fel of þam fotum, genime neoþowearde medowyrt &
lustmocan & acrinde, gecnua eall to duste, gemeng wið hunig, lacna mid
þy.
 31.1.1. Wiþ ælcum heardum swile oððe geswelle adrige beana
& geseoþ butan sealte, meng þonne wið hunig, lege on.
 31.1.2. Wiþ þon ilcan genim beren melo, seoþ on ecede, do
on.
 31.1.3. Eft wiþ þon belenan meng wið rysele, lege on.
 31.1.3. Wið swile eft gebeat hunan, meng wiþ rysele, lege on
oððe gate horn gebærned & wiþ wæter gemenged.
 31.1.5. Eft rysele oþþe gelyndo wiþ garleac gemenged & on
aled þone swile þwænþ.
 31.2.1. Wiþ swile eft, cerfille gecnuwad mid rysele & on
gemelt weax gedon & on aled bet.
 31.3.1. Wið swile eft, gate flæsc gebærned to ahsan mid
wætere on gesmiten ealne þone swile tofereþ.
 31.3.2. Eft iuniperi þæt is gorst þæt sæd gecnuwa
& seoþ on wætere.
 31.3.3. Eft sinfulle wiþ rysele gemenged & wiþ hlaf &
wiþ celendran æt somne gemenged.
 31.3.4. Wiþ yflum wætan & swile genim heorotes sceafoþan
of þam horne oþþe þæs hornes melo, meng wiþ wæter, smit on
eal.
 31.3.6. Þæt worms & þone yfelan wætan aweg deþ
& adrifþ.
 31.4.1. Wiþ swile genim gate tyrdlu on scearpum ecede gesoden
& on selfe wisan on gedon.
 31.5.1. Wiþ ælcum yflum wætan, mucgwyrte þa grenan leaf
getrifulad & wiþ rysele gegniden togædere, smire an ge þeoh þær
dylstan on synd.
 31.5.2. Þæt deah wiþ þan.
 31.5.3. Ge þæt deah eac wiþ fota geswelle.
 31.5.3. Wiþ innan gewyrsmedum geswelle þam þe wyrð of fylle
oþþe of slege oððe of hricsca hwilcum, þa wyrt þe hatte fifleafe.
 31.5.5. Genim & gebeat & lege on gelome oþ þætte
open sie se swile, lacna þonne þa wunda swa oþre wunda.
 31.5.6. Wið swile eft, hluttor pic genim, do ahsan to, seoð
ætgædere, gelege þonne þone swile mid þy gelome.
 31.5.8. Wiþ swile eft, gate tyrdlu drige, gegnid & asifte
þurh smæl sife, do þonne rysle to swa swa syn twa pund & ealdes
wines swa micel swa þe þince, wyrc to sealfe.
 31.6.1. Eft gebærned sealt gegnid wel on gewleced wæter oþ
þæt hit sie swa þicce swa huniges tear, lege on þone swile, ofer lege
mid claðe & mid eowcigre wulle bind on.
 31.6.3. Wiþ færlicum sare & geswelle nim weax &
hemlic, getrifula, wyrc swa wearm to sealfe, bind on þæt sar.
 31.7.1. Wiþ fær swile nim hunan, gebeat & gemeng wiþ
rysele, lege on.
 31.7.1. Eft mare twynihte, grut mealtes, smedma, cersan, æges
þæt hwite, bisceopwyrt, elene, ontre, elehtre, sigsonte, galluc, meng
tosomne, lege on.
 31.7.3. Wiþ deadum swile nim grundeswelgean, lege on gleda &
gewyrme & lege þonne swa wearme on þone swile & bebind mid claðe,
læt beon nihterne on gif his þearf sie.
 31.7.6. Wið deadum swile, agrimonian gebeat, meng wið win &
wiþ sealt, do on þone swile, sona gewit aweg.
 31.7.7. Wiþ swile, attorlaðan gecnuwa, lege on þone swile,
lege læst on þæt dolh self.
 31.7.8. Drenc wiþ deadum swile þæt he utslea, eoforþrote,
eolone, gotwoðe, twa wenwyrta do on ealu drince.
 31.7.9. Wiþ deadum swile genim swanewyrt, gecnuwa wel, gemeng
wið ferscre buteran, lege on þone swile oþ þæt gelacnod sie.
 31.7.11. Wiþ swile, cunille, spring wyrt, clate wyl on buteran
& on hunige, lege on þa wyrta, gemeng wið æges þæt hwite.
 31.7.13. Sweþing wiþ swile, ban wyrt ufewearde gecnuwa
smæle, þa wyrte gemeng wið æges þæt hwite, beclæm þæt
lim mid þe se swile on sie.
 31.8.1. Wyrc þæt bæþ of þam ilcum wyrtum on cealdum
wylle wætre, gecnuwa þa wyrta swiþe wel, lege on, þæt wæter lafa
on þone swile.
 31.9.1. Wið swile cnuwa niðewearde hamor wyrt & secg, bind
on.
 32.1.1. Læcedomas wiþ blæce & bæþ, fiftyne ealra.
 32.2.1. Wel eolenan niþewearde & mintan on sealtes rynian
þæt hit sie þicce swa briw, gemeng togædere, smire mid.
 32.2.2. Wiþ blæce nim eolonan niþewearde & ompran eac
swa sio þe swimme & ontran & bisceopwyrt & æscrinde, seoþ on
buteran, aseoh þurh clað, meng þonne wið pipor & wiþ teoran,
gegrind, smire mid.
 32.2.5. Wiþ blæce wyl eolonan on buteran, meng wiþ sote,
sealt, teoro, hunig, eald sape, smire mid.
 32.2.6. Wið blæce genim gose sinero & niþewearde elenan
& haran sprecel, bisceopwyrt & hegrifan, þa feower wyrta cnuwa
tosomne, wel awring, do þæron ealdre sapan cucler fulne gif þu hæbbe,
lytel eles meng wiþ swiþe & on niht alyþre.
 32.2.9. Scearpa þone sweoran ofer sunnan setlgange, geot swigende
þæt blod on yrnende wæter, spiw þriwa æfter, cweþ þonne, hafa
þu þas unhæle & gewit aweg mid gange, eft on clænne weg to huse
& gehwæþerne gang swigende.
 32.2.12. Bæþ wið blæce, awyl tyn siþum þa wyrte on
hwere & syndrigea betonican, neftan, marubian, agrimonian, gearwe, minte,
ehheoloþe, hindheoloþe, curmealle, eordgealla, dile, merce, finul, ealra
emfela gewyrc þonne stol of þrim treowum niþan ðyrele, site on bydene
& þe oferhref ufan mid hwitle þy læs se æþm ut geot under
þone stol on þa bydene, læt reocan on.
 32.2.17. Swa þu meaht on þam wyrtum þriwa don & under
niþan styre mid sticcan gif þu hattre wille & ær þam bæþe
smire þone lichoman & þone andwlitan mid geswette wætre & gehrer
twa ægru on hatum wætere, gesmire ealne þone lichoman mid.
 32.3.1. Læcedom wiþ hreofum lice, adelfe ompran &
gelodwyrt, gecnuwa, wyl þonne on buteran, do hwon sealtes to.
 32.3.2. Wiþ deadum lice, stæþwyrt, merce, gnid on ealoð,
sele drincan.
 32.3.3. Wið hreofle well on hlonde cwicrinde, ellenrinde
niþewearde, æscrinde & wad, elmrinde, hemlic, do þonne buteran on
& hunig.
 32.3.5. Wiþ hreofle, wegbræde, læcewyrt, leac, minte,
magþa eolone, swefl, gecnuwa wiþ rysle, do þæs swefles swilcan þara
wyrta twæde.
 32.4.1. Wiþ hreofle eft genim horses rysele, gemeng swiþe
wiþ sealte, smire mid.
 32.4.2. Bæþ wiþ hreofle, wyl on wætere æscrinde,
cwicbeamrinde, holen rinde, fulanbeames, ananbeames, secg, þeorwyrt,
hegerife, marubian, beþe mid & þæt lic gnid mid þære
hegerifan.
 32.4.4. Wyrc sealfe of marubian on buteran of wyrm meluwe, of haran
sprecele, hegerifan, genim healfe þa sealfe, gemeng wiþ gecnuwade elenan,
smire oþ þæt batige, siþþan mid þære oþerre.
 32.4.7. Bæþ wiþ þam miclan lice, eolone, brom, ifig,
mucwyrt, ælfþone, beolone, cottuc, efelastan, wyl on wætere swiþe,
geot on bydene & sitte on.
 32.4.8. Drince þisne drenc wiþ þon, betonican, curmille,
hofe, agrimonia, springwyrt, reade netle, elehtre, saluie, singrene,
alexandria, sie geworht of wiliscum ealað, drince on þam baþe & ne
læte on þone eþm.
 32.4.11. Sealf wiþ þam miclan lice, elene, þung, ompre,
grundeswelge, hole cersan, wegbræde, efelaste, ontre, hofe, galluc,
celeþonian, cottuc, wel on buteran eal togædere, healf sie swines rysele
oððe horses smeru smire þonne mid.
 32.4.14. Wið swile genim wegbrædan nioþowearde, gecnuwa
wiþ rysele, lege & gebind on þone swile.
 33.1.1. Drencas & sealfa wiþ springe, springwyrt, reade hofe,
wegbræde, fefer fuge, aprotane, mageþe, pipor, win.
 33.1.2. Gif he on earan sie gebeate wegbrædan & fefer fugean
& pipor, wring on þæt eare.
 33.1.3. To sealfe wið springe nim dolhrunan wegbrædan,
mageþan, þone bradan cawel nioþoweardne, geormenleaf niþeweard, docce
niþewerd, reade hofe, butere & hunig.
 33.1.5. Sealf eft medowyrt, acumban, hind hioloðe, gearwe,
cneowholen, æþelferðing wyrt, agrimonia.
 33.2.1. Wiþ deadum springe, wyl on buteran selfætan,
æfterþam & springwyrt.
 33.2.2. Wiþ springe, mageþa, wudu merce, wyrc to sealfe, drince
gode wyrta.
 33.2.3. Wiþ springe nim elehtran, gecnuwa on hunig, meng to
somne, lege on þone swile oþþæt hal sie.
 33.2.4. Wið springe, springwyrt, cerfillan & hunig & gose
smera gecnuwa, wyl to somne, lege on ðone spring.
 34.1.1. Gif nægl sie of handa & wiþ wearhbrædan nim
hwæte corn, meng wið hunig, lege on þone finger.
 34.1.2. Wið angnægle, argesweorf & ealde sapan & ele
gif þu hæbbe, gif þu næbbe do flytan to, meng tosomne, lege on.
 34.2.1. Wiþ wearhbrædan, magoþan croppan wyl on buteran
& sealt, smire mid.
 35.1.1. Be asweartedum & adeadedum lice, sio adl cymð oftost
of omum æfter adle welme on weg gewitenre, weorþeð hwilum lic
asweartod.
 35.1.2. Þonne of þam frum welme sio adl mid cealdum þingum
biþ to celanne & to lacnianne.
 35.1.4. & þonne sio adl cymð utan butan sweotolum tacne
þonne scealt þu ærest þa hæto celan mid cellendre getrifuladre mid
hlafes cruman ofþendum mid ceald wætre oþþe mid þy selfan seawe
þære cellendre oþþe mid æges þy hwite oþþe mid wine oþþe
mid oþrum þingum þam þe þæt ilce mægen hæbbe.
 35.1.8. Þonne se þelma & sio hæto sie aweg gewiten &
se dæl þæs lichoman sie gewended hwon oððe blæc oþþe won
oþþe swilces hwæt scearpa þonne þa stowe.
 35.1.10. Þonne betst þu ða.
 35.1.10. & drige mid onlegene swa swa mon on weax hlafe &
of wearmum bere & of swelcum þingum wyrcð.
 35.1.11. Nis him blod to lætanne on ædre ac ma hira man sceal
tilian mid wyrtdrencum utyrnendum oþþe spiwlum oþþe migolum mid þy
þu meaht clænsian þæt omcyn & þæs geallancoðe þa
readan.
 35.1.14. Ge, þeah þæt yfel cumen ne sie of þara omena
welme swa þeah deah swilcum mannum se scearpa wyrtdrenc.
 35.2.1. Gif þa omihtan wannan þing oþþe þa readan syn
utan cumen of wundum oþþe of sniþingum oððe of slegum sona þu þa
þing lacna mid scearpinge & onlegena beres æfter þære wisan þe
læcas cunnan wel.
 35.2.3. Þu hit betst.
 35.2.3. Gif þæt asweartode lic to þon swiþe adeadige
þæt þær nan gefelnes on ne sie þonne scealt þu sona eal þæt
deade & þæt ungefelde of asniþan oþ þæt cwice lic þæt
þær na miht þæs deadan lices to lafe ne sie þæs þe ær ne
isen ne fyr gefelde.
 35.2.7. Æfter þon lacnige mon þa dolh swa þu þone dæl
þe þonne git hwilce hwega gefelnesse hæbbe & eallunga deade ne
synd.
 35.2.9. Þu scealt mid gelomlicre scearpunge hwilum mid miclum,
hwilum mid feawum, wene & teoh þæt blod fram þære adeadedan
stowe.
 35.2.10. Lacna ða scearpan þus, genim bean mela oþþe
ætena oððe beres oþþe swilces meluwes swa þe þince þæt hit
onniman wille, do eced to & hunig, seoþ ætgædere & lege on
& bind on þa saran stowa.
 35.2.13. Gif þu wolde þæt sio sealf swiðre sie do lytel
sealtes to, on bind hwilum & þweah mid ecede oþþe mid wine.
 35.3.1. Gif þearf sie sele hwilum wyrtdrenc & gesceawa simle
þonne þu þa strangan læcedomas do hwilc þæt mægen sie &
sio gecynd þæs lichoman hwæþer hio sie strang þe heard &
eaþelice mæge þa strangan læcedomas aberan þe hio sie hnesce &
mearwe & þynne & ne mæge aberan þa læcedomas.
 35.3.5. Do þu ða læcedomas swilce þu þa lichoman gesie.
 35.3.5. For þon ðe micel gedal is on wæpnedes & wifes
& cildes lichoman & on þam mægene þæs dæghwamlican wyrhtan
& þæs idlan, þæs ealdan & þæs geongan & þæs
þe sie gewin þrowungum & þæs þe sie ungewuna swelcum þingum.
 35.3.8. Ge, þa hwitan lichoman beoð mearuwran & tedran
þonne þa blacan & þa readan.
 35.3.9. Gif þu wille lim aceorfan oððe asniðan of lichoman
þonne gesceawa þu hwilc sio stow sie & þære stowe mægen for
þon ðe þara stowa sum raþe rotaþ gif hire mon gimeleaslice tilað.
 35.3.12. Sume lator felað þara læcedoma sume raþor.
 35.4.1. Gif þu scyle aceorfan oððe asniþan unhal lim of
halum lice þonne ceorf þu þæt on þam gemære þæs halan lices
ac micle swiþor snið oððe ceorf on þæt hale & þæt cwice
lic swa þu hit sel & raþor gelacnost.
 35.4.3. Þonne þu fyr sette on mannan þonne nim þu merwes
porres leaf & gegniden sealt, ofer lege þa stowe, þonne bið þy þe
raþor þæs fyres hæto aweg atogen.
 35.4.6. Þæt ilce biþ nyttol ices slite oþþe hundes gif
hit man sona to deð.
 35.4.6. & eft ymb þreo niht smire mid hunige þæt þy
þe raþor sio hryfing of fealle.
 36.1.1. Wiþ þære adle þe mon hæt circuladl genim
cwicbeamrinde & æpsan & apuldor, mapuldor, ellen, wiþig, sealh,
wir, wice, ac, slahþorn, bircean, elebeam, gatetreow, æsces sceal mæst,
& ælces treowes dæl þe man begitan mæg butan hægþorne &
alore, þara treowa mæst þe her awriten synd, & eac gagel &
cneowholen, singrenan, eolonan, redic, wealwyrt, þa greatan netlan, wermod,
eorþgeallan.
 36.1.6. Genim þonne tynamberne cetel, do þriddan dæl þara
rinda & þa wyrta wylle swiþe on maxwyrte gif þu hæbbe, gif þu
næbbe wyl on wætre swiþe.
 36.1.8. Do þonne of þa rinda & do niwe on innan þæt
ilce wos, do swa þriwa, aseoh þonne clæne swa hatne þone drenc &
do þonne mele fulne buteran on swa hatne & gehrere togædere, læt
standan twa niht oþþe þreo.
 36.1.11. Ado þonne of þa buteran & genim þonne gagel
croppan & ifig croppan, heldan & betonican, eolonan, redic, banwyrt,
eorðmistel, gebeat togædere, wylle on þære buteran, ado þonne þa
buteran clæne of þam wyrtum þæs þe mon mæge.
 36.1.14. Genim þonne smæl beren mela & gebærned sealt,
briwe þonne on þære buteran & hrere þonne swiþe butan fyre &
do pipor, to ete þonne ærest þone briw on neaht nestig.
 36.1.16. Drince þonne æfter þone drenc & nanne oþerne
wætan tyn nihtum, þritig gif he mæge.
 36.1.17. Genim þonne acmistel, gebeat smæle & adrige &
gegnid to meluwe, aweh þonne wiþ ænne pening, do þæt on þæt
betste win.
 36.1.19. Drinc swa nigon dagas & ne ete niwne cise ne fersce
gos ne ferscne æl ne fersc swin ne naht þæs þe of morode cume ne
fixas unscellehte ne flohtenfote fugelas.
 36.1.21. Gif he hwilc þissa ete sie þæt sealt & nane
þinga beor ne drince & gemetlice win & eala.
 36.1.22. Gif mon þisum læcedome befyligð þonne biþ se
man hal.
 36.2.1. Wiþ circuladle genim doccan þa þe swimman wille,
gebeat swiþe smale, awylle on ealdum morode gode hand fulle, do þonne þa
wyrta of, do eft oþre hand fulle þære ilcan wyrte, wylle eft swiðe,
gedo þonne þa wyrta of, genim þonne swefl, gebeat swiþe smale.
 36.2.4. Gedo þonne on þa sealfe þæt hio sie swa þicce
swa briw, smire þonne þa speccan mid þære sealfe oþ þæt him sel
sie.
 37.1.1. Wiþ þon þe mon ne mæge his micgean gehealdan &
þære geweald nage, eofores clawa oþþe oþres swines gebærn to
ahsan, scead þonne þa ahsan on þæs seocan mannes drincan.
 37.1.3. Eft swines blædran untydrendes, þæt is gylte,
gebærn to ahsan, do on win, sele drincan.
 37.1.4. Wiþ þon ilcan eft, gate blædre ahyrste, sele etan.
 37.1.5. Sume swa gehyrste gegnidaþ to duste, scead on win
sellað drincan gif hie beoð butan fefre.
 37.1.6. Gif mon ne mæge gemigan, eft, cymenes genim swa micel
swa ðu mid þrim fingrum up ahebban mæge, getrifula & gedo to wines
twegen bollan fulle & oþre twegen wæteres, sele drincan nihtnestigum.
 37.1.9. Eft gif mon ne mæge gemigan, drince gyþrifan on
wætre gegnidene.
 37.1.10. Eft genime eac gearwan & wegbrædan, wyl on wine,
sele drincan.
 37.1.11. Eft rammes blædre gesodene þicge he.
 37.1.11. Genim finoles wyrttruman eft & þa wyrt selfe, gebeat
& gegnid on win, ofþæne wel & aseoh, sele drincan.
 37.1.12. Eft gosa tungan gebrædde & geþicge.
 37.1.13. Eft gif þu finde fisc on oþrum fisce innan genim
þone & gebræd swiþe & gebryte on drincan & sele þam seocan
men drincan swa he nyte.
 37.1.15. Swa þu scealt þa oþre ætas & drincan sellan.
 37.1.16. Gif mon ne mæge gemigan drince he lilian wyrttruman
awylledne on wine oððe on ealað.
 37.1.17. Gif he þonne to swiðe mige drince gyþrifan on
wætere gegnidene.
 37.1.18. Gif mon blode mige genim wudurosan, seoþ on wætre
oððe on ealað, sele drincan.
 37.2.1. Gif wif ne mæge gemigan nim tuncersan sæd, seoð on
wætre, sele drincan.
 37.2.2. Gif mon ne mæge gemigan, gecnuwa lufestice &
ellenrinde & oleastrum, þæt is wilde elebeam, gemeng wið surum
hluttrum elað, sele drincan.
 38.1.1. Her sindon dolh sealfa to eallum wundum & drencas &
clæsnunga on gehwilce wisan ge utan ge on þam innoþum, wegbræde
gebeaten wið ealdne rysele gemenged, fersc ne nyt biþ.
 38.2.1. Eft dolhsealf, genim wegbrædan sæd, getrifula smale,
scead on þa wunde.
 38.2.2. Sona bið selre.
 38.3.1. Wiþ ealdre wunde tobrocenre, grundeswelge wiþ ealdne
rysele gemenged & on aled, lacna swilce wunda.
 38.3.2. To wunde clæsnunga genim clæne hunig, gewyrme to
fyre, gedo þonne on clæne fæt, do sealt to & hrere oþ þæt
hit hæbbe briwes þicnesse, smire þa wunde mid, þonne fullað hio.
 38.3.4. Gif banbrice on heafde sie, mageþan & gotwoþan
gecnuwa wel on hunige, do þonne buteran on.
 38.3.6. Þæt bið god dolhsealf.
 38.3.6. Eft wið þon eac biþ god lustmocan crop to lecganne on
gebrocen heafod & gif hund slite.
 38.3.7. Wiþ hundes slite genim þa readan netlan &
attorlaþan & spices, ælces emfela, seoð on buteran, wyrc to sealfe.
 38.3.9. Sona beoð þa unnyttan ban ute.
 38.4.1. Dolhsealf wið lungenadle, hleomoce hatte wyrt, sio
weaxeð on broce, gewyrc þa on morgenne þonne hio gedeaw sie, sume beoð
undeawe, & gose scearn þonne hio ne ete.
 38.4.3. Gecnuwa þa hleomocan, meng wiþ þam gose scearne, do
læs þæs scearnes, wyl on buteran, awring.
 38.4.4. Þæt biþ god sealf.
 38.4.5. Sealf, haran sprecel nim on ealdum lande & lungenwyrt,
seo biþ geolu ufeweard, & æges dydrin, mid þy sceal mon lacnian
þone man þe biþ lungenne wund.
 38.4.7. Wiþ innan wunde sealf, win, ele, galluc, hunig.
 38.4.7. Dolhsealf, gyþrife & gelod wyrt & þa brunan
wyrt bradleafan sio weaxeþ on wuda & lustmoce croppan, gecnuwa þa ealle
& wyl ærest on buteran healfe & awring.
 38.5.1. Dolhsealf eft, grundeswelge þa ðe weaxað on
worþigum, sio biþ god to dolhsealfe, & ribbe & gearwe &
giþrife, gecnuwa þa wyrta ealle, wyl on buteran & awring.
 38.5.3. Eft dolhsealf god, acrind, adrige þa rinde & swiðe
smale gecnuwa & adelf niþeweardne slahðorn, ascaf þa ytemestan rinde
& swiðe smale gecnuwa, asift smale þurh smæl sife, do begea emfela.
 38.5.6. Þæt mela bið god on to sceadenne.
 38.5.6. Gif þu raðe wille lytle wunde gelacnian, eacersan
getrifula oððe geseoð on buteran, wyrc to sealfe, smire mid.
 38.5.8. Dolhsealf, gearwan, gyþrifan, singrenan, gotwoþan
læst, gecnuwa wið buteran swiðe wel, lege neahterne swa gecneden, do
þonne on pannan, wyl swiðe, do þæt fam of clæne aseoh þurh
clað, do on hwit sealt, hrer swiðe oþ þæt gestanden sie.
 38.5.11. Dolhsealf, mersc hofe, æþelferðingwyrt &
gyþrifan & singrenan on þa ilcan wisan wyrce.
 38.5.12. Dolhsealf, genim wades croppan & netelan, eac gecnuwa
wel, wyl on buteran, aseoh þurh clað, do hwit sealt on, hrere swiðe.
 38.6.1. Dolhsealf, acrind, æferðe, meodowyrt, adrige ealle
& gecnuwa smale, asift þurh sife, meng wiþ hunige & æges
þæt hwite.
 38.6.2. Dolhsealf, gif mon sie mid isene gewundod, wudurofe,
singrene, gelodwyrt, springwyrt, gyþrife, grundeswelge, magoðe, wyrmwyrt
nioþoweard, gecnua wel tosomne ealle, meng wið buteran, wyl þa wyrta on
þære buteran swiðe, afleot þæt fam of clæne, aseoh þurh
clað, do on blede, hrer wið oþ þæt gestanden sie.
 38.7.1. Gif mon mid treowe geslegen sie oððe mid stane oþþe
byl on men gebersteð to þon dolhsealf, gyþrife, ontre, gelodwyrt,
sigelhweorfa, gecnuwa þa wyrta swiþe, gemeng wel wið buteran & on
þa ilcan wisan gerena þe ic ær cwæþ.
 38.8.1. Gif men sie lim of aslegen, finger oððe fot oþþe
hand, gif þæt mearh ute sie genim sceapes mearh gesoden, lege on þæt
oþer mearh, awriþ swiðe wel neahterne.
 38.8.3. Dolhsealf, hæsles ragu & holen rinde niþewearde
& gyþrifan, gecnua swiðe wel þa wyrta, gemeng wið buteran, seoð
swiðe, fleot of þæt fam, aseoh þurh clað swiþe clæne.
 38.8.5. Gif þæs dolges ofras synd to hea ymb stric mid hate
isene swiðe leohtlice þæt þæt fel hwitige.
 38.9.1. Dolhsealf, gotwoþan gecnuwa swiðe wel, meg wið
buteran, seoð swiðe & wyll & awring þurh clað, fleot þæt
fam of, geselt swiðe wel.
 38.9.2. Gif dolh fulige ceow strælwyrt on & gearwan.
 38.9.3. Dolhsealf, genim ribban & gearwan & dolhrunan
nioþowearde & doccan & gose scearn & pices lytel & hunig,
wylle on buteran, do on þæt dolh.
 38.9.5. Þonne clænsað hit & halað.
 38.9.6. Dolhsealf, genim gearwan & læcewyrt, wyl on
buteran.
 38.10.1. Sealf wiþ þon þæt dolh ne fulige, genim brer þe
hiopan on weaxaþ, ceow þa rinde on þæt dolh.
 38.10.2. Ne fulaþ hit.
 38.10.2. Dolhsealf, medowyrt nioþeweard, lustmoce, hofe,
eoforfearn, wyl on hunige, do þicce maxwyrt on gemang.
 38.10.4. Dolhdrenc, eoforþrote nioþoweard & medowyrt, eac
swa agrimonia nioþoweard & ufeweard, wyl on ealaþ þa wyrta, gebirm
mid giste, sele drincan.
 38.11.1. Dolhdrenc, geaces suran, wudu cunille, giþrife,
eoforþrote niþewearde, æscþrote, cnuwa smale, do on ceald wæter,
gnid betweoh handum, aseoh þurh clað, sele drincan scenc fulne
neahtnestig.
 38.11.3. Dolhdrenc, ribbe nioþeweard & ufeweard,
eoforþrotan & æscþrotan nioþowearde cnuwa smale, do on weallende
wæter, gnid betweoh handum & aseoh þurh clað, sele drincan.
 38.11.6. To ælcum dolge sealf, gesomna cue mesa, cu migoþa,
gewyrce to flynan þa swa mon sapan wyrcð micelne citel fulne, nim þonne
apuldorrinde & æscrinde, slahþornrinde & wirrinde & elmrinde
& holenrinde & wiþigrinde & geongre ace, sealhrinde do þa ealle
on micelne citel, geot þa flynan on, wyl swiþe lange, do þonne of þa
rinda, wyl þa flenan þæt hio sie þicce, do simle on læssan citel
swa hio læsse sie, geot on fæt þonne hio genoh þicce sie, geæl
þonne cealcstan swiðe & gesamna sot & asift þurh clað &
þone cealcstan eac on þa flynan smire mid þæt dolh.
 38.11.13. Eft wiþ þon ilcan genim hofan & gelodwyrt &
brune wyrt & lustmocan crop & haran sprecel, wyl on buteran & wring
þonne of þa wyrta, do oþre on ribban, bisceopwyrt, gearwan, attorlaþan,
do þa on þa ilcan buteran, wyl eft swiðe, awring þa of.
 38.11.17. Þæt biþ god dolhsealf.
 39.1.1. Her sint læcedomas wiþ ælces cynnes omum &
onfeallum & bancoþum, eahta & twentig.
 39.2.1. Nim grenes merces leaf, gegnid oþþe getrifula wið
ecedes derstan, smire mid þy þa saran stowa.
 39.2.2. Wiþ omum utablegnedum nim sur molcen, wyrc to cealre
& beþ mid þy cealre.
 39.2.3. Wið omum eft genim beordræsta & sapan &
æges þæt hwite & ealde grut, lege on wiþ omena geswelle.
 39.2.4. Wiþ omena geberste sitte on cealdum wætere oþ
þæt hit adeadod sie, teoh þonne up, sleah þonne feower scearpan ymb
þa poccas utan & læt yrnan þæt sticce þe hit wille, wyrc þe
sealfe þus, nim brunewyrt & mersc mear geallan & reade netlan, wyl on
buteran & smire mid & beþe mid þam ilcum wyrtum.
 39.3.1. Wiþ þon ilcan genim angoltwæccean, gegnid swiþe,
do eced to & on bind & smire mid.
 39.3.2. Wiþ þon ilcan genim safinan, gnid to duste & meng
wiþ hunig & smire mid.
 39.3.3. Wið þon ilcan genim gebrædde ægru, meng wið
ele, lege on & beþe swiðe mid betan leafum.
 39.3.4. Eft genim cealfes scearn oþþe ealdes hryþeres wearm
& lege on.
 39.3.5. Eft wiþ þon genim heorotes sceafoþan of felle ascafen
mid pumice & wese mid ecede & smire mid.
 39.3.6. Eft genim eofores geallan, gif þu næbbe nim oþres
swines, gegnid & smire mid þy þær hit sar sie.
 39.3.7. Wiþ þon ilcan genim swealwan nest brec mid ealle aweg
& gebærn mid scearne mid ealle & gnid to duste, meng wiþ eced
& smire mid.
 39.3.9. Wið þon ilcan gehæt ceald wæter mid hatan isene
& beþe gelome mid þy.
 39.4.1. Wiþ hatum omum nim betonican & wermod & finul,
gnid on eala & redic, sele him drincan.
 39.4.2. Wiþ hatum omum nim fenompran & þa smalan clatan,
wyl on gate meolce & supe.
 39.4.3. Wiþ hatum omum nim hunan & efelastan &
alexandrian & betonican & celeþonian & cerlices sæd, drince on
wine.
 39.4.4. Sealf, nim ellenes blostman & þone crop, wyl on
buteran & smire mid.
 39.4.5. Gif hit wille wyrsman smire mid æges geolcan, ofer smire
mid þy & drige to gledum oþ þæt hit heard sie, þweah þonne
aweg & smire eft mid þære sealfe.
 39.4.7. Wiþ hatum omum nim wines dræstan, meng wiþ hreaw
ægru & mid feþere smit on & ne þweah ær hit hal sie.
 39.4.9. Wiþ seondum omum nim cneowholen micle ær oðrum mete
dæghwam to þam dolge & hryþeres geallan, hunig, sot.
 39.4.10. Do tosomne, lacna mid.
 39.4.11. Wiþ þon ilcan, þæt is fic, lustmoce þa
croppihtan nim to baþe & gebærne to sealfe wulfes ceacan þa
winestran & þa teþ sundor, meng wið hunige & smire mid &
ferscne cyse on lege, meng þæt oþer wið meoluce, supe þry morgenas
nigon supan.
 39.5.1. Wiþ bancoþe, þæt is oman, nim nigontyne snæda
eolonan & nygon ontran & endlefan reades secges, do on eala & drinc
micle ær þonne þu ete & þa eolonan ane seoð oþ þæt hio
merwe sie, cnuwa tosomne, smire mid þær ut slea.
 39.5.4. Drenc wiþ onfeallum, cymed, pipor, cost, merces sæd,
ceaster wyrte sæd, cnua wel, do on eala.
 39.5.5. Drenc wiþ onfeallum, cnua on eala oþþe geseoð
celeþonian & heahhioloþan, bisceopwyrt, gyþrifan.
 39.5.6. Drenc wiþ onfeallum, sigsonte, cipe, leac, wegbræde
nioþoweard, wyl ealle on wætre & geswet mid hunige.
 39.5.8. Drenc wiþ þon, nim þa smalan clæfer wyrt
nioþowearde, wyl on ealoþ oððe on beore.
 39.5.9. Drenc wiþ onfealle, wyl on ealoð finuglan, bisceopwirt
heahhioloþe.
 39.5.10. Drenc wiþ onfealle, wyl on ealað spring wyrt oþþe
on beore.
 39.5.11. Drenc eft wið onfealle, wyl on ealaþ cropleac,
dweorgedwostlan, wyrmwyrt.
 39.5.12. Drenc wiþ onfealle, merce, attorlaþe, betoce, rude,
secg, ontre, clate, bisceopwyrt, gewyrc on ealað.
 39.5.13. Eft wiþ onfealle genim æt fruman hæslenne sticcan
oþþe ellenne, writ þinne naman on, asleah þry scearpan on, gefylle mid
þy blode þone naman, weorp ofer eaxle oþþe betweoh þeoh on yrnende
wæter & stand ofer þone man.
 39.5.16. Þa scearpan aslea & þæt eall swiginde gedo.
 39.6.1. Wið onfealle, gefoh fox, asleah of cucum þone tuxl,
læt hleapan aweg, bind on næsce, hafa þe on.
 40.1.1. Wiþ poc adle, onred, hamwyrt nioþoweard, feldmore
niþeweard, onredes emfela & þara oþerra twegea feldmoran healfe
læsse þonne hamwyrte, cnuwa swiðe to somne, do hluttor ealu þæt
þa wyrta oferstige, læt standan þreo niht, sele scenc fulne on morgen.
 40.1.4. Drenc wið pocadle, wyl wæter on croccan, do hunig, on
fleot simle þæt fam of oþ þæt hit nelle ma fæman, sup þonne
& drinc oft & gelome swa þu hatost mæge & mid þy hunige
smire þær hit utslea on þone poc.
 40.1.7. Ne biþ sona nan teona.
 40.1.7. Sealf wiþ pocadle, wyl on buteran singrenan, gearwe,
gyþrife, readre netelan crop.
 40.1.8. Drenc wiþ poccum, bisceopwyrt, attorlaþan, springwyrt,
clatan nioþewearde, on ealað geworht.
 40.1.10. Wiþ poccum, swiðe sceal mon blod lætan &

 40.1.11. Gif hie utslean ælcne man sceall aweg adelfan mid
þorne & þonne win oððe alordrenc drype on innan.
 40.1.12. Þonne ne beoð hy gesyne.
 40.2.1. Wiþ poccum, genim glofwyrt, awyl on buteran & smire
mid.
 41.1.1. Wiþ innan onfealle, næglæs hatte wyrt suþerno,
sio bið god to etanne wiþ innan onfelle on niht nestig.
 41.1.2. Wiþ innan onfealle, wyl elonan, eluhtran, on ealað,
drinc hates bollan fulne.
 41.1.3. Eft wyrtdrenc of wermode, betonican of þære ruwan
wegbrædan, drince fela nihta.
 41.1.4. Wiþ þære geolwan adle, hune bisceopwyrt, helde,
hofe, menge þa togædere, do ælcre gode hand fulle maxwyrte, do to wose
amber fulne & to stanbæþe dyþhomar, hune, wermod.
 41.1.7. Stanbæþ, drince drenc of ompran of wine & of
wætre, geswete swiðe.
 42.1.1. Of gealadle, sio biþ of þære geolwan, cymeþ great
yfel.
 42.1.1. Sio biþ ealra adla ricust þonne geweaxeð on innan
ungemet wætan.
 42.1.2. Þis sint tacn, þæt him se lichoma eall abiterað
& ageolwað swa god seoluc & him beoð under tungan tulge swearte
ædra & yfele & him bið micge geolu.
 42.1.4. Læt him of lungen ædre blod, sele him oft styrgendne
drenc, stanbaðu gelome.
 42.1.5. Wyrc him ðonne stilne drenc of ompran on wine & on
wætre & on þam baðe gehwilce morgene drince mylsce drincan.
 42.1.7. Sio gebet þa biternesse þæs geallan.
 43.1.1. Wiþ wæter bollan, betonican swilce anes peninges
gewæge on wearmum wætere gnide, drince þry dagas ælce dæg godne
bollan fulne.
 43.1.2. Eft genim æscþrotan oþþe wealwyrte wyttruman
þæs seawes feower cucleras fulle, gedo on bollan fulne wines, sele
drincan.
 44.1.1. Wiþ canceradle, þæt is bite, sure, sealt, ribbe,
æg, sot, gebærned lam, hwætes smedma, meng wið ægru, medowyrt,
æferþe, acrind, apuldorrind, slahþornrinde.
 44.1.3. Gif se bite weaxe on men gewirc niwne cealre & lege on,
clæsna þa wunde mid.
 44.2.1. Wiþ cancere, on cyperenum fæte gebærn swefl, gegnid
to duste swa þu smalost mæge & asift þurh clað, meng wið ealde
sapan & sie swefl ricra, do huniges teares medmicel to, sceawe gif to
stið sie þæn mid þy hunige, lege on geormen leaf.
 44.2.4. Þonne hit halige wyl on buteran geaces suran &
singrenan & wudurofan, smire mid þa ofras þær hit readige, læt
þa oðre sealfe clænsian þæt dolh, ne do nan wæter to.
 44.2.6. Sealf wiþ cancre, genim cu meoluc butan wætere, læt
weorþan to fletum, geþwer to buteran, ne wæsc on wætre.
 44.2.8. Nim sigelhweorfan þa smalan unwæscene, do clæne,
cnua swiðe, gemeng wel wið þære buteran, do on pannan ofer fyr, awyl
swiðe, aseoh wel þurh clað, lacna mid þy.
 44.2.10. Wiþ canceradle, acrind on norþan treowe be eorþan
& medowyrt nioþeweard, æferðe niþeweard, cuneglæsse
nioþoweard, do ealra emfela, gecnua to duste, do henne æges þæt hwite
to & hunig, do begea emfela, gemeng wið þam dustum, clæm on ðone
cancer, ne do nan wæter to.
 45.1.1. Wiþ attre drencas & læcedomas, betonican, merce,
wermod, finul, redic, cnua on ealað, sele drincan.
 45.1.2. Wið attre, betonican & þa smalan attorlaþan do on
halig wæter, drinc þæt wæter & et þa wyrta.
 45.1.3. Wið ælcum attre, redic & clate ete ær, ne
mæg þe nan man attre awyrdan.
 45.1.4. Wið ælcum attre, bisceopwyrt niþeweard & elehtre
& springwyrt nioþeweard, eoforþrotan & clatan, awyl on ealað,
sele drincan gelome.
 45.1.6. Gif næddre slea man þone blacan snegl awæsc on
halig wætre, sele drincan, oþþe hwæt hwega þæs þe fram scottum
come.
 45.1.8. Eft wegbrædan gegnid swiþe, drinc on wine.
 45.1.8. Wiþ nædran bite, betonican þætte þry penegas
gewege, do on þry bollan fulle wines, sele drincan.
 45.2.1. Wiþ nædran bite eft, fifleafe awrungenu & wiþ
win gemenged god biþ to drincanne.
 45.2.2. Wiþ nædran bite eft, celeþonie getrifulade, drince
on neaht nestig <foreign>III</foreign> bollan fulle.
 45.2.3. Wiþ nædran slege, springwyrt, atorlaþan,
eoforþrotan, bisceopwyrt, wyrc to drence.
 45.3.1. Wiþ þon þe mon þicge ator genim þa haran hunan,
gewyrc micelne dæl & næderwyrte, cnua togædere & wring
þæt seaw, do wines þrie mel on & sele drincan.
 45.3.3. Wiþ nædran slite nim wegbrædan & agrimonian
& nædder wyrt, sele gegnidene on wine drincan & wyrc sealfe of þam
ilcum wyrtum & nim þa agrimonian gewyrc anne hring ymb þone slite utan,
ne oferstihð hit furþor & bind þa wyrte eft ofer þæt dolh.
 45.3.6. Wiþ nædran slege do of þinum earan þæt teoro
& smire mid ymb & sing þriwa þæs halgan sancte Iohannes gebed
& gealdor.
 45.5.1. Wiþ fleogendum atre & ælcum æternum swile, on
frigedæge aþwer buteran þe sie gemolcen of anes bleos nytne oððe
hinde & ne sie wiþ wætre gemenged, asing ofer nigon siþum letania
& nigon siþum pater noster & nigon siþum þis gealdor.
 45.5.4. Þæt deah to ælcum & huru to deopum dolgum.
 45.5.4. Sume an word wið nædran bite lærað to cweþenne
þæt is, faul, ne mæg him derian.
 45.5.6. Wið nædran slite gif he beget & yt rinde, sio þe
cymð of neorxna wonge, ne dereð him nan atter.
 45.5.7. Þonne cwæþ se þe þas boc wrat þæt hio
wære tor begete.
 45.6.1. Gif hwa drince wyrm on wætere, of sniðe sceap raðe,
drince hat þæt sceapes blod.
 45.6.2. Gif mon sie wyrtum forboren sele springwyrt þæt he ete
& halig wæter supe.
 45.6.3. Wiþ þon þe mon sie forboren gif he hæfþ on him
scyttisc weax, þa smalan attorlaðan, oððe on awyldum ealað drince ne
mæg hine wyrtum forberan.
 46.1.1. Gif anawyrm on men weaxe smire mid þære blacan
sealfe.
 46.1.1. Gif he ut þurh ete & þyrel gewyrce genim huniges
dropan, drype on þæt þyrel, hafa þonne gebrocen glæs geara
gegrunden, scead on þæt þyrel, þonne sona swa he þæs onbirigð
þonne swilt he.
 46.1.4. Sealf wið anawyrme, þus mon sceal wyrcean, genim
<foreign>quinquefolian</foreign> þæt is fifleafe, rudan, wyl on buteran, geswet mid
hunige.
 46.2.1. Drenc, <foreign>quinquefolian</foreign> þæt is fifleafe, sele on
ealað drincan þritig nihta.
 46.2.2. Drenc wið þon, rædices sæd & caules gnid on
eala oþþe on win, drince wiþ anawyrme lange & gelome oþ þæt
sel sie.
 46.2.3. Clam wiþ þon, þa readan tigelan gecnuwa to duste,
gemeng wið grut, abræd cicel, lege on þæt dolh, wyrc oþerne gif
þearf sie.
 47.1.1. Læcedomas wið þeoradlum, æscrind, æspan rind,
elmrind, cwicrind, sio micle worþig netle nioþoweard, wermod,
hindhioloðe, bescreada þa rinda ealle utan, & gecnua swiþe, wyl
tosomne, do ealra emfela, of geot mid hluttre ealoþ, læt standan þone
drenc nihterne on fate ær mon hine drincan wille.
 47.1.5. Drince on morgenne scenc fulne þises drences, to middes
mergenes stande east weard & bebeode hine gode geornlice & hine
gesenige cyrre hine, sungonges ymb, æfter þam drence gange siþþan
& stande sume hwile ær he hine reste, geote swa micel on swa he þær
of do, drince þisne drenc nigon niht & þicge swilcne mete swa he
wille.
 47.1.9. Drenc wiþ þeoradle, sundompran ymb delf, sing þriwa
<foreign>pater noster</foreign>, bred up, þonne þu cweþe <foreign>set libera nos a malo</foreign> genim
þære fif snæda & seofon piporcorn, gecnua togædere & þonne
þu þæt wyrce sing <foreign>XII</foreign> siþum þone sealm <foreign>miserere mei deus &
gloria In excelsis deo & pater noster</foreign>, ofgeot þonne mid wine þonne
dæg & nihtscade, drince þonne þone drenc & bewreoh ðe wearme.
 47.1.15. Genim þonne hind hioloþan ane, ofgeot mid wætere,
drince oþre morgne scenc fulne, þonne oþre siþe seofon snæda &
nigon piporcorn, þriddan siþe nigon snæda & <foreign>XI</foreign> piporcorn.
 47.1.17. Drinc siþþan swiðne drenc seþe wille up yrnan
& of dune, læt þonne blod under ancleow.
 47.2.1. Drenc wiþ þeoradle, nime healf wudu & bulentsan
þa smalan, þunorwyrt, wuduweaxan nioþoweard, wealwyrt nioþowearde,
gecnua þonne ealle tosomne, wyrce him to drence, do on wylisc ealo oþþe
on beor, læt standan nihterne, drince þonne swilcne nigon morgenas, nime
þy teoþan morgne þæs drinces twa bleda fulle, bewylle on ane &
þa wyrta sien mid, aseoh þurh claþ, asete up þær hit eorþan hrinan
ne mæge oþ þæt hit mon drincan mæge.
 47.2.7. Þonne þu hit gedruncen hæbbe bewreoh þe wearme,
lige on þa sidan þe he þonne getenge sie.
 47.2.8. Gif he on þam innoþe bið þonne adrifð hine þes
drinc ut.
 47.2.9. Sealf wiþ þeore, nim garleac & greate wyrt, wermod,
leade netlan cið, gecnua smale & hiorot smeru gemang þæt hit sie
swilc swa dah, do þonne on linenne clað, wyrme þonne gehwæþer ge
þæt lic ge þa sealfe to fyre.
 47.2.12. Þonne þu hit smyrian wille þær sio adl sie fylge
him mid þisse sealfe & mid þys drence.
 47.2.13. Drenc wiþ þeoradle, drige wermod, redic, wealwyrt,
ealra þreora em fela, do on ealu, gnid wel, læte æt ærestan standan
þreo niht ær þon he hine drince & siþþan he hine drince ymb
seofon niht, forlæte blod under þam ancleowe, drince forþ þone drenc
feowertyne niht, læte þonne eft blod under þam oþran ancleowe.
 47.2.17. Drince ealles þone drenc þritig nihta, on undern gode
blede fulle, oþre þonne þu restan wille.
 47.2.19. Wiþ þeorwyrme on fet nim þa readan netlan, gecnua,
do wæter to, lege on hatne stan, læt afreoþan, bind on þone fot
neahterne.
 47.2.20. Eft sealf, ætan gecnua lege on.
 47.2.21. Wiþ þeore on fet gegnid wealwyrt on geswet win &
hwitcwudu & pipor, drince þæt.
 47.3.1. Oxa lærde þisne læcedom, genime wealwyrt &
clufþung & cneowholen & efelastan & camecon & tungilsinwyrt
<foreign>VIIII</foreign>, brune bisceopwyrt & attorlaþan & reade netlan & reade
hofan & wermod & gearwan & hunan & dolgrunan &
dweorgedwostlan, do ealle þas wyrta on wylisc ealo & drince þonne nigon
dagas & blod læte.
 47.3.5. Wiþ þeor wærce wyrc to drence alexandre, sinfulle,
wermod, twa cneowholen, saluian, safine, wealmore, lufestice, fefer fuge,
merce, cost, garleac, æscþrotu, betonice, bisceopwyrt, on twybrownum
ealað gewyrce, swet mid hunige, drinc nigon morgenas nanne oþerne wætan,
drinc æfter swiþne drenc & læt blod.
 47.3.9. Oxa lærde þisne læcedom.
 47.3.9. Wiþ þeore, cneowholen niþeweard, acumba, cwið &
brune wyrt, ealra emfela, do on wilisc ealu, bewyl oþ þriddan dæl &
drince þa hwile þa he þurfe.
 47.3.11. & þær sio adl gesitte fylge him simle mid tige
horne oþ þæt hal sie.
 48.1.1. Wiþ þam wyrmum þe innan eglað þam men genim
wegbrædan, getrifula & þæt seaw sele on cuclere supan & þa
wyrt selfe swa gecnuwade lege on þone nafolan.
 48.1.3. Wið cilda innoþes wyrmum genim grene mintan ænne
gelm, gedo on þry sestras wæteres, seoð oþ þriddan dæl, aseoh,
þonne sele drincan.
 48.1.5. Wið cilda innoþ sare, dweorgedwostle & cymen genim,
gebeat, gemenge wiþ wæter, lege ofer ðone nafolan.
 48.1.6. Sona bið hal.
 48.1.6. Wið wyrmum þe innan eglað, geældes heortes hornes,
ahsan oððe dust gemeng wið hunig, gesmire mid þone bæcþearm &
þone nafolan mid þy, þonne feallað hie.
 48.1.8. Wið wyrmum þe innan eglað getrifolad cost to duste,
gedo godne dæl in hat wæter, sele drincan.
 48.2.1. Wiþ wyrmum eft, gate tord heard & swiðe drige
gemeng & gegnid wiþ hunig, sele drincan.
 48.2.2. Þæt adrifþ hie aweg.
 48.2.2. Wið wyrmum þe innan eglað eft, redic seoð on
wætre oþ þone þriddan dæl, menge wiþ win, sele drincan.
 48.2.4. Eft wiþ þon, gate geallan gedo on wulle, lege &
bind on þone nafolan.
 48.2.5. Wiþ þon ilcan, mintan wel getrifulade meng wiþ hunig,
wyrc to lytlum cliwene, læt forswelgan.
 48.2.6. Eft, ele & ecedes em micel gemenged sele þry dagas
drincan.
 48.2.7. Eft, eoforþrote, merce, betonice, nefte, giðcorn, wyl
on wine.
 48.2.8. Wiþ wyrmum þe innan eglað, wyrtdrenc of ontran, of
feldmoran, sele drincan.
 48.2.9. Sealf, ete celeþonian, brunewyrt awylle on morode, do
þonne scip tearo & swefl to, smire mid.
 49.1.1. Wiþ þam smalan wyrme, wiþewindan twig foreweard &
þa fealwan doccan, næs þa readan, & þis greate sealt gebeaten
togædere swiðe smale & lytel buteran.
 50.1.1. Wiþ hond wyrmum & deaw wyrmum genim doccan oððe
clatan þa þe swimman wolde, þa wyrttruman meng wið fletan & wið
sealt, læt standan þreo niht & þy feorþan dæge, smire mid þa
saran stowa.
 50.2.1. Gif wyrm hand ete genim mersc mear geallan & reade
netlan & reade doccan & smæle clifan, wyl on cu buteran.
 50.2.2. Þonne sio sealf gesoden sie furþum nim þonne sealtes
þry men, scead on, hrer tosomne & smire mid, lyþre mid sapan, ymb niht
smire mid.
 50.2.4. Wiþ deawwyrme stæppe on hat col, cele mid wætre,
stæppe on swa hat swa he hatost mæge.
 50.2.5. Wið deawwyrme sume nimað wearm cwead monnes þynne,
bindað neahterne on, sume swines lungenne wearme.
 50.2.7. Wiþ hond wyrme nim sciptearo & swefl & pipor
& hwit sealt, meng tosomne, smire mid.
 50.2.8. Weax sealf wiþ wyrme, weax sealf, butere, pipor, hwit
sealt, meng tosomne, smire mid.
 51.1.1. Wiþ wyrmum þe mannes flæsc etað, ram geallan
þone fagan cnua on niwe ealo ær þon hit asiwen sie, wele þæt ofer
fyllo drincan þreo niht.
 51.1.3. Eft, genim grunde swelgean þe on eorþan weaxeþ &

 51.1.4. Eft, genim beren ear, beseng, lege on swa hat & hat

 51.1.5. Wiþ flæsc wyrmum genim monnes suran, þa leaf gewel

mæge aræfnan.
 52.1.1. Wiþ lusum, acrind & hwon wermod gecnua on ealu, sele

 53.1.1. Wið smega wyrme, niwe cyse & beobread &

 53.1.1. Eft, monnes heafod ban bærn to ahsan, do mid pipan on.
 54.1.1. Wiþ wyrmætum lice & cweldehtum, acrinde dust,

 55.1.1. Wiþ aslegenum lice, brom, feltere, gearwe, hofe, wyl on

 56.2.1. Wið aslegenum lice sealf, eolone swiðe gesoden &

 57.1.1. Wiþ fice drenc & sealf, wyrmwyrt wylle on meolce

 57.1.1. Sealf, cnua glæs to duste, do huniges tear on, lacna

 58.1.1. To wensealfe & wen bylum wyrc hie of nioþoweardre

 58.2.1. Wensealf, ontre, cersan, reade netlan, wermod, twa

 58.3.1. Wensealf, hiorotes mearh, ifig tearo & gebeaten pipor

 58.4.1. Wiþ þa blacan blegene syle þam men etan twegen

 59.1.1. Wiþ lyftadle nim scenc fulne weallendes wæteres,

 59.1.3. Drinc eall be dropan, rest hwile, sting finger on ciolan,

 59.1.8. Wiþ neurisne, banwyrt do on sure fletan & on hunig,

 59.1.9. Eft, renwyrmas cnua, do on.

 60.4.2. Wiþ þon do æges þæt hwite on gelome.
 60.5.1. Wiþ bryne, wad gecnua, wyl on buteran, smire mid.
 61.1.1. Wiþ lið wærce cnua liðwyrt wið hunige oþþe
ceow & lege on.
 61.1.1. Eft, wulfes heafod ban bærn swiðe & gecnua smale,

 61.1.3. Wið liþ wærce cnua wermod wiþ teorwe &

 61.1.4. Wiþ lið seawe, gelodwyrt, brune wyrt & hare wyrt

 61.1.6. Þæt biþ god sealf.

 61.1.10. Eft, genim surne æppel, gebræd & lege on, do

 61.2.1. Wiþ lið seawe genim mageþan, meng wið hunig, do on

 61.2.2. Wiþ seawe genim acrinde & drige & wirc to smedman

 61.2.3. Wið lið seawe genim cetelhrum & berenhealm,

 61.2.4. Gif liþule utyrne genim merce nioþoweardne & hunig

 61.2.6. Eft, genim medowyrte nioþowearde, gecnua smale, meng

 61.3.1. Gif liþule utyrne genim eced & sure cruman berenes

 61.3.3. Gif liþule utyrne genim wermod & gecnua, do on teoro,

 62.1.1. Wiþ feferadle, elehtran, gyþrife, wegbræde, gecnua

 62.2.1. Wiþ fefre eft hylpð syndrigo marubie to drincanne.
 62.2.1. Wiþ lenctenadle, wermod, eoforþrote, elehtre,

 62.3.5. & þriwa þonne onsupe þæs wæteres swelces

 63.1.1. Wiþ feond seocum men þonne deofol þone monnan fede

 63.1.4. Drenc wiþ feondseocum men of ciricbellan to drincanne,

 63.1.11. Wiþ bræcseocum men, cost, gotwoþe, eluhtre,

 63.1.14. Drince þisne drenc æt æghwilcum niwe nigon
morgenas & nane oþre wætan þæt þicce & stille sie &

 63.1.16. Wið weden heorte, bisceopwyrt, elehtre, banwyrt,

 63.1.18. Mid þy sange þu ga þæt þu sie æt þam
wyrtum & þriwa ymbga & þonne þu hie nime gang eft to ciricean mid
þy ilcan sange & gesing <foreign>XII</foreign> mæssan ofer & ofer ealle þa
drencan þe to þære adle belimpaþ on weorðmynde þara twelfa
apostola.
 64.1.1. Wiþ ælcre yfelre leodrunan & wið ælfsidenne
þis gewrit writ him þis greciscum stafum.
 64.1.2. Eft oþer dust & drenc wiþ leodrunan, genim brembel

 64.1.6. Gif sio adl netnum sie geot mid halig wætre on muð
þæt ilce dust.
 64.1.7. Sealf, elehtre, hegerife, bisceopwyrt, þa readan
