heafod & þa breost.
 64.1.8. Drenc, haran sprecel, alexandrie, rude, elehtre, hegerife,
bisceopwyrt, magoþe, cropleac, armelu, sio cneoehte wenwyrt, do on halig
wæter.
 64.1.10. Gif mon mare ride genim elehtran & garleac &
betonican & recels, bind on næsce, hæbbe him mon on & he gange in
on þas wyrte.
 66.1.1. Wiþ ungemynde & wið dysgunge do on ealo bisceopwyrt
elehtran, betonican, þa suþernan finuglan, neftan, hindhioloðan,
gyþrifan, merce, drince þonne.
 66.1.3. Wiþ ungemynde & disgunge do on eala cassiam &
elehtran, bisceopwyrt, alexandrian, giþrife, feldmoran, & halig wæter,
drince þonne.
 67.1.1. Wið genumenum mete genim elehtran, lege under weofod,
sing nigon mæssan ofer, þæt sceal wiþ genumenum mete, lege under
þæt fæt þe þu wille on melcan.
 67.1.3. Gif ealo awerd sie genim þa elehtran, lege on þa feower
sceattas þæs ærnes & ofer þa duru & under þone þerxwold
& under þæt ealofæt, do mid halig wætre þa wyrt on þæt
eala.
 67.2.1. Gif mete sy awyrd & ungehwæde mylcen oððe fild
oþþe bryþen, halga þa wyrte, do on & under þæt fæt &
under þa duru, do elehtran & clifan & betonican & bisceopwyrt.
 68.1.1. Wiþ þon gif hunta gebite mannan, þæt is swiþra,
sleah þry scearpan neah fromweardes, læt yrnan þæt blod on grenne
sticcan hæslenne, weorp þonne ofer weg aweg.
 68.1.3. Þonne ne biþ nan yfel.
 68.1.3. Eft asleah ane scearpan on þam dolge, gecnua læcewyrt,
lege on.
 68.1.4. Ne biþ him nan yfel.
 68.1.4. Wiþ gongelwæfran bite nim æferþan nioþowearde
& slahþorn rage, adrig to duste, geþæn mid hunige, lacna þæt
dolh mid.
 68.1.6. Wiþ huntan bite, blace sneglas on hattre pannan gehyrste
& to duste gegnidene & pipor & betonican, ete þæt dust &
drince & on lecge.
 68.1.8. Wið huntan bite nim niþeweardne cottuc, lege on
þæt dolh.
 68.1.8. Eft, asleah <foreign>V</foreign> scearpan ane on þam bite & feower
ymbutan, weorp mid sticcan swigende ofer wænweg.
 69.1.1. Wiþ wede hundes slite, agrimonian & wegbrædan
gemenge mid hunige & æges þæt hwite, lacna þa wunde mid þy.
 69.1.2. Wiþ hundes dolge, foxes clate, grundeswelge, wyl on
buteran, smire mid.
 69.1.3. Eft, betonican, getrifula, lege on þone bite.
 69.1.4. Eft, wegbrædan gebeat, lege on.
 69.1.4. Eft, twa cipan oððe þreo seoþ, gebræd on ahsan,
meng wið rysle & hunige, lege on.
 69.1.5. Eft, gebærne swines ceacan to ahsan, scead on, Eft.
 69.1.6. Genim wegbrædan moran, gecnua, wiþ rysle do on
þæt dolh, þonne ascrypð hio þæt ater aweg.
 70.1.1. Gif mon sie to wræne wyl hindheoloþan on wiliscum
ealað, drince on neaht nestig.
 70.1.2. Gif mon sie to unwræne wyl on meolce þa ilcan wyrt,
þonne awrænst þu.
 70.1.3. Wyl on eowe meolce, eft, hindhioloþan, alexandrian,
fornetes folm hatte wyrt.
 70.1.4. Þonne biþ hit swa him leofost bið.
 71.1.1. Wiþ rægereosan, rudan swa grene seoþ on ele & on
weaxe, smire mid þone rægereosan.
 71.1.2. Eft, nim gate hær, smec under þa brec wiþ þæs
rægereosan.
 71.1.3. Gif hoh sino forad sie nim fornetes folm, seoð on
wætre, beþe mid þæt lim & þweah mid þæt lim & wyrce
sealfe of buteran, smire æfter baþe.
 72.1.1. On hwilce tid blod sie to forganne on hwilce to lætenne,
blodlæs is to forganne fiftyne nihtum ær hlafmæsse & æfter fif
& þritig nihtum forþon þonne ealle æterno þing fleogaþ &
mannum swiðe deriað.
 72.1.3. Læcas lærdon þa þe wisoste wæron þæt nan
man on þam monþe ne drenc ne drunce ne ahwær his lichoman wanige butan
his nydþearf wære & þonne on middeldagum inne gewunode forþon þe
sio lyft biþ þonne swiþost gemenged.
 72.1.6. Romane him forþon & ealle suð folc worhton eorþ
hus for þære lyfte wylme & æternesse.
 72.1.8. Eac secgeað læcas þætte geblowene wyrta þonne
sien betste to wyrcenne, ge to drencum ge to sealfum ge to duste.
 72.1.9. Hu mon scule blodlæse on þara six fifa ælcum on
monðe forgan & hwonne hit betst sie, læcas lærað eac þæt nan
man on þon fif nihta ealdne monan & eft <foreign>X</foreign> nihta & fiftyne &
twentiges & fif & twentiges & þritiges nihta ealdne monan ne
læte blod ac betweox þara sex fifa ælcum.
 72.1.13. & nis nan blodlæstid swa god swa on foreweardne
lencten þonne þa yfelan wætan beoþ gegaderode þe on wintra
gedruncene beoð & on kalendas aprilis ealra selest þonne treow &
wyrta ærest up spryttað þonne weaxeð sio yfele gillestre &
þæt yfele blod on þam holcum þæs lichoman.
 72.2.1. Gif monnes blod dolh yfelige genim þonne geormen leaf,
awylle on wætre & beþe mid & gecnua nioþowearde, lege on.
 72.2.2. Gif þu wille on snide blod forlætan nim ceteles hrum,
gegnid to duste, scead on þa wunde.
 72.2.3. Genim rigen healm, eft, & beren, gebærn to duste.
 72.2.4. Gif þu ne mæge blod dolh awriþan genim horses tord
niwe, adrige on sunnan oððe be fyre, gegnid to duste swiþe wel, lege
þæt dust swiþe þicce on linenne clað, wriþ mid þy þæt
bloddolh neahterne.
 72.2.7. Gif þu geotend ædre ne mæge awriþan genim
þæt selfe blod þe ofyrnð, gebærn on hatum stane & gegnid to
duste, lege on þa ædre þæt dust & awrið swiðe.
 72.2.9. Gif mon æt blodlætan on sinwe beslea meng tosomne
weax & pic & sceapen smera, lege on clað & on þæt dolh.
 73.1.1. Gif men cine hwilc lim genim rigen mela, do on þæt lim
& nane wætan.
 73.1.2. Gif þu wætan dest to oþþe smera sealfe ne meaht
þu hit gelacnian & se man sceal swiþe stille beon þy þu scealt hine
halne gedon.
 74.1.1. Wiþ weartum & wearrum on lime genim singrenan &
huniges seaw, meng togædere, do on þa weartan & wearras.
 74.1.2. Eft, cealfes scearn & ahsan gemeng wið eced &
lege on.
 74.1.3. Eft, wiþies rinde gebærn to ahsan, do eced to, trifula
swiðe & lege on.
 75.1.1. Wiþ scurfedum nægle nim gecyrnadne sticcan, sete on
þone nægl wið þa wearta, sleah þonne þæt þæt blod springe
ut, wyrc þonne þymel to & lege eald spic on ufan þone nægl, heald
þritig nihta wiþ wætan, nim þonne hwæten corn & hunig, meng
tosomne, lege on, do þæt to oþ þæt hal sie.
 76.1.1. Wiþ gicþan, doccan & wyrm melu & sealt, ealra
emfela, meng wið sure fletan & smire mid þy.
 76.1.2. Wiþ gicþan, nim sciptearo & ifigtearo & ele,
gnid togædere, do þriddan dæl sealtes, smire mid þy.
 77.1.1. Gif þu wille þæt yfel swile raðe utberste nim weax
& hemlic hatte wyrt, gebeat gewyrmed tosomne, wyrc to sealfe, bind on þa
stowa.
 78.1.1. Gif men unlust sie getenge nime betonican þæt wille
þry penegas gewegan, drinc on swetum wætere.
 79.1.1. Gif mon fram longum wege geteorod sie drince betonican on
þam suðrenan, oxumelle, þæt eceddrenc þe we ær beforan writon
wiþ þære healf deadan adle.
 80.1.1. Wiþ þon þe mon hine fordrince, drince betonican on
wætre ær oþerne drincan.
 80.1.2. Eft, wyl betonican & eorð geallan on hluttrum ealað
oþþe on swilcre wætan swa he drincan scyle, drince simle ær mete.
 80.1.3. Eft, genim swines lungenne, gebræd & on neaht nestig
genim fif snæda simle.
 81.1.1. Wiþ miclan cele nim netelan, seoþ on ele, smire &
gnid ealne þinne lichoman mid.
 81.1.2. Se cyle gewit aweg.
 82.1.1. Gif men sie micel wæce getenge, popig gegnid on ele,
smire þinne andwlitan mid & þone lichoman ealne.
 82.1.2. Wundorlice raþe him biþ sio wæcce gemetgod.
 83.1.1. To monnes stemne nim cerfillan & wuducerfillan,
bisceopwyrt, ontran, grundeswelgean, wyrc to drence on hluttrum ealað.
 83.1.2. Nim þreo snæda buteran, gemenge wið hwæten mela
& gesylte, þige mid þy drence, do swa nigon morgenas, ma gif his
þearf sie.
 84.1.1. Gif mon þung ete, aþege buteran & drince.
 84.1.1. Se þung gewit on þa buteran.
 84.1.2. Eft wiþ þon stande on heafde, aslea him mon fela
scearpena on þam scancan.
 84.1.3. Þonne gewit ut þæt atter þurh þa scearpan.
 85.1.1. Gif mon fundige wiþ his feond to gefeohtanne, stæþ
swealwan briddas geseoþe on wine, ete þonne ær oþþe wylle wætre
seoðe.
 86.1.1. Wiþ miclum gonge ofer land þy læs he teorige,
mucgwyrt nime him on hand oþþe do on his sco þy læs he meþige &
þonne he niman wille ær sunnan upgange cweþe þas word ærest,
<foreign>Tellam te artemesia ne lassus sum in uia</foreign>.
 86.1.4. Gefena hie þonne þu up teo.
 87.1.1. Gif mannes feax fealle wyrc him sealfe, nim þone miclan
þung & haran sprecel & eawyrte nioþowearde & ferdwyrt, wyrc of
þære wyrte & of þisum eallum þa sealfe & of þære buteran
þe nan wæter on ne come.
 87.1.3. Gif feax fealle awylle eoforfearn & beþe þæt
heafod mid þy swa wearme.
 87.1.4. Wiþ þon gif man calu sie, plinius se micla læce
segþ þisne læcedom, genim deade beon, gebærne to ahsan &
linsæd eac, do ele to on þæt, seoþe swiþe lange ofer gledum, aseoh
þonne & awringe & nime welies leaf, gecnuwige, geote on þone ele,
wylle eft hwile on gledum, aseoh, þonne smire mid æfter baþe.
 87.2.1. Heafod bæþ wið þon, weliges leaf wylle on
wætere, þweah mid þy ær þu hit smeruwe & þa leaf cnua swa
gesoden, wriþ on niht on oþ þæt hio sie drige þæt þu mæge
smerwan æfter mid þære sealfe, do swa <foreign>XXX</foreign> nihta, leng gif his þearf
sie.
 87.2.4. Wiþ þon þe hær ne weaxe, æmettan ægru genim,
gnid smit on þa stowe.
 87.2.5. Ne cymð þær næfre ænig feax up.
 87.3.1. Gif hær to þicce sie genim swealwan, gebærn under
tigelan to ahsan & læt sceadan þa ahsan on.
 88.1.1. Wiþ horses hreofle nim þa haranwyrt, cnua wel, gemeng
þonne wið ferscre buteran, wyl swiðe on butran, do on þæt hors swa
hit hatost mæge, smire ælce dæge, do simle þa sealfe on.
 88.1.3. Gif sio hreofol sie micel genim hlond, gehæt mid stanum,
þweah mid þy hlonde swa hatum þæt hors, þonne hit drige sie smire
mid þære sealfe, lacna inne.
 88.1.5. Eft, genim rynian sealt, gehæt, þweah mid þy &
ðonne drige sie smire mid fisces smerwe.
 88.1.7. Gif hors geallede sie nim æþelferðing wyrt &
gotwoþan & mageþan, gecnua wel, do buteran to, wring wætende þurh
clað, do hwit sealt on, hrer swiþe, lacna þone geallan mid.
 88.1.9. Wiþ horses geallan nim æscþrotan & gotwoþan
ufewearde & bogen eac swa, cnua tosomne, wyl on rysle & on buteran,
aseoh þurh clað, smire mid.
 88.2.1. Gif hors sie ofscoten oþþe oþer neat nim ompran
sæd & scittisc weax, gesinge mon <foreign>XII</foreign> mæssan ofer & do halig
wæter on þæt hors oððe on swa hwilc neat swa hit sie, hafa ðe
þa wyrte simle mid.
 88.3.1. Wiþ þon ilcan nim tobrecenre nædle eage, stinge
hindan on þone byrlan, ne biþ nan teona.

Lch II (2 Head)<extent></extent>
B21.2.1.2.1.
Bald's Leechbook: Cockayne 1864-6, II, 158-174 (Bk II, Table of Contents).



 1. Þas læcedomas belimpað to eallum innoþa mettrymnessum.
 2. Læcedomas wiþ magan sare, ealra <foreign>X</foreign>, & gif se maga
aþened sie & hwæt he þicgean scyle on þære adle.
 3. Læcedomas be geswelle & sare þæs magan, hu him mon
scyle blod lætan.
 4. Læcedomas wiþ heardum swyle þæs magan & smerenessa
& hwæt he þicgean scyle.
 5. Læcedomas wiþ magan aþundenesse & hwæt he on
þære adle þicge.
 6. Læcedomas wiþ unluste & wlætan þe of magan cymð
& hwæt he þicgean scyle, <foreign>IIII</foreign> cræftas.
 7. Læcedomas wið adeadodum magan & gif he forsogen sie
& tacn adeadodes magan, hu þæt ne gemylt þæt he þigeþ, <foreign>VI</foreign>
læcedomas.
 8. Læcedomas wiþ sare & unluste þæs magan se þe ne
mæg ne mid mete ne mid drincan beon gelacnod & bitere hræcetunge
þrowað, <foreign>IIII</foreign> cræftas.
 9. Læcedomas wiþ inwunde magan.
 10. Læcedom wið wlættan & to hætenne untrumne
magan.
 11. Læcedom wiþ aþundenesse magan windigre & eþunge.
 12. Læcedom wiþ spiwþan & wiþ þon ðe him mete
under gewunian nelle.
 13. Læcedom wiþ magan springe.
 14. Læcedom wið eallum magan untrumnessum.
 15. Læcedom wiþ þæs magan springe þonne þurh muþ
bitere hræcð oþþe bealcet oþþe him on þam magan se mete
abiterað & sygeþ & hu sio ablawung þæs magan cymð of þam
blacum omum.
 16. Læcedomas & tacn þæs hatan omihtan magan, ungemet
fæsta, & þæs ungesceadlice cealdan magan; Tacn hu se hata omihta
maga ungemet þurst & swol þrowað & nearonesse & geswogunga
& gemodes tweonunge, unlust ge wlætta & hu ðone cealdan magan
ungeliclice mettas lyste, læcedomas to bæm micle & eþele & be
lattre meltunge sumra metta.
 17. Læcecræftas be lifre missenlice gecyndo & adlum &
hu hio on þa swiðran sidan aþened biþ oþ þone nuseoþan & hu
hio biþ fiflæppedu & hu hio is blodes timber & hus &
þætte sex þing wyrceaþ liferwærce & lacnung þara ealra &
sweotol tacn þara ealra, ge be micgean ge be unluste ge be his hiwe &
oþrum manegum tacnum.
 18. Læcas lærað þisne læcedom wiþ lifre swyle &
aþundenesse.
 19. Læceas secgeaþ þas tacn be aswollenre & gewundadre
lifre & læcedomas wið þon & be þære lifre heardunge.
 20. Læcas lærað þis wiþ þære lifre wunde þonne
se swyle ge wyrms tobyrst.
 21. Læcedomas & tacn aheardodre lifre & ablawenre on
manigfealde wisan, ge on þam læppum ge on þam uferum ge on þam
filmenum ge on þam holcum þære lifre.
 22. Læcedomas wiþ þære gefelan heardnesse þære lifre
& sealfa & wyrtdrencas oþþe gif hio tobyrst & niþer gewit
oððe upastihð oþþe to langsum wyrð sio ungefele aheardung þære
lifre.
 23. Læcedomas hwæt him sie to forganne on liferadle, hwæt
him sie to healdanne, ge on læcedomum ge on mete, & tacn þæt se
swile þwinan ne mæg ne utyrnan on þære lifre.
 24. Læcedomas & wyrtdrencas wiþ eallum lifer wærcum,
ealra þreotyne, & gif lifer weaxe.
 25. Læcas eac be eallum wambe coþum & adlum sweotol tacn
fundon & læcedomas & hu mon þa yfelan wætan þære wambe
lacnian scyle & þonne adl to þære wambe wile for þære yfelan
omihtan wætan, cneow hatiað, lendenu hefegiað, sariað þara lendena
liran, togeoteþ betweox sculdrum, utgong gemenged.
 26. Læcedomas gif sio wamb wund bið, hu þæt mon ongitan
mæge & gelacnian, <foreign>V</foreign> cræftas.
 27. Læcedomas be wambe missenlicre gecyndo oþþe misbyrdo, hu
þæt mon mæge ongitan & gelacnian & be wambe hattre gecyndo
& be cealdre & wætre gecyndo & be hattre & drigre gecyndo
& þæt hæmed þing ne duge þyrrum lichoman & ne sceþeþ
hatum ne wætum, seofon cræftas, & þætte hæmed þing
swiðost eglað þam ðe hornadle habbað.
 28. Læcedomas wiþ þon þe monnes þæt uferre hrif sie
gefylled wið yfelre wætan & be windigre wambe.
 29. Læcedomas wiþ þon þe mete untela mylte & cirre on
fule & yfle wætan oþþe scittan.
 30. Læcedomas gif þu wille þæt þin wamb sie simle
gesund & be coðe & sare be wambe coðe & innefaran sare & to
wambe gemetlicunge, syxtyne cræftas.
 31. Læcedomas & tacnung on þam roppe & smæl
þearme & on utgonge, hu hie þrowiað ormætne þurst & unlust
& be hiora hiwe & þam nafolan & rægreosan & bæc
þearme & niweseoþan & milte, scare & hu unlæcas wenað
þæt þæt sie lendenadl oþþe milt wærc & hwær þa wamb
seocan þa adle þrowien & hu him sie & hu hiora mon tilian scyle,
feower wisa.
 32. Læcedomas hu mon swa geradne man lacnian scule ge mid
blodlæse & sealfe & baðo & lacnung on þæt hrif to
sendanne; & þas læcedomas magon wið lendenece & gif mon sonde
mige, wiþ ut wærce, wið magan adlum & clawunga & wifa
dedternessum & be þære coðe hu man lyste utgan & ne mæg &
gif se utgang sie windig & wæterig & blodig, <foreign>XII</foreign> wisan.
 33. Læcedomas wið þære frecnan coðe þe se mon his
utgang þurh ðone muð him fram wyrpð & aspiwan sceal & wið
Innoðwundum & smæl þearma sare & wið tobrocenum innoþum
& wiþ fortogenesse innan & wið þære wambe þe late mylt &
se þara læcedoma ne gimð þonne becymð him on wæter bolla, lifer
wærc, miltes sar, micgean forhæfdnes, wambe ablawung, lendenwærc, sond
& stanas on blædran weaxað, þreotyne cræftas.
 34. Læcedomas & be þæs mannes mihtum sceal mon þa
læcedomas sellan þe þonne gefoge synd, ge heafde ge heortan & wambe
& blædran & sogeþan, & hu geares hit sie be hæto & cele
& wiþ lattre meltunge oððe gif wamb forweaxen & forwundod sie
& gif mon sie innan forblawen & wið wambe wrinum & gicþum,
nygan wisan.
 35. Læcedomas be cilda oferfyllo & wambe & gif him mete
tela ne mylte & him swat ofga & stince fule.
 36. Læcedomas be miltewærce & þæt he bið on þa
winstran sidan & tacn ðære adle, hu higelease hi beoð, & hu lang
se milte sie & be þæs miltes filmene on þa winstran healfe, be
hleahtre þe of milte cymð, hu se milte æghwæt þrowað þæs
þe oþer limo ge hat ge ceald & be bæðe & hæmed þinge
& hwanan sio hæto cume & cele þæs miltes, eahta cræftas.
 37. Læcedomas hu mon scyle þone monnan innan & utan mid
cealdum & hatum læcedomum lacnian & hwilc mete him sie to þicgenne
& hwilc him sie to forganne.
 38. Læcedomas hu mon sceal þa wætan & wonsceafta utan
lacnian & be þam wætum yflum þæs miltes & wið slipunge
wætan þæs miltes.
 39. Læcedom wiþ windigre aþundenesse þæs miltes, sio
cymð of æpla æte & hnuta & pysena & huniges æte &
þone rop & inneforan & wambe & magan þa geondblawad & wið
sogeþan & seadan þe of milte cymð & hu sio adl gewent on wæter
bollan, ealles tyn cræftas.
 40. Læcedomas be ablawunge & aheardunge þæs blodes on
þam milte.
 41. Læcedomas wiþ þære heardnesse & sare miltes &
hu mon mæg swines blædran mid ecede gefyldre gehnescan þa heardnesse
& wiþ eallum inadlum, þry cræftas.
 42. Læcedomas gif omihtre blod & yfele wætan on þam
milte syn þindende, þonne sceal him mon blod lætan on þas wisan þe
þeos læceboc segþ & be þæs blodes hiwe.
 43. Læcedomas hwæt him on þære adle to þicgenne sie
hwæt to forganne.
 44. Læcedom, eft, se þe þæt yfel uttihð of þam milte,
swiðe æþele, & se eac deah wiþ magan ablawunge & innoþa,
hnesceþ þa wambe, þynnaþ þa oman, bitere hræcetunge aweg deþ
& breost coþe & sid wærc & lifer adle & milte wærc
& wambe wind, eal þa liht.
 45. Læcedomas & swiðdrenc wiþ aswollenum.
 46. Læcedomas wiþ gehwæþerre sidan sare & tacn
wundorlicu hwanan sio cume & hu sio adl toweard sie & hu mon þara
tilian scyle.
 47. Læcedomas þa ðe þynnunge hæbben & smalunge
mægen, þam lichoman þe þa hæto medmicle oþþe strange þrowien
& hu mon scyle swines blædran on don.
 48. Læcedomas selran gif þas oþre helpe ne syn, hu him mon
eac blod scyle lætan.
 49. Læcedomas & weax sealfa & scearpunga wiþ sidan
sare & hwæt he þicgean scyle.
 50. Læcedomas eft wið sidan sare.
 51. Læcedomas wið lungenadle & laþlicu tacn, hwanan sio
adl cume & hu mon lacnian scyle, drencas & sealfa & briwas, ge
wið lunge wunde & gif lungen breoþe & gif lungen drugige, an &
twentig cræfta.
 52. Læcedomas & spiwedrencas mannum to hæle & gif man
hine ofer gemet brece to spiwanne & eft wece drenc oþþe gif drenc of
men nelle ealles, twentig drencea.
 53. Læcedomas & leohte drencas mannum to hælo &
unspiule drenceas wiþ untrumum innoþum, eahta cræftas.
 54. Læcedomas & drencas wið instice & gif stice butan
innoþe sie.
 55. Læcedomas & drencas gif mon innan forhæfd sie &
wiþ incoþe & fær coþe.
 56. Læcedomas gif mon sie on utwærce & tacn be utsihte,
ge on þam uferran hrife ge on þam niþerran, & hwanan sio adl cume
& hu mon hie scyle lacnian & hwæt mon þicgean scyle; & eft
wiþ þon gif mon blode ane utyrne & wiþ miclum sare & ablaunesse
þæs innoþes oþþe gif mon for roppes untrumnesse utyrne oþþe gif
hwa blodryne þrowige on þam niþerran dælum his lichoman oþþe gif
hwam sie micge on blod, gif hio gehwyrfþ oððe gif mon utgang næbbe
& eft utyrnende briw, fif & hund seofontig læcedoma.
 57. Læcedomas wiþ þearmes utgange & gif men bilyhte sie
ymb þone þearm & wið blæc þearmes utgange, nigon wisan.
 58. Læcedomas be þære adle þe stanas on men innan
geweaxen on þære blædran oððe elles hwær & tacn þære
adle be halra manna & unhalra micgea hiwum & hwilcne mete mon þicgean
scyle oþþe forgan, twentig cræfta.
 59. Læcedomas wiþ þære healfdeadan adle & hwanan sio
cume & hu mon lacnian scyle, sealfa & onlegena & wyrtdrencas,
oþþe gif neb oþþe heafod sar sie, be baðe & blodlæse &
þæt sio adl ær feowertigum oþþe fiftigum wintra on monnan ne becume
& be þam suþernan wyrteceddrence, an & twentig cræfta.
 60. Læcedomas wiþ wifa gecyndum forsetenum & eallum wifa
tydernessum, gif wif bearn ne mæge geberan oþþe gif bearn weorþe dead
on wifes innoþe oððe gif hio cennan ne mæge do on hire gyrdels þas
gebedo swa on þisum læcebocum segþ; & manigfeald tacn þæt mon
mæge ongitan hwæþer hit hyse cild þe mæden cild beon wille &
wiþ wifa adle & gif wif migan ne mæge & gif wif ne mæge raðe
beon geclænsod & wiþ wifa blodsihtan & gif wif of gemyndum sie
& gif þu wille þæt wif cild hæbbe oþþe tife hwelp oþþe
gif men cwið sie forweaxen oþþe gif man semninga swigie, an &
feowertig cræfta.
 61. Læcedom wiþ þære geolwan adle & wið þæm
miclan lice & dolhdrencas twegen & oþer mæg wiþ lungen wunde
eac.
 62. Læcedomas wiþ miclum heafod ece & wærce & sealf
to þon ilcan & leah & eagsealfa & gebed to eagum.
 63. Læcedom wiþ þeoradle & wiþ lungenadle & wiþ
utwærce & gif mon blode spiwe & wiþ blodryne & gif lim
færinga ace & wiþ blæce on andwlitan.
 64. Læcedom, se monian wiþ innoþes forhæfdnesse &
gutomon/ wið milte wærce & stice & spican wiþ utsihtan &
dracontian wiþ fule horas on men & alwan wiþ untrymnessum &
galbanes wiþ nearwum breostum & balzaman smiring wiþ eallum
untrumnessum & petraoleum to drincanne anfeald wiþ innan tydernesse &
utan to smerwanne & tyriaca, is god drenc, wiþ innoþ tydernessum &
se hwita stan wið eallum uncuþum brocum.
 65. Læcedom gif hors sie ofscoten & wiþ utwærce &
gif utgang forseten sie & wiþ lenctenadle, eft, wiþ utwærce &
wiþ unlybbum & wiþ þære geolwan adle & gif men sie færlice
yfele & to gehealdanne lichoman hælo & wiþ gicþan & ælue
& wiþ londadle & gongelwæfran bite & wið utsihte &
heafodsealfa.
 66. Be þam stane þe gagates hatte.
 67. Be wæge eles & oþerra missenlicra þinga.
