 55.1.1. Drenc gif mon innan forhæfd sie, gecnua eolonan, wyl on
ealoð & betonican, wermod & þa clufihtan wenwyrt, sele drincan.
 55.1.2. Wiþ incoþe costes, godne dæl & finoles sædes
oþer swilc, gebeat smæle & gegnid to duste, genim þæs cucler
fulne, gedo on eald win oþþe cæren drince, þonne neahtnestig þry
dagas.
 55.2.1. Wiþ færcoþe, bisceopwyrt, wermod, betonica, redic,
merce, cost, rudan sæd, wyrc to drence.
 56.1.1. Gif mon ne mæge utgegan genim uman & eac gecrypte
hand fulle & medmicelne bollan fulne ealað, bewyl þrimme þæt ealo
on þære wyrte, drince þonne neahtnestig.
 56.1.3. Eft, gif mon syþ garleac on henne broþe & selð
drincan þonne to læt hio þæt sar.
 56.1.4. Eft, gate meoluc & eced seoþ ætgædere, sele
drincan.
 56.1.5. Eft, gate meoluc & hunig & sealt, sele drincan.
 56.1.5. Eft, wylle gearwan on hunige & on butran, ete þa wyrt
mid.
 56.2.1. Wiþ utwærce eft, efelastan ufewearde, wegbrædan,
ellenrinde, sealt on ealo gegniden.
 56.3.1. Tacn be utsihtan, ge on þam eferran hrife ge on þam
niþerran, þa adle mon mæg ongitan be þam utgange, hwilc se on onsyne
sie.
 56.3.2. Sum biþ þynne, sum mid þiccum wætum geond goten,
sum mid þæs innoþes & mid þara smæl þearma gebrocum gemenged,
sum swiðe gefylled mid wormse, sum swiðe blodig, sum cymð of þam
uferran hrife, sum of þam niþerran.
 56.3.5. Þam þe of þam uferran hrife cymð se utwærc þis
tacn bið, þæt se man sar gefelð æt his nafolan & on his
sculdrum hefig sar & þurst & unlust & þurh bæc þearm lytel
blod dropað.
 56.4.1. Sio utsihtadl cymð manegum ærest of to miclum utgange
& þonne lange hwile ne gymð mon þæs oþ þæt se innoþ
wyrð ge onburnen ge þurh þæt gewundod.
 56.4.3. Hwilum onginneð of þam midhrife, se is betweox
þære wambe & þære lifre, & þa seaw þa ðe beoð
gemengedu of mettum wiþ blod & wiþ oman geondgeotaþ þone innoþ
wyrceað yfelne utgang & for þære grimnesse þara omena ne mæg
beon gehæfd þy se mete ac beoþ somod þa innoþas bedrifen þonne
wyrð þæt to utwærce.
 56.4.7. Hu mon þa utyrnendan men scyle lacnian, þam mon sceal
sellan þa mettas þa ðe wambe nearwian & þam magan ne sceþþan,
caules seaw, hwilum pysena broþ & eced & por mid wegbrædan gesoden
& ealdne cyse gesodenne on gate meolce mid þy smerwe gate.
 56.4.10. Hwilum bræde þone cyse & drigne hlaf &
wæter þæt sie rose on gesoden, hwilum scearp win drince.
 56.4.12. Wyrc him onlegena to clame geworht, beren melo oþþe
hwæten mid hunige gesoden mid medmicle.
 64.1.1. Þætte oþerne healfne pening gewege, gegnid swiþe
smale, do þonne on hluttor æg & sele þam men to supanne.
 64.1.2. Hio is swiþe god eac on þas wisan wið hwostan &
wiþ springe, do þas wyrte on, he biþ sona hal.
 64.1.3. Þis is balzaman smyring wiþ eallum untrumnessum þe on
mannes lichoman biþ, wiþ fefre & wiþ scinlace & wið eallum
gedwolþinge.
 64.1.5. Eal swa same se petra oleum he is god andfeald to drincanne
wið innan tiedernesse & utan to smerwanne on wintres dæge for þon
þe he hæfð swiðe micle hæte, for ðy hine mon sceal drincan on
wintra & he is god gif hwam seo spræc oþfylð, nime þonne &
wyrce cristes mæl under his tungan & his an lytel swelge.
 64.1.10. Gif mon eac of his gewitte weorðe þonne nime he his
dæl & wyrce cristes mæl on ælcre lime, butan cruc on þam heafde
foran, se sceal on balzame beon & oþer on þam heafde ufan.
 64.2.1. Tyriaca is god drenc wiþ eallum innoð tydernessum &
se man se þe hine swa begæþ swa hit her on segð þonne mæg he him
miclum gehelpan.
 64.2.2. To þam dæge þe he wille hine drincan he sceal
fæstan oþ midne dæg & ne læte hine wind beblawan þy dæge.
 64.2.4. Ga him þonne on bæþ, sitte þær on oð þæt
he swæte.
 64.2.5. Nime þonne ane cuppan do an lytel wearmes wætres on
innan, nime þonne ane lytle snæd þæs tyriacan & gemenge wiþ
þæt wæter & seoh þurh þynne hrægl, drince þonne.
 64.2.7. & ga him þonne to his reste & bewreo hine wearme
& licge swa oþ he wel swæte.
 64.2.8. Arise þonne & sitte him up & scirpe hine &
þicge siþþan his mete to nones & beorge him georne wiþ þone wind
þæs dæges.
 64.2.10. Þonne gelyfe ic to gode þæt hit þam men miclum
gehelpe.
 64.3.1. Se hwita stan mæg wiþ stice & wiþ fleogendum
attre & wiþ eallum uncuþum brocum.
 64.3.2. Þu scealt hine scafan on wæter & drincan tela
micel & þære readan eorþan dæl scafe þær to & þa
stanas sint ealle swiðe gode of to drincanne wiþ eallum uncuþlicu
þing.
 64.3.4. Þonne þæt fyr of þam stane aslegen hit is god
wið ligetta & wið þunorrada & wið ælces cynnes gedwol þing
& gif mon on his wege biþ gedwolod slea him anne spearcan beforan biþ
he sona on rihtan.
 64.3.7. Þis eal het þus secgean ælfrede cyninge domne helias
patriarcha on gerusalem.
 65.1.1. Gif hors ofscoten sie nim þonne þæt seax þe
þæt hæfte sie fealo hryþeres horn & sien <foreign>III</foreign> ærene næglas
on, writ þonne þam horse on þam heafde foran cristes mæl & on
leoþa gehwilcum þe þu ætfeolan mæge.
 65.1.3. Nim þonne þæt winestre eare þurh sting swigende,
þis þu scealt don, genim ane girde, sleah on þæt bæc.
 65.1.5. Þonne biþ þæt hors hal.
 65.1.5. & awrit on þæs seaxes horne þas word,
<foreign>Benedicite omnia opera domini dominum</foreign>.
 65.1.6. Sy þæt ylfa þe him sie þis him mæg to bote.
 65.1.7. Wiþ utwærce, brembel þe sien begen endas on
eorþan, genim þone neowran wyrttruman, delf up, þwit nigon sponas on þa
winstran hand & sing þriwa, <foreign>miserere mei deus</foreign> & nigon siþum
<foreign>pater noster</foreign>, genim þonne mucgwyrt & efelastan, wyl þas þreo on
meolcum oþ þæt hy readian, supe þonne on neaht nestig gode blede fulle
hwile ær he oþerne mete þicge.
 65.1.12. Reste hine softe & wreo hine wearme.
 65.1.12. Gif ma þearf sie do eft swa, gif þu þonne git
þurfe do þriddan siþe, ne þearft þu oftor.
 65.1.13. Gif utgang forseten sie genim giðcornes leafa gode hand
fulle & þa ruwan wegbrædan nioþowearde & doccan þa þe
swimman wille, wyl þas þreo on ealdum ealað swiþe & do sealte
buteran on, wylle þicce læt drincan gode blede fulle hwile ær oðrum
mete & wreoh hine wearme & reste stille, do þus þriwa, ne þearf
oftor.
 65.2.1. Wiþ lungenadle læcedom dun tæhte, saluie, rude be
healfan þære saluian, fefer rugian emmicel þara twegea wyrta, þære
saluian þreo swelc dweorgedwostlan, hiere þe nu ealra wyrta fyrmest on
þa sealfe.
 65.2.3. Þe him þises læcedomes þears sie healde hine
georne wiþ geswet eala, drince hluttor eala & on þæs hluttran
ealað wyrte wylle geonge acrinde & drince.
 65.2.6. Wiþ utwærce genim unsmerigne healfne cyse, do
englisces huniges <foreign>III</foreign> snæda to, wylle on pannan oþ þæt hit brunige,
genim þonne geongre acrinde hand fulle & swa swigende æt ham gebring
& næfre in on þone mon, sceafe þæt grene on utan, wylle þa
sæp spone on cu meolce, geswete mid þrim snædum huniges, þone drenc
þicge þonne mid ðy cyse, æfter drence, <foreign>VII</foreign> niht eala forga &
meoloc þicge unsure.
 65.2.11. Wiþ unlybbum supe cu buteran <foreign>VIIII</foreign> morgnas, <foreign>III</foreign>
sopan, <foreign>VIII</foreign> morgnas cerfillan gemetlice on wine, þridda dæl wætres,
nime þonne hwerhwettan nioþowearde, gnid on wylisc ealo, swete mid hunige,
drince þære teoþan niht, to mete þone drenc on þreo þicge æt
þam þrim honcredum.
 65.3.1. Wiþ þære geolwan adle genim nioþowearde eolenan,
gedo þæt þu hæbbe on þan forman dæge, þonne þu hire ærest
bruce on morgen nim þreo snæda & þreo on niht & hire sculon beon
on hunig gesnæd & þy æfteran mergen <foreign>IIII</foreign> snæda & <foreign>IIII</foreign> on
niht & þriddan mergen <foreign>V</foreign> snæda & <foreign>V</foreign> on niht & þy feorþan
mergen <foreign>VI</foreign> & <foreign>VI</foreign> on niht.
 65.3.5. Þes drenc sceal wiþ þon ilcan, genim alexandrian
& grundeswelgean, cnua smale & do to drence on hluttrum ealað.
 65.3.6. Gif men sie færlice yfele wyrce <foreign>III</foreign> cristes mæl, an
on þære tungan, oþer on þam heafde, þridde on þam breostum.
 65.3.8. Sona bið sel.
 65.3.8. To gehealdanne lichoman hælo mid drihtnes gebede þis
is æþele læcedom, genim myrran & gegnid on win swilce sie tela
micel steap ful & þicge on niht nestig & eft þonne restan wille.
 65.3.11. Þæt gehealdeþ wundorlice lichoman hælo & hit
eac deah wiþ feondes costungum yflum.
 65.4.1. Þonne is eft se æþelesta læcedom to þon ilcan,
genim myrran & hwit recels & safinan & saluiam & wurman, &
þæs recelses & myrran sy mæst & þa oþre syn awegene, þara
sien emfela & ætsomne on mortere gegnide to duste, sette under weofod
þonne cristes tid sie & gesinge mon <foreign>III</foreign> mæssan ofer þa <foreign>III</foreign> dagas
on midne winter & æt stefanes tide & sancte Iohannes euangelista
& þa þry dagas þicge on wine on neaht nestig & þæt þær
to lafe sie þæs dustes hafa & geheald.
 65.4.7. Hit mæg wiþ eallum fær untrymnessum, ge wiþ fefre
ge wiþ lenctenadle ge wiþ atre ge wiþ yfelre lyfte.
 65.4.8. Gewritu eac secgeaþ se þe þone læcedom bega
þæt he hine mæge gehealdan <foreign>XII</foreign> monaþ wiþ ealra untrymnessa
frecenesse.
 65.5.1. Þonne eft wið gicþan, þæt eal se lichoma sy
clanes hiwes & glades & beorhtes, genim ele & ealdes wines
dræstan emfela, do on mortere, gemeng wel to somne & smire mid þy
þone lichoman on sunnan.
 65.5.3. Wið ælfe & wiþ uncuþum sidsan gnid myrran on
win & hwites recelses em micel & sceaf gagates dæl þæs stanes
on þæt win, drince <foreign>III</foreign> morgenas neaht nestig oþþe <foreign>VIIII</foreign> oþþe
<foreign>XII</foreign>.
 65.5.6. Wiþ londadle wyl wermod swa drigne, swa grenne swa þer
he hæbbe on oleo infirmorum oþ þæt þæs eles sie þriddan
dæl bewylled & smire mid þone lichoman ealne æt fyre & mæsse
preost sceal don þone læcedom gif man hæfþ.
 65.5.9. Wiþ gongel wæfran bite, smit on isen swat.
 65.5.9. Wiþ utsihte, mer geallan, blæc snegl, wyl on meolcum,
sup on æfenne & on morgenne.
 65.5.11. Heafod sealf, murre & alwe, libania, ealra gelice
fela, meng wiþ eced, smire mid þæt heafod.
 65.5.12. Wiþ þon ilcan, swefl & swegles æppel, murre
& æghwilces cynnes recels, nigon wyrta englisce, polleie, brembel,
æppel, elehtre, bisceopwyrt, finul, ruwe wegbræde, haran sprecel, sio
hare wyrt, liþ wyrt, ealra þissa emfela, oleum infirmorum, halig wæter,
halig sealt, oþer ele, smire þe mid þys ufan þonne þu hi gnide.
 66.1.1. Be þam stane þe gagates hatte is sæd þæt he
<foreign>VIII</foreign> mægen hæbbe.
 66.1.1. An is, þonne þunorrad biþ ne sceþeð þam men
þe þone stan mid him hæfð.
 66.1.2. Oþer mægen is, on swa hwilcum huse swa he biþ ne
mæg þær inne feond wesan.
 66.1.4. Þridde mægen is þæt nan attor þam men ne mæg
sceþþan þe þone stan mid him hafaþ.
 66.1.5. Feorþe mægen is þæt se man se þe þone laþan
feond on him deagollice hæfþ gif he þæs stanes gesceafenes hwilcne
dæl on wætan onfehð þonne biþ sona sweotol æteowod on him
þæt ær deagol mað.
 66.1.7. Fifte mægen is, se þe ænigre adle gedreht biþ gif
he þone stan on wætan þigeþ him biþ sona sel.
 66.1.9. Syxte mægen is þæt drycræft þam men, ne
dereþ se þe hine mid him hæfð.
 66.1.10. Seofoþe mægen is þæt se þe þone stan on
drince onfehð he hæfþ þe smeþran lichoman.
 66.1.11. Eahtoþe is þæs stanes mægen þæt nan
nædran cynnes bite þam sceþþan ne mæg þe þone stan on wætan
byrigþ.
 67.1.1. Pund eles gewihð <foreign>XII</foreign> penegum læsse þonne pund
wætres.
 67.1.1. & pund ealoð gewihð <foreign>VI</foreign> penegum mare þonne pund
wætres.
 67.1.2. & <foreign>I</foreign> pund wines geþihð <foreign>XV</foreign> penegum mare þonne
<foreign>I</foreign> pund wætres.
 67.1.3. & pund huniges gewihð <foreign>XXXIIII</foreign> penegum mare þonne
pund wætres.
 67.1.4. & <foreign>I</foreign> pund buteran gewihð <foreign>LXXX</foreign> penegum læsse
þonne pund wætres.
 67.1.5. & pund beores gewihð <foreign>XXII</foreign> penegum læsse þonne
pund wætres.
 67.1.5. & <foreign>I</foreign> pund melowes gewihð <foreign>CXV</foreign> penegum læsse

 67.1.6. & <foreign>I</foreign> pund beana gewihð <foreign>lV</foreign> penegum læsse þonne

 67.1.7. & <foreign>XV</foreign> pund wætres gaþ to sestre.

 1. Wiþ heafod ece & wiþ ealdum heafod ece & wiþ
healfes heafdes ece.
 2. Wiþ aswollenum eagum & god eah sealf & wið miste on
eagan & wið flie & wið wyrmum on eagum & wiþ þæm gif
flæsc on eagum weaxe & gis on eagum weaxan reade sponge & gif eagan
tyren & sceade sealf to eagum & smeþe eah sealf.
 3. Wiþ earwærce & wiþ þæm gif wyrmas syn on earan
& god ear sealf.
 4. Wiþ toþ ece & gif teþ syn hole.
 5. Wiþ innan tobrocenum muðe.
 6. Wiþ ceocadle & wiþ ceolwærce.
 7. Wiþ heals wærce.
 8. Wiþ bite.
 9. Wiþ hwostan.
 10. Wiþ þam þe mon blode hræce.
 11. Wiþ seondum geallan.
 12. Wiþ þære geolwan adle.
 13. Wiþ breost wærce.
 14. Wiþ hwostan & wiþ lungenadle.
 15. Wiþ magan wærce & wiþ aþundenesse.
 16. Wið milt wærce.
 17. Wiþ linden wærce.
 18. Wiþ wambe wærce & rysel wærce.
 19. Wiþ blædder wærce.
 20. Wiþ þam gif man ne mæge gemigan & þam men þe
stanas weaxan on þære blædran.
 21. Wiþ þam gif men sie se utgang forseten.
 22. Wiþ utsihtadle drenc & briw.
 23. Wiþ þam wyrmum þe beoþ on mannes innoþe.
 24. Wiþ lið wærce.
 25. Wiþ weartum.
 26. Wið þam miclan lice smiring & bæþ & drenc
& briw.
 27. Wiþ singalum þurste untrumra manna.
 28. Wiþ innan fortoge & smæl þearma ece.
 29. Wiþ þam þe man sie mid fyre anum forbærned & wiþ
þam þe man sie mid wætan forbærned & wiþ sunbryne.
 30. Wiþ þeore drenc & eft wiþ þære & sceotendum
wenne & eft beþing wiþ þam gif þeor gewunige on anre stowe.
 31. Wiþ wenne sealf.
 32. Wiþ dolge sealf.
 33. Wiþ þam gif man sie ufan on heafod wund & sie ban
gebrocen & wiþ þam gif sio eaxl upstige & god dolhdrenc & gif
gebrocen ban sie on heafde & of nelle.
 34. Wiþ hundes slite & wiþ þon gif sinwe forcorfene &
wiþ þam gif sinwe sien gescruncene.
 35. Wiþ gongewifran bite.
 36. Wiþ cancre.
 37. Wiþ þam þe wif ne mæge bearn acennan & gif of wife
nelle gan æfter þam beorþre þæt gecyndelic sie & gif of wife
sie dead bearn & wiþ þam gif wif blede to swiþe æfter þam
beorþre.
 38. Wiþ þam þe wifum sie forstanden hira monað gecynd &
wiþ þam gif wife to swiþe offlowe sio monoþ gecynd.
 39. Wiþ smeagea wyrme smiring & anlegen & beþing &
sealf.
 40. Wiþ þam þe man sie monaþseoc.
 41. Wiþ ealle feondes costunga drenc & sealf, wiþ þon
ilcan & hu man scyle gewitseocne man lacnian & hu mon scyle wyrcean
spiwdrenc utyrnendum.
 42. Wiþ þam gif swiþdrenc on men gesittan & he nelle
utgan.
 43. Wiþ attres drence.
 44. Wiþ lusum.
 45. Wiþ þam gif þorn stinge mon on fot oððe hreod &
þonne nelle ofgan.
 46. Wiþ æsmælum & wiþ eallum eagna wærce.
 47. Wiþ lyft adle gif se muþ sie woh oþþe won læcedom
& beþing & bæþ sealf & leah & blodes læs.
 48. Wiþ ficadle drenc & beþing.
 49. Wiþ sculdor wærce & earma.
 50. Wiþ cneowa sare.
 51. Wiþ fota sare.
 52. Wiþ þam gif þu ne mæge blod dolg forwriþan.
 53. Wiþ þam gif meoloc sie gewerd.
 54. Wiþ niht gengean sealf.
 55. Wiþ þam gif men beo sio heafod panne gehlenced.
 56. Wið þam gif men nelle meltan his mete.
 57. Wiþ wif gemædlan.
 58. Wiþ feondes costunga.
 59. Wiþ þeor wenne gif he sie men on cneowe oþþe on oþrum
lime.
 60. Be þam hu mon scyle ear sealfe wyrcean.
 61. Wiþ ælfcynne sealf & wiþ niht gengan & þam
monnum þe deofol mid hæmð.
 62. Wiþ ælfadle læcedom & eft hu mon sceal on þa
wyrte singan ær hi mon nime & eft hu mon sceal þa wyrta don under
weofod & ofer singan & eft tacnu be þam hwæþer hit sie
ælfsogoþa & tacn hu þu ongitan meaht hwæþer hine mon mæg
gelacnian & drencas & gebedu wiþ ælcre feondes costunge.
 63. Tacnu hu þu meaht ongitan hwæþer mon sie on
wæterælfadle & læcedom wiþ þam & gealdor on to singanne
& þæt ilce mon mæg singan on wunda.
 64. Wið deofle liþe drenc & ungemynde & wiþ deofles
costunga.
 65. Wiþ þon gif mon sie gegymed & tacnu hwæþer he
libban mæge.
 66. Drenc wiþ þam gif þeor sie on men.
 67. Wiþ deofle seoce & wiþ deofle.
 68. Wiþ weden heorte leoht drenc.
 69. Wiþ þam gif men sie maga asurod & forþunden &
wiþ magan wærce & gif man biþ aþunden.
 70. Wiþ wambe wærce & wiþ magan wærce & wiþ
wambe heardnesse.
 71. Wiþ springe smiring & sealf.
 72. Wiþ attre drenc & smiring.
 73. Wiþ þære geolwan adle.
 74. Wiþ þam gif innelfe si ute.
 75. Wiþ ælcre innan untrymnesse & wiþ hefignesse &
wiþ hleorblæce.
 76. Be þam hu man scyle halige sealfe wyrcean.

Lch II (3)<extent></extent>
B21.2.1.3.2.
Bald's Leechbook: Cockayne 1864-6, II, 304-58 (Bk III).



 1.1.1. Wiþ þon þe mon on heafod ace genim nioþowearde
wrætte, do on readne wræd, binde þæt heafod mid.
 1.1.2. Wiþ þon ilcan nim senepes sæd & rudan, gegnid on
ele, do on hat wæter, þweah gelome þæt heafod on þam wætre.
 1.1.3. He biþ hal.
 1.1.4. Wiþ ealdum heafod ece genim dweorgedwostlan, wyl on ele
oððe on butran, smire mid þa þunwongan & bufan þam eagum on ufan
þæt heafod, þeah him sie gemynd oncyrred he biþ hal.
 1.1.6. Wiþ swiþe ealdum heafod ece nim sealt & rudan &
ifig crop, cnua ealle to somne, do on hunig & smire mid þa þunwangan
& þone hnifel & ufan þæt heafod.
 1.1.8. To þon ilcan sec lytle stanas on swealwan bridda magan
& heald þæt hie ne hrinan eorþan ne wætre ne oþrum stanum,
beseowa hira <foreign>III</foreign>, on þon þe þu wille do on þone mon þe him
þearf.
 1.1.10. Sie him biþ sona sel.
 1.1.11. Hi beoþ gode wiþ heafodece & wiþ eagwærce
& wiþ feondes costunga & nihtgengan & lenctenadle & maran
& wyrtforbore & malscra & yflum gealdorcræftum.
 1.1.13. Hit sculon beon micle briddas þe þu hie scealt on
findan.
 1.1.14. Gif mon on healf heafod ace gecnua rudan swiþe, do on
strang eced & smire mid þæt heafod ufan rihte.
 1.1.15. Wiþ þon ilcan adelf wegbrædan butan isene ær
sunnan upgange, bind þa moran ymb þæt heafod mid wræte reade
wræde.
 1.1.17. Sona him bið sel.
 2.1.1. Wiþ aswollenum eagum genim cucune hrefn, ado þa eagan of
& eft cucune gebring on wætre & do þa eagan þam men on sweoran
þe him þearf sie.
 2.1.3. He biþ sona hal.
 2.1.3. Wyrc gode eagsealfe, nim celeþonian & bisceopwyrt,
wermod, wudu merce, wudu bindes leaf, do ealra emfela, cnuwa wel, do on hunig
& on win & on æren fæt oððe on cyperen, do twæde þæs
wines & þriddan dæl þæs huniges, do þæt se wæta mæge
furþum ofer yrnan þa wyrta, læt standan <foreign>VII</foreign> niht & wreoh mid
brede, aseoh þurh clænne claþ ðone drenc, do eft on þæt ilce
fæt, nytta swa þe þearf sie.
 2.1.8. Se mon se him gedeþ ymb <foreign>XXX</foreign> nihta foxes gelyndes dæl
on þa eagan, he biþ ece hal.
 2.2.1. Gif mist sie fore eagum nim cildes hlond & huniges tear,
meng tosomne begea emfela, smire mid þa eagan innan.
 2.3.1. Eft, hrefnes geallan & leaxes & eles & feld beon
hunig meng to somne, smire mid þære sealfe innan þa eagan.
 2.4.1. Wiþ flie gebærned, sealt & swegles æppel &
attrum, ealra emfela, gnid to duste & do on þa eagan, þweah leohtlice
mid wylle wætre & smire æfter mid wifes meolce.
 2.5.1. Gif wyrmas sien on eagum scearpa þa bræwas innan, do on
þa scearpan celeþonian seaw.
 2.5.2. Þa wyrmas bioþ deade & þa eagan hale.
 2.5.2. Gif flæsc on eagum weaxe wring wyrmwyrte on þa eagan
oþ þæt him sel sie.
 2.6.1. Gif on eagan weaxen reade sponge drype on hat culfran blod
oþþe swealwan oððe wifes meoluc oþ þæt þa sponge aweg synd.
 2.6.2. Gif eagan tyren nim drige rudan & huniges tear, meng
tosomne, læt standan <foreign>III</foreign> niht, awring þurh þicne clað linenne &
do on þa eagan siþþan.
 2.6.4. Wyrc gode drige scade sealfe, nim swegles æppel &
gebærned sealt & pipor & attrum & hwit cwudu, gegnid to duste,
asift þurh clað, do lytlum on.
 2.6.6. Eft, hwit cwudu & gebærned oster scyl gnid to duste
& nytta swa þe þearf sie, ægþer mæg adon flie of eagan.
 2.6.8. Wyrc smeþe eagsealfe nim buteran, wyl on pannan, afleot
þæt fam of & ahlyttre þa buteran on blede, do eft þæt hluttre
on pannan, gecnua celeþonian & bisceopwyrt, wudu merce, wyl swiþe,
aseoh þurh clað, nytta swa þe þearf sie.
 3.1.1. Wiþ ear wærce genim henne gelyndo & ofter scylle,
sete on gleda, gewyrm hwon & dryp on þa earan, sona beoð hale.
 3.1.2. Eft, celendran seaw & wifes meoluc gewyrm on scylle
& dryp on þa earan.
 3.1.3. Gif wyrmas sien on earan to belenan seaw wearm on þa
wyrmas.
 3.1.4. Hie beoþ deade & feallað of & þa earan hale.
 3.2.1. Eft, wring curmeallan seaw on oþþe marubian oððe
wermod wearmne.
 3.2.2. Sona him bið sel.
 3.2.2. Wyrc gode ear sealfe, genim bares geallan & fearres
& ele, ealra emfela, læt drypan wearm on þæt eare.
 4.1.1. Wiþ toþ ece ceow pipor gelome mid þam toþum.
 4.1.1. Him biþ sona sel.
 4.1.1. Eft, seoð beolenan moran on strangum ecede oþþe on
wine, sete on þone saran toþ & hwilum ceowe mid þy saran toþe, he
bið hal.
 4.1.3. Gif þa teþ synd hole ceow boþenes moran mid ecede on
þa healfe.
 5.1.1. Wiþ innan tobrocenum muðe nim plum treowes leas wyl on
wine & swile mid þone muþ.
 6.1.1. Wið ceocadle nim þone hweorfan þe wif mid spinnað,
bind on his sweoran mid wyllenan þræde & swile innan mid hate gate
meolce.
 6.1.2. Him biþ sel.
 6.1.3. Wiþ ceolwærce adelf ær sunnan upgange wegbrædan,
bind on his sweoran.
 6.1.4. Eft, bærn swealwan to duste & meng wiþ feldbeon
hunig, sele him etan gelome.
 7.1.1. Wiþ healf wærce wyl neoþewearde netelan on oxan
smerwe & on buteran, þonne þone healfwærc smire ða þeoh.
 7.1.2. Gif þa þeoh wærce smire þone heals mid þære
sealfe.
 7.1.3. Eft, wyl niþewearde netelan on ecede, do oxan geallan on
þæt eced & þa wyrte of, smire mid þone heals.
 8.1.1. Wiþ bite wyrc sealfe, nim þas wyrte, safenan & mersc
mealwan & attorlaþan & weoþobend & hwerhwettan & clufwyrt
& sigel hweorfan, hindheoloþan, mucgwyrt, wudufillan, garclifan,
wrætte, lufestice, mageþan, giþcorn, wad, finul, þefanþorn,
selfæte, eoforþrote, cicena mete, dulhrune, wylisc moru, hnutbeames leaf,
næp, gearwe, hofe, hocleaf, alexandre, fica perfica, se fula wermod, sio
greate banwyrt, acleaf, wegbræde, grundeswelge, read clæfre, leahtric,
þufeþistel, taru, hegeclife, clufþung, englisc moru, dynige.
 9.1.1. Wiþ hwostan wyl marubian on wætre godne dæl, geswet
hwon, sele drincan scenc ful.
 9.1.2. Eft, marubian, swiðe wyl on hunige, do hwon buteran on,
sele <foreign>III</foreign> snæda oþþe <foreign>IIII</foreign> etan, on neaht nestig besup scenc fulne mid
wearmes þæs ærran drences.
 10.1.1. Wiþ þon þe mon blode hræce & spiwe genim god
beren mela & hwit sealt, do on ream oþþe gode flete, hrer on blede oþ
þæt hit sie þicce swa þynne briw, sele etan <foreign>VIIII</foreign> snæda <foreign>VIIII</foreign>
morgenas on neaht nestig, do þæs meluwes twæde & þæs sealtes
þriddan dæl, wyrc ælce dæge niwne.
 11.1.1. Wiþ seondum geallan ete rædic & pipor on neaht
nestig & awylled linsæd on meolce supe mid, do þus gelome.
 11.1.2. Him biþ sona sel.
 12.1.1. Wið þære geolwan adle sio cymð of seondum geallan
genim þæs scearpan þistles moran & betonican & attorlaþan hand
fulle & gyþrifan hand fulle & <foreign>VIIII</foreign> snæda nioþowearde
æscþrotan, ofgeot mid strangan beore oþþe mid strangum ealað &
drince gelome, sele him etan gewyrtodne henfugel & gesodenne cawel on godum
broðe, do þus gelome.
 12.1.5. Him biþ sona sel.
 12.2.1. Wyrc godne dustdrenc wiþ þære geolwan adle, nim
merces sæd & finoles sæd, dile sæd, eoforþrotan sæd,
feldmoran sæd, sæþerian sæd, petorsilian sæd, alexandran sæd,
lufestices sæd, betonican sæd, caules sæd, costes sæd, cymenes
sæd & pipores mæst, þara oðerra emfela, gegnid ealle wel to
duste, nim þæs dustes godne cucler fulne, do on strang hluttor eala,
drince scenc fulne on neaht nestig.
 12.2.6. He is god wiþ ælcre liman untrumnesse & wiþ
heafodece & wiþ ungemynde & wiþ eagwærce & wiþ
ungehyrnesse & breostwærce & lungenadle & lendenwærce &
wiþ ælcre feondes costunga.
 12.2.9. Gewyrc þe dust genoh on hærfeste, þonne þu þa
wyrta hæbbe nytta þonne þe þearf sie.
 13.1.1. Wið breostwærce, marubie, nefte, ontre, bisceopwyrt,
wenwyrt, wyl on hunige & buteran, do þæs huniges twæde &
þære buteran þriddan dæl, nytta swa þe þearf sie.
 14.1.1. Wiþ hwostan & lungenadle genim swegles æppel &
swefl & recels, ealra emfela, meng wiþ weaxe, lege on hatne stan, drinc
þurh horn þone rec & ete æfter ealdes spices <foreign>III</foreign> snæda oððe
butran & supe mid fletum.
 14.1.4. Wiþ lungenadle genim betonican & marubian,
agrimonian, wermod, felterre, rude, acrind, gagollan, wyl on wætre, bewyl
þæs wæteres þriddan dæl, to of þa wyrte, drince on morgenne
wearmes scenc fulne, ete <foreign>III</foreign> snæda mid þæs briwes þe heræfter
segþ.
 14.2.1. Wyrc briw wiþ lungenadle, nim betonican & marubian,
wermod, hindheoloþan, wenwyrt nioþoweard, elehtre, elene, rædic,
eoforþrote, feldmore, gecnua ealle swiþe wel & wyl on buteran &
awring þurh clað, scead on þæt wos beren mela, hrer on blede butan
fyre oþ þæt hit sie swa þicce swa briw, ete <foreign>III</foreign> snæda mid þy
drence wearmes.
 14.3.1. Eft, wyl on hunige anum marubian, do hwon beren mela to,
ete on neaht nestig & þonne þu him selle drenc oððe briw, sele him
hatne & læt gerestan þone man æfter tide dæges on þa swiðran
sidan & hafa þone earm aþened.
 15.1.1. Wiþ magan wærce wyl pic on cu meolce, ado þæt pic
of, supe hwon wearm, sona biþ sel.
 15.1.2. Wiþ aþundenesse & gif men nelle myltan his mete
wyl on wætere polleian & leac cersan, sele drincan him, biþ sona sel.
 16.1.1. Wiþ milte wærce cnua grene sealhrinde, seoð on
hunige anum, sele him etan <foreign>III</foreign> snæda on neaht nestig.
 17.1.1. Wiþ lenden wærce marubie, nefte, bogen, em fela ealra,
do on god ealu, wyrc to drence, swet hwon, sele drincan, licge upweard æfter
þon gode hwile.
 19.1.1. Wiþ blædder wærce, wudu merce & leaccerse, wyl
swiþe on ealað, sele drincan & etan gebrædne stær.
 20.1.1. Gif man ne mæge gemigan & him weaxan stanas on
þære blædran wyl sundcorn on ealað & petersilian, sele him
drincan.
 21.1.1. Gif men sie se utgang forseten wyl wermod on surum ealaþ
& do buteran þær.
 21.1.2. To him biþ sona sel gif he hit drincþ.
 22.1.1. Wiþ utsiht adle, <foreign>V</foreign> leafan, hleomoce, curmealle,
elehtre, gecnua þa wyrta & wyl on meolce, sele him drincan wearm on
morgenne & on æfen.
 22.1.3. Wyrc briw to þon ilcan, wudu cunellan, hleomoc, bewyl
þara/ meolce þriddan dæl, þære wyrte of þam meolcum, scead
hwæten mela þær on & ete þone briw cealdne, & supe þa
meoluc.
 22.1.5. Him bið sona sel.
 22.1.5. Gif se briw & se drenc inne gewuniað þu meaht
þone man gelacnian, gif him offleogeð him bið selre þæt þu hine na
ne grete.
 22.1.7. Him biþ his feorhadl getenge.
 23.1.1. Gif wyrmas beoþ on mannes innoðe wyl on buteran grene
rudan, drinc on neaht nestig scenc fulne.
 23.1.2. Hi gewitað ealle aweg mid þy utgange & he bið
sona hal.
 23.2.1. To þon ilcan genim cymenes dust, meng to gate geallan
& fearres, gnid þone nafolan mid ealle.
 23.2.2. Hi gewitaþ niþer of þæm men.
 24.1.1. Wiþ lið wærce sing <foreign>VIIII</foreign> siþum þis gealdor
þær on & þin spatl spiw on, <foreign>Malignus obligauit, angelus curauit,
dominus saluauit</foreign>.
 24.1.2. Him biþ sona sel.
 24.2.1. To þon ilcan genim culfran tord & gate tord, drige
swiðe & gnid to duste, meng wiþ hunig & wiþ butran, smire mid
þa leoþu.
 25.1.1. Wiþ weartum genim hundes micgean & muse blod, meng to
somne, smire mid þa weartan.
 25.1.2. Hi gewitaþ sona aweg.
 26.1.1. Wiþ miclan lice genim nioþowearde elenan & þung
& ompran þa þe swimman wile, ealra emfela, & gecnua wel & wyl
on buteran, do wel sealtes on & smire mid.
 26.1.3. Wyrc bæð wiþ þam miclan lice, elene,
ælfþone, marubie, curmealle, ellentanas & actanas, wyl swiðe on
wætre & beþe on swiðe hatum þæt lic.
 26.1.5. Wyrc drenc wið þam miclan lice, hindhioloþan,
curmeallan, bogen, nefte, agrimonia, betonica, finul, dile, do on god ealo,
sele drincan on dæge <foreign>III</foreign> scencas fulle.
 26.1.7. Wyrc briw wiþ þon ilcan, genim nioþowearde elenan
& eofor þrotan, redic & þa readan netlan nioþowearde, scearfa
smæle & gecnua wel, wyl siþþan on buteran, do clæne ifig taran
þær on gif þu hæbbe & hwon berenes melwes, do on blede mid þam
wyrtum & hrer mid sticcan oþ þæt hit col sie, sele etan on neaht
nestig <foreign>III</foreign> snæda, sele þone briw & þone drenc ær þam
bæþe þy læs hit inslea æfter þam baþe.
 27.1.1. Wiþ singalum þurste untrumra manna nim wermod &
hind hioloþan & gyþrifan, wylle on ealaþ, geswete hwon, sele him
drincan.
 27.1.2. Hit hælþ þone þurst wundorlice.
 28.1.1. Wiþ innan fortoge, smæl þearma ece, genim betonican
& wermod, merce, rædic, finul, gecnua ealle & do on eala, sete
þonne & bewreoh, drinc on neaht nestig scenc fulne.
 29.1.1. Wiþ bryne, gif mon sie mid fyre ane forbærned nim
wudurofan & lilian & hleomoc, wyl on buteran & smire mid.
 29.1.2. Gif mon sie mid wætan forbærned nime elm rinde &
lilian moran, wyl on meolcum, smire mid þriwa on dæg.
 29.1.4. Wiþ sunbryne, merwe ifig twigu wyl on butran, smire mid.
 30.1.1. Wyrc godne ðeor drenc, wermod, bogen, garclifan,
polleian, wenwyrt, þa smalan fel terre, eagwyrt, þeorwyrt, ceaster æsces
<foreign>II</foreign> snæda, elenan <foreign>III</foreign>, commuces <foreign>VIII</foreign>, wuduweaxan godne dæl,
curmeallan, gescearfa þas wyrta on god hluttor eala oþþe wylisc ealu,
læt standan <foreign>III</foreign> niht bewrigen, sele drincan scenc fulne tide ær oþrum
mete.
 30.1.5. Wiþ þeore & wiþ sceotendum wenne nim bogen &
gearwan & wudu weax & hrefnes fot, do on god ealu, sele drincan on
dæge <foreign>III</foreign> scencas fulle.
 30.1.7. Gif þeor gewunige on anre stowe wyrc beþinge, nim
þæt ifig þe on stane weaxe & gearwan & wudu bindes leaf &
cuslyppan, gecnua ealle wel, lege on hatne stan on troge, geot hwon wæteres
on, læt reocan on þæt lic þær þær him þearf sie, þonne se
col sie do oþerne hatne on, beþe swa gelome.
 30.1.11. Him biþ sona sel.
 31.1.1. Wyrc gode wensealfe, nim wudu merce & hrefnes fot &
wermod nioþoweardne, cu slyppan, rudan, wudu, bindes leaf, ifig leaf þe on
eorþan wixþ, þa clufihtan wenwyrt, gecnua ealle, wyl on rammes smerwe
oþþe on buccan, do þriddan dæl buteran, awring þurh claþ, do
þonne godne scip taran to & hrer oþ þæt hit col sie.
 32.1.1. Wyrc gode dolh sealfe, nim gearwan & wudu rofan
nioþowearde, feld moran, & nioþoweardne sigelhweorfan, wyl on godre
buteran, awring þurh clað & læt gestandan.
 32.1.3. Wel ælc dolh þu meaht lacnian mid.
 33.1.1. Gif mon sie ufan on heafod wund & sie ban gebrocen nim
sigelhweorfan & hwite clæfran wisan & wudurofan, do on gode butran,
aseoh þurh clað & lacna siþþan.
 33.2.1. Gif sio eaxl upstige nim þa sealfe, do hwon wearme mid
feþere.
 33.2.1. Him bið sona sel.
 33.2.2. Wyrc godne dolhdrenc, nim agrimonian & wudu rofan, do
on god ealo, sele drincan godne scenc fulne on neaht nestig.
 33.2.3. Gif gebrocen ban sie on heafde & of nelle cnua grene
betonican & lege on þæt dolh gelome oþ þæt þa ban of syn
& þæt dolh gebatod.
 34.1.1. Wiþ hundes slite cnuwa ribban, lege on þæt dolh
& rudan wyl on butran, lacna mid þæt dolh.
 34.1.2. Gif sinwe syn forcorfene nim renwyrmas, gecnuwa wel, lege
on oþ þæt hi hale synd.
 34.1.3. Gif sinwe sien gescruncene nime æmettan mid hiora
bedgeride, wyl on wætre & beþe mid & rece þa sinwe geornlice.
 35.1.1. Wiþ gongewifran bite nim henne æg, gnid on ealu hreaw
& sceapes tord niwe swa he nyte, sele him drincan godne scenc fulne.
 36.1.1. Wiþ cancre nim gate geallan & hunig, meng to somne
begea emfela, do on þæt dolh.
 36.1.2. To þon ilcan, niwe hundes heafod bærn to ahsan, do on
dolh.
 36.1.3. Gif hit nelle þæt nim monnes drogan, drig swiðe,
gnid to duste, do on.
 36.1.4. Gif þu mid þys ne meaht gelacnian ne meaht þu him
æfre nahte.
 37.1.1. Wiþ þon þe wif ne mæge bearn acenuan nim feld
moran nioþowearde, wyl on meolcum & on wætre, do begea emfela, sele
etan þa moran & þæt wos supan.
 37.1.3. To þon ilcan bind on þæt winstre þeoh up wið
þæt cennende lim nioþowearde beolonan oþþe <foreign>XII</foreign> corn cellendran
sædes & þæt sceal don cniht oððe mæden.
 37.1.5. Swa þæt bearn sie acenned do þa wyrta aweg þy
læs þæt innelfe utsige.
 37.1.6. Gif of wife nelle gan æfter þam beorþre þæt
gecyndelic sie seoþe eald spic on wætre, beþe mid þone cwiþ oððe
hleomoc oþþe hocces leaf wyl on ealoþ, sele drincan hit hat.
 37.1.8. Gif on wife sie dead bearn wyl on meolce & on wætre
hleomoc & polleian, sele drincan on dæg tuwa.
 37.1.9. Georne is to wyrnanne bearneacnum wife þæt hio aht
sealtes ete oððe swetes oþþe beor drince ne swines flæsc ete ne naht
fætes ne druncen gedrince ne on weg ne fere ne on horse to swiðe ride þy
læs þæt bearn of hire sie ær riht tide.
 37.1.13. Gif hio blede to swiþe æfter þam beorþre
nioþowearde clatan wyl on meolce, sele etan & supan þæt wos.
 38.1.1. Wiþ þon þe wifum sie forstanden hira monaþ gecynd
wyl on ealað hleomoc & twa curmeallan, sele drincan & beþe þæt
wif on hatum baþe & drince þone drenc on þam baþe.
 38.1.3. Hafa þe ær geworht clam of beor dræstan & of

nioþoweardne þonne hio of þam baðe gæþ & drince scenc fulne

 38.1.7. & bewreoh þæt wif wel & læt beon swa
beclæmed lange tide þæs dæges, do swa tuwa swa þriwa swæþer
þu scyle.
 38.1.8. Þu scealt simle þam wife bæþ wyrcean & drenc
sellan on þa ilcan tid þe hire sio gecynd æt wære.
 38.1.9. Ahsa þæs æt þam wife.

under þæt hrægl þæt se mon swæte swiþe.
 39.1.1. Wið smeawyrme smiring, nim swines geallan & fisces

 39.1.4. Wyrc beþinge to þon ilcan, nim æpsrinde &

 39.2.1. Wyrc þa blacan sealfe gif þe þearf sie, gesamna þe

 40.1.1. Wiþ þon þe mon sie monaþ seoc nim mere swines fel,

 41.1.1. Wyrc godne drenc wiþ eallum feondes costungum, nim

Med 2 (Torkar)
B21.2.3.
Medical recipes from British Library MS. Addit. 43703, fol. 261r.18-262r.1, 262r.2-5, 15-17, 17-24: Torkar 1976, 330-38.



 1. Wiþ utsyhte.
 2. Nim galluc niþeweardne, gewyl in þeorfum meolcum, supe
gemet hat.
 4. Nim swegle æppel, do in meolc, sele drincan.
 5. Nim nioþewerde liðwyrt grene, wel in beore oþþe in
þeorfum meolcum, supe þæt and drince swiþe.
 7. Wiþ utsyhte.
 8. Nim gesodene haran, ete wiþ þon.
 9. Wiþ utsyhte.
 10. Nim rudan, smeorowyrte, wel in ealoð sele drincan.
 11. Gyf utgong forseten sy.
 12. Nim henneægero þone geolocan and lybcorna þryttig and
hwites sealtes godne dæl and wah meolo.
 14. Wyrttruman, meng eal tosomne do in æges scylle, sete on
gleda, do ealoð ænne sopan to supe swa hat.
 16. Gyf utgong forseten sie.
 17. Genim grundeswelgian and ellenrinde berynde utan, wel
þonne/ swiþe in ealoð, asioh þurh clað, nim þonne <foreign>vi</foreign> and <foreign>xxx</foreign>
lybcorna, gnid smæle, do wætes hwon in, geot innon þone drenc, do

Lch II (Fragment)
B21.2.4.
Leechbook Fragment: Cockayne 1864-6, II, 280-88.



 1.1. Wiþ þære healf deadan adle & hwanon seo cume, seo
adl cymð on þa swiðran healfe þæs lichoman oððe on þa wynstran
þær þa sina toslupað & beoð mid slipigre & þiccere
wætan yfelre & yfelre, þiccere & mycelre.
 2.1. Þa wætan man scæl mid blodlæsum & drencum &
læcedomum on weg adon.
 2.2. Þonne seo adl cume ærest on ðone mannan þonne ontyne
þu his muð, sceawa his tungan, þonne bið heo on þa healfe hwittre
þe seo adl on beon wile.
 2.4. Lacna hine þonne þus, gefere þæne mannan on swiðe
fæstne cleofan & wearmne, gereste him swiðe wel hleowe þær &
wearme gleda bere man gelome inn.
 3.1. Onwreoh hine þonne & sceawa his handa georne & swa
hwæþere swa ðu cealde finde læt him sona blod on þære cealdan
ædre.
 3.2. Æfter þære blodlæse huhwega ymb <foreign>III</foreign> niht sele him
wyrt drenc utyrnende, do giðcorna swa feala swa læcas witon þæt to
wyrtdrence sculon & swa gerade wyrta.
 4.1. Hwilum alwan æfter hire rihte him mon scæl sellan,
hwilum scamoniam, hwilum eft æfter wyrtdrencum.
 4.2. Þonne he gerest sy læt eft blod on ædre swa þu on
fruman dydest, hwilum þu teoh mid glæse oððe mid horne blod of þam
saran stowum adeadodum.
 5.1. Wiþ þære healfdeadan adle, beþe hwilum þa saran
stowe æt heorðe oððe be gledum & smere mid ele & mid halwendum
sealfum & gnid swyðe þæt þa sealfa in besincen.
 5.3. Wyrc to sealfe ealdne rysle sealtne, heortes mearh, gose rysle
oððe hænna & do gode wyrta, to beðe þa saran stowe æt fyre.
 6.1. Hwilum onlege & onbind pic & weax, pipor & smeru
& ele togædere gemilted.
 6.2. Hwilum on þa saran sinua & aswollenan lege on & bind
on gate tyrdelu gemenged wið hunig oððe on ecede gesoden.
 6.3. Þonne þwinað þa aslapenan & þa aswollena sina.
 7.1. Wyrc him wyrt drenc þe ne bið utyrnende ne spiwol ac
todrifð & lytlað þa yfelan wætan on þam seocum men þe biþ
swa swa horh oððe risoda oððe gillistre.
 8.1. Genim huniges þis lytle pund, do þonne to þan gebeaten
& asift pipor, syle þonne to þicganne þam untruma men.
 8.2. Eft, ymbe þreo niht syle him on þam ilcan gemete oððe
mare & swa ymb feower niht.
 9.1. Wið þære healf deadan adle do þu hwilum sealtes
cucler mæl to, menge wið hunig & eft pipor.
 9.2. Cunna swa ægþer ge on þisum læcedome ge on oðrum
þæm þe ic eac write hu hit on niman wolde.
 9.3. Gif þæt lic heard si utan lege on þane læcedom þe
þæt heard forði hwelige & þæt yfel ut teo.
 9.4. Teoh him blod of gif þæt neb oððe þæt heafod sar
si on þam hnescan & nytta þara læcedoma þe þane horh of þam
heafde teo oþþe þurh muð oððe þurh nosu.
 9.7. & þonne he þa miht hæbbe gedo þæt he gelome
gefnese.
 9.7. Syle him þa mettas þe syn eaðmylte & god seaw
hæbben & he fram þam mettum mæge smaligan.
 9.9. Þæt syn gesodene wyrta, wyll, geote man þæt
æreste wos & þæt aftere onweg, do þonne god wos to & syle to
þycganne, do lytel sealt & ele & merce to & porr & þæm
gelice.
 9.11. Heald þonne georne þæt se mete si gemylt ær he him
eft gyfe forðan þe se ungemylta mete him wyrcð mycel yfel.
 9.13. Scires wines drince æthwæga, gif he ma wille drince hat
wæter.
 9.14. Healde hine georne wið bæþ & hwilum þonne he hit
geþrowian mæge læte him blod on innan earme & scearpige þa
scancan, æþele læcedom.
 9.15. & hu seo healf deade adl ær feowertigum oððe
fiftigum wintra næfre on men ne becume.
 10.1. Sume bec lærað wið þære healfdeadan adle þæt
man pintreow bærne to gledum & þonne þa gleda sette toforan þam
seocum men & þæt he þonne ontyndum eagum & opene muþe þane
rec swelge þa þrage þe he mæge & þonne he ma ne mæge onwende
his neb aweg lythwon & eft wende to & onfo ðam steme.
 10.4. & swa do ælce dæge oð þæt se dæl þæs
lichoman þe þær adeadod wæs & gelewed to þære ærran
hælo becume.
 11.1. Soðlice seo adl cymð on monnan æfter feowertigum
oððe fiftigum wintra.
 11.2. Gif he bið cealdre gecyndo þonne cymð æfter
feowertigum, elcor cymð æfter fiftigum wintra his gærgetales.
 11.3. Gif hit gingran men gelimpe þonne bið þæt
eaðlæcnere & ne bið seo ylce adl þeah þe ungleawe læcas wenan
þæt þæt seo ylce healfdeade adl si.
 11.5. Hu gelic adl on man becume on geogoðe on sumum lime swa swa
seo healfdeade adl on yldo deð?
 11.6. Ne bið hit seo healfdeade adl ac hwilc æthwega yfel
wæte bið gegoten on þæt lim þe hit on gesit ac bið
eaðlæcnere ac seo soðe healfdeade adl cymð æfter fiftigum wintra.
 12.1. Gif mon sy þære healfdædan adle seoc oððe bræc
seoc wyrc him oxumelli, suðerne eceddrenc ecedes & huniges &
wæteres gemang.
 13.1. Nim ecedes anne dæl, huniges twegen dælas wel
geclæsnodes, wæteres feorðan, seoð þonne oð þæt þriddan
dæl þære wætan oððe feorðan & fleot þæt fam &
þæt rot symle of oðþæt hit gesoden si.
 13.3. Gif þu wille þone drenc strengran wyrcan þonne do þu
swa mycel þæs ecedes swa þæs huniges & nytta þæs
læcedomas ge wið þisse adle ge wið ælcere ful neah.
 13.5. Nim simble þæs eceddrences swa geworhtes swa mycel swa
þe þince.
 13.6. Do wið þissum adlum rædic on þæt seaw þæs
drinces, læt beo nihterne on, syle þonne on morgenne þam seocum men
neahtnestigum þane rædic swa geseawne to þicganne swa he swyðust
mæge & þæt þu þanne læfe þæs seawes syððan se
rædic ofe sy geot hat wæter on, syle drincan þam seocum men to fylle.
 13.10. And þonne ymbe anes dæges hwile stinge him mon feþere
on muð oððe finger, nede hine to spiwanne.
 13.12. Nim, eft, eles anne dæl, wearmes wæteres twegan,
sealtes twegan cuceles fulle, meng togædere, syle to drincanne ceac fulne
& þanne stinge finger on muð, bæde to spiwanne, læt þanne
spiwan on þane ylcan ceac þe he ær of dranc, gesceawa þonne
hwæðer þe spiwða sy swa micel swa he ær gedranc.
 13.16. Gif he mara sy tyla his swa, gif he emmicel si þane þe
he ær gedranc syle eft on ða ilcan wisan oðþæt he ma spiwe þanne
he gedrince ær.
 13.17. Þis sceal swiþust wið blædran adle & þæm
stanum þe on blæddran syn.
 14.1. Wið þære healfdeadan adle nim þæt wæter þe
pyosan ræran on gesodene, ofer willeda, syle drincan.
 14.2. Swiðe þonne wecð þæt þone innoð &
clænsað.
 14.3. Eft, synfullan leaf on win gegniden, þæt clænsað
þane innað.
 14.3. Wiþ þan ilcan eft, ellenes blosman genim & gegnid
& gemenge wið hunig & gedo on box & þonne þearf si genim
bollan fulne hluttres geswettes wines, gemenge wið þæt & aseohhe,
syle drincan.
 14.6. Wið þan ilcan, betan mid hire wyrtruman seoð on
wætere butan sealte, syle þonne þæs wæteres bollan fulne to
gedrincanne.

Med 3 (Grattan-Singer)
B21.3.
Lacnunga: Grattan and Singer 1952, 96-130, 146-204.



 1.1. Wið heafodwræce, genim hamorwyrt & efenlastan
nyðowearde, cnuca, lege on clað, gnid in wæter, gnid swiðe þæt
heo sy eall geleðred, þweah mid þy leaðre þæt heafod gelome.
 2.1. Wið heafodwræce, hindhæleða & grundeswylgean
& fæncyrsan & giðrifan wyl in wætere, læt reocan in þa
eagan þa hwile hy hate synd, & ymb ða eagan gnid mid þam wyrtum swa
hatum.
 3.1. Wið heafodwærce, betan wyrtruman, cnuca mid hunige,
awring, do þæt seaw on þæt neb, gelicge upweard wið hatre sunnan,
& ahoh þæt heafod nyþerweard oððæt seo ex sy gesoht, hæbbe
him ær on muðe buteran oððe ele, asitte þonne uplang, hnige þonne
forð, læte flowan of þæn nebbe þa gilstre, do þæt gelome
oððæt hyt clæne sy.
 4.1. To heafodsealfe & to ehsealfe, aluwan, gegnid in eced,
smyre þæt heafod mid & in þa eagan do.
 5.1. Eahsealf, win & piper, do in horn, & in þa eagan
þonne þu ðe restan wille.
 6.1. Eahsealf, genim streawberian nyþewearde & pipor, do in
clað, bebind, lege on gesweted win, drype of þan claðe ænne dropan in
ægðer eage.
 7.1. Gif eagan forsetene beoð, genim hræfnes geallan &
hwitmæringc, wudulehtric & leaxes geallan, do tosomne, dryp on þæt
eage þurh linhæwenne clað & gehwæde arodes woses, þonne wacað
þæt eage.
 8.1. Þis is seo seleste eahsealf, nim doran hunig & foxes
smero & rahdeores mearh, mæng tosomne.
 9.1. Gif poc sy on eagan, nim mærcsapan & hinde meolc,
mæng tosomne & & swingc, læt standan oð hit sy hluttor, nim
þonne þæt hluttre, do on ða eagan, mid godes fultume he sceal aweg.
 10.1. Þis is seo æðeleste eahsealf, wið eahwyrce &
wið miste, & wið wænne, & wið weormum, & wið gicðan,
& wið tyrendum eagan, & wið ælcum uncuðum geswelle, genim
feferfugian blosman & ðunorclæfran blosman & dyles blosman &
hamorwyrte blosman & twegra cynna wyrmod & pollegian &
neoðowearde lilian & hæwene hnydelan & lufestice & dolhrunan,
& geporta ða wyrta tosomne, & awyll on heortes mearge oððe on his
smerwe, & menge, do ðonne on tela micel in ða eagan & smere utan
& wyrm to fyre, & ðeos sealf deah wið æghwylcum geswelle to
ðicganne & to smergenne, on swa hwylcum lime swa hit on bið.
 11.1. Wið hwostan, nim huniges tear & merces sæd &
diles sæd, cnuca þa sæd smale, mæng ðicce wið ðone tear,
& pipera swiðe, nim ðry sticcan fulle on nihtnihstig.
 12.1. Wið eagena dymnesse, nim wulfes camb neoðeweardne &
lege on hunig ðreo niht, nim þonne & wipa þæt hunig of, cnuca
þonne an sticce ðære wyrte, wring þonne ðurh linhæwenne clað
on þæt eage.
 13.1. Gif eagan tyran, genim grene rudan, cnuca smale & wes mid
doran hunige oððe mid dunhunige, wring þurh linenne clað on þæt
eage swa lange swa him ðearf sy.
 14.1. Se man se ðe biþ on healsoman, nime healswyrt &
wudamerce & wudafillan, & streawbergean wisan, & eoforþrotan
& garclifan, & isenheardan butan ælcan isene genumen, &
æðelferðþincwyrt & cneowholen & bradbisceopwyrt &
brunwyrt, gesomnige ealle þas wyrta togædere þrim nihtan ær sumor on
tun ga, ælcre efenmicel, & gewyrce to drænce on wyliscan ealaþ,
& þonne on niht þonne sumor on tun gæð on mergen, þonne sceal
se man wacyan ealle þa niht, þe ðone drenc drincan wile, & þonne
coccas crawan forman syðe þonne drince he æne, oþre siðe þonne
dæg & niht scade, þriddan siðe þonne sunne upga, & reste hine
syþþan.
 15.1. Þis is seo grene sealf, betonica, rude, lufestice, finol,
saluie, æðelferþincwyrt, sauine, helde, galluces moran, slarige, merce,
cearfille, hræmnes fot, mugwyrt, organa, melde, quinquefolium, ualeriane,
clate, medewyrt, dweorgedwoslan, pipeneale, solsequium, biscupwyrt, hæsel,
quice, hegecliue, grundeswylie, brocminte & oþre mintan, cicena mete,
gagel, hegehymele, cost, eorðnafala, hnutbeames leaf, lauberge, cymen, ele,
weax.
 16.1. Wið adle, nim þreo leaf gageles on gewylledre mealtre
meolce, syle þry morhgenas drincan.
 17.1. Wið heafodece, rude & dweorgedwosle & betan more
& wuduroue, nim ealra euenmicel swa ðu mæge mid þinan scitefingre to
þinum ðuman befon, cnuca hy smale, & mylt buteran & do of eall
þæt fule & do on clæne pannan, & awyl ða wyrta þæron
wel, & wring ðurh clað, do ele to, gif ðu begytan mæge, &
smyre his heafod mid, þær hit acy.
 18.1. Sealf wið fleogendum attre & færspryngum, nim
hamorwyrte handfulle & mægeðan handfulle & wegbrædan handfulle,
& eadoccan moran, sece ða þe fleotan wille, þære ðeah læst,
& clænes huniges ane ægscylle fulle, nim þonne clæne buteran,
þrywa gemylte ðe þa sealfe midweorcean wile, singe man ane mæssan ofer
ðam wyrtum ær man hy tosomne do & þa sealfe wyrce.
 19.1. Wið ðone bledendan fic, nim murran ða wyrt, &
ceorf/ of nygan penegas & do on ælcne hunig, & ðige ða on
æfen, & eft oðre nygan on mergen, & do swa nigon dagas & <foreign>IX</foreign>
niht butan ðe raðor bot cume.
 21.1. Cardiacus hatte seo adl ðe man swiðe swæteð on, on
hy man sceal wyrcean utyrnende drænceas & him wyrcean cliðan toforan
his heafde & to his breostan, genim grene rudan leaf, scearfa smale &
cnuca swiðe, & beren meala gesyft do ðærto, & swetedne eced,
wyrc to cliðan & do on þicne clað & bind on þreo niht &
þry dagas, do eft niwne to, & drince seoca of bræmelberian gewrungene
oft.
 22.1. Sing ðis wið toðece, syððan sunne beo on setle,
swiðe oft, <foreign>caio laio quaque uoaque ofer sæloficia</foreign> sleah manna wyrm,
nemne her þone man & his fæder, cweð þonne, <foreign>lilumenne</foreign> æceð
þæt ofer eall þonne alið, colað þonne hit on eorðan hatost
byrneð, <foreign>finit, amen</foreign>.
 23.1. Wið ðone dropan, iue & fifleafe, nædderwyrt &
hlædderwyrt & eorðgeallan, wyrc ðas wyrta on hærfeste &
scearfa/ hy smale & drige hy, & heald hy ofer winter, & nytta hy
þonne ðe ðearf sy, wylle hy on ealað.
 24.1. Wið geswel, genim lilian moran & ellenes spryttinge
& porleaces leaf, & scearfa swiðe smale & cnuca swiðe, & do
on ðicne clað, & bind on.
 25.1. Sing ðis gebed on ða blacan blegene <foreign>IX</foreign> syðan,
ærest pater noster, <foreign>Tigað tigað tigað calicet aclu cluel sedes
adclocles acre earcre arnem nonabiuð ær ærnem niðren arcum cunað
arcum arctua fligara uflen binchi cutern nicuparam raf afð egal uflen arta
arta arta trauncula trauncula, querite et inuenietis, adiuro te per patrem et

gedrince, gyt hyt sy wæpnedcynnes sing ðis leoð in þæt swiðre
eare þe her æfter awriten is, gif hit sy wifcynnes sing in þæt
wynstre eare, <foreign>Gonomil orgomil marbumil marbsai ramum tofeð tengo docuillo
biran cuiðær cæfmiil scuiht cuillo scuiht cuib duill marbsiramum</foreign>.
 26.5. Sing nygon siðan in þæt eare þis galdor & pater
noster æne.
 27.1. Þis ylce galdor mæg mon singan wið smeogan wyrme, sing
gelome on þa dolh, & mid ðinan spatle smyre, & genim grene
curmeallan, cnuca, lege on þæt dolh, & beðe mid hattre cumicgan.
 28.1. Wið ðon ðe mon attor gedrince, nim marubian sæd,
mængc wið wine, syle drincan.
 29.1. Þis is se halga drænc wið ælfsidene & wið
eallum feondes costungum, writ on husldisce, <foreign>In principio erat uerbum usque
non conprehenderunt, et plura et circumibat iesus totam galileam docens usque

 29.5. Nim cristallan & disman & sidewaran & cassuc
& finol, & nim sester fulne gehalgodes wines, & hat unmælne mon
gefeccean swigende ongean streame healfne sester yrnendes wæteres, nim
þonne & lege ða wyrta ealle in þæt wæter & þweah þæt
gewrit of ðan husldisce þærin swiðe clæne, geot þonne þæt
gehalgade win ufon on ðæt oþer.
 29.10. Ber þonne to ciricean, læt singan mæssan ofer, ane
<foreign>omnibus sanctis</foreign> oðre <foreign>Contra tribulatione</foreign>, þriddan <foreign>sanctam marian</foreign>,
sing ðas gebedsealmas, <foreign>Miserere mei deus, Deus in nomine tuo, Deus

ælmihtiges drihtnes naman & cweð, <foreign>in nomine patris et filii et
spiritus sancti sit benedictum</foreign>, bruc syþþan.
 30.1. To wensealfe, Nim elenan & rædic, cyrfillan &
hræmnes fot, ængliscne næp & finul & saluian &
suþernewuda & cnuca tosomne, & nim garleaces godne dæl, cnuca,
& wring, þurh clað on gemered hunig, þonne hit swiðe gesoden sy,
þonne do ðu pipor & sidewaran, gallengar & gingifre & rinde
& lawerbergean & pyretran, godne dæl ælces be ðære
mæðe, & syððan hit swa gemænged þara wyrta wos & þæt
hunig, þonne seoð ðu hit twa swa swiðe swa hit ær wæs, þonne
hæfst/ þu gode sealfe wið wennas & wið nyrwet.
 31.1. To godre bansealfe þe mæg wið heafodece & wið
ealra lyma tyddernysse, sceal rude, rædic & ampre, uane, feuerfuge,
æscðrote, eofoðrote, cilðenige, bete & betonican, ribbe &

lambes cerse, hylwyrt, hæsel, cwice, wudurofe & wrættes cið,

nim ealra ðyssa wyrta efenfela, do on mortere, cnuca eall tosomne & do
ðærto ifigcroppas.
 31.8. & nim æscrinde & weliges twiga & acrinde &
wirrinde & surre apoldrerinde & seales rinde & wudubindan leaf,
þas ealle sculan beon genumene on neoðoweardan & on easteweardan þan
treowan, scearfige ealle ðas rinda togædere & wylle on haligwætere
oððæt hy wel hnexian, do þonne to þan wyrtum on mortere, cnuca eall
tosomne.
 31.12. Nim þonne heortes smera & hæferes smera & eald
morod & fearres smeru & bares smeru & rammes smeru, mylte mon ealle
tosomne & geote to trindan, somnige mon þonne ealle þa ban tosomne ðe
man ge gaderian mæge, & cnocie man þa ban mid æxse yre &
seoðe & fleote þæt smeru, wyrce to trindan, nime þonne ealde
buteran & wylle þa wyrta & þa rinda, don eall tosomne, þonne hit
beo æne awylled sette þonne, scearfa þonne eall þæt smera on pannan
swa micel swa þu sealfe habban wille & þu getyrwan mæge, sete ofer
fyr, læt socian, næs to swiðe weallan, oððaet hyo genoh sy, seoh
ðurh clað, sete eft ofer fyr.
 31.21. Nim þonne nygon clufa garleaces gehalgodes, cnuca on wine,
wring þurh clað, scaf on myrran þa wyrt & fanthalig wex &
brynestor/ & hwitne rycels, geot þonne innan ða sealfe, swa micel

oxsan mearh & earnes mearh, do þonne ða tyrwan, ond mæng þonne mid
cwicbeamenum sticcan oð heo brun sy.
 31.26. Sing þonne þærofer, <foreign>Benedictus dominus deus meus</foreign>
& þone oþerne <foreign>benedictus dominus deus israel, & mangnificað,
& credo in unum</foreign>, & þæt gebed, matheus, marcus, lucas, iohannes,
sy þæt sar þær hit sy, smite mon ða sealfe ærest on þæt
heafod.
 32.1. Gif poc sy on eagan, nim mearhsapan & hinde meoluc,
mæng tosomne & swyng, læt standan oð hit sy hluttor, nim þonne
þæt hlutre, do on ða eagan, mid godes fultume heo sceal aweg.
 32.3. Nim clatan moran, cnuca swiðe & wyl on beore, syle
drincan wel wearm þonne ðu geseo þæt hy utslean, mid godes fultume ne
wyrð him nan orne.
 33.1. Þas wyrte sculon to lungensealfe, banwyrt & brunwyrt,
betonican & streawberian wise, suþernewuda & isopo, saluie &
sauine & rude, garclife & hæsel, cwice, medewyrt, dolhrune.
 34.1. Wið heafodece, wyl in wætere pollegian & leac,

 35.1. Wið hreofum lice, adelf ampron & gelodwyrt, teon ut

Lch III (Foetus)
B21.4.
On the Human Foetus: Cockayne 1864-6, III, 146.



 1. Her onginð secgan ymbe mannes gecynde hu he on his modor
innoþe to men gewyrðeð.
 2. Ærest þæs mannes brægen bið geworden on his moder
innoþe, þonne bið þæt brægen utan mid reaman bewefen on þære
syxtan wucan.
 5. On oðrum monþe þa ædron beoð geworden, on <foreign>lxv</foreign> &
þreo hundræd scytran & lengran hi beoð todælede & þæt
blod þonne floweð on þa fet & uppan þa handa & he þonne byþ
on limum todæled & to somne gearwað.
 9. On þam þriddum monþe he biþ man butan sawle.
 10. On þam feorþan monþe he bið on limum staþolfæst.
 11. On þam fiftan monþe he biþ cwica & weaxeð & seo
modur lið witleas & þonne þa ribb beoð geworden, þonne gelimpð
þæræ manigfeald sar þonne þæs byrþres lic on hire innoþe
scypigende bið.
 15. On þam syxtan monþe he byþ gehyd & ban beoð
weaxende.
 16. On þam seofoþan monþe þa tan & þa fingras beoð
weaxende.
 17. On þam eahtoþan monþe him beoð þa breost þing
wexende & heorte & blod & he bið eall staþolfæstlice
geseted.
 19. On þam nigoþan monþe witodlice wifum bið cuð
hwæþer hi cennan magon.

 1.1. Ðis is seo seleste eahsalf wið ehwærce & wið

 8.1. Wið innoþes astyrunge.

Med 5.10 (Schauman-Cameron)
B21.5.10.
Recipes: Schauman and Cameron 1977, 291-3.



 1. Wið yflum & miclum footsuilun.
 1. Cnua beolonan moran suiðe, lege on ða foet.
 2. Hie geðuinað & alne ðone ece wunderlice afirrað.
 3. Eft to ðon ilcan.
 3. Genim ðære læssan mucgwyrte moran, cnua wel, gemæng
suæ calde wið hunig, ete ðæt gemong on marne & ðonne he restan
welle.
 6. Ðæs ilcan lecedom mæg wið ðeh wærce.
 7. Gif foet oððo sconcan oððo cnio suellen, genim
neodowarde beolonan oððo eolectran, gecnua suiðe wið smæng wið
maelum hwæte meolwe gecneed to dage.
 9. Clæn on ðet asuoln limm, wrið on næhterne.
 10. On mærne bið se suile geðuinen sio duæning dæg
ðaeh ðe hio on neate sie.
 11. Wyrc god dust to rotigendum dolge, nim acrinde &
slahðornes wyrtruman rinde.
 13. Innewarde adryg wyrt to duste.
 13. Ðæt bið god In dolg to scædenne.
 14. Ðis dust is good to scedenne gif men foet suellen & ða
tan cinen.
 15. Ne wæt ða ðu foet, & hie sie stille ðendon ðu
hine lecnige.
 17. Wið foetadle, wyrc scoas of seles felle, do on ða foet
& hiæ biað sona soel.
 18. To ðon ilcan.
 18. Wið lend wærce, wyrc gyrdels of seles felle, gyrd mið
& he bið hal.
 19. Wið ðeh æci, wyrc drenc, nim eofordrotan walwyrt.
 20. Do in win oððo in god waelc alo, drinc on næhtnistig
bollan fulle.
 22. Wyrc him aec god bæð eapuldorn, salhðorn, aesc,
cuiicbean, aac, eofordrote, æscðrote, eolone, biscop wyrt, ifign,
betonica, ribbe, rædic.
 24. Waell ðis all in wætre & ðis is god baeð wið
ðeh æci.
 26. Wið aslepnum lic.
 26. Genim neoðowardne seeog, waell in wætre, lege hatne stan
in letrican on ðæt liic ðær hit aslepne sie.
 28. Wyrc him aec gode salfe, genim ða readan netlan &
hræfnes fot.
 29. In suines smeome & scepes & in butran &
scipteorwe.
 30. Mið ða salfe ðæt lic ðær hit alepen sie.
 31. Is oðer god salf to ðon ilcan peopor hwytcudu.
 32. Suefl cost ecid oele.

END_TEXT

PeriD
B21.6.
Peri Didaxeon: Loweneck 1896, 3-53, corrected by Sanborn 1983.



 1.3.2. <foreign>Incipit liber, qui dicitur peri didaxeon</foreign> Her onginþ seo
boc peri didaxeon, þæt ys seo swytelung, hu fela gera wæs behuded se
læcecræft.
 1.3.4. And be his gewitnesse þa gelæredusþan læce
gewislice smeadon.
 1.3.5. Þæt was se ærusta Apollo and his suna Esculapfius
and Asclepius; and Asclepius was Ypocrates yem.
 1.3.7. Þeos IIIIor gemetum ærest þa getymbrunga þare
læcecrafte after Noes flode ymba wintra a þusund and fif hund wintra on
Artaxis dæge, se was Persa cingc; hy aluste þa leoht þæra
læcecræfte.
 1.3.10. Giwislica se Apollon ærest he gemetta meþodicam,
þæt syndon sa ysene, þa mann mid cnifun hæle menn; and Escolafius
empiricam, þæt is ilæcnunga of læcecrafta; and Asclepius loicam,
þæt ys seo gehealdenysse þære æ and þæs lifæs; and Ypocras
theoricam, þæt ys foresceawunga þara seocnesse.
 1.3.16. Þannum Plato and Aristotiles, þa gelæredusþan
aþwytyna, þas æfterfyligdun þan forecwedenan læcum, and hi
gesæddun þæt feower wætun syndon on þan manniscen lichama;
forþam byð wylyd ealswa middangeardes boga, þat ys þa wæte on þan
heafode and þæt blod on þara breosta and se ruwa gealla on þan
innoþe and se swerta gealle innan ðare blædran.
 1.3.22. And hyra anra gehwylce rixaþ ðra monþas: Þæt ys
fram XVIII kl'. ian. usque in VIII kl'. ap'l'., þæt on ðan heafde se
wæte byð wexende; and fram XVIII kl'. ap'l'. usque in VIII kl'. iulii,
þæt ðæt blod biþ wexinde on þan breosten; ab XVIII kl'. iulii
usque in octaua kl'. octobris, þæt sa ruwa gealle byð wexenda on þan
innoþe, forþan synd þa dæges genemnede cinotici, þæt sindan þa
dæges caniculares, and þara byd fif and feowertig dæga; and on þan
dægen/ ne mæg nan læce wel don fultum ænigen seoce manne.
 1.5.3. Anð þe feorðan gescornesse ys ab XVIII kl'. octobris
usque in VIII kl'. Ian., þat se blace gealle wixt on þara bladre.
 1.5.5. Þis gescead ys hæfter þam feorwer heorren heofenes
and eorðan and þara lyfte and þara dupnesse.
 1.5.7. Þa wæs ealswa drihte licede, ealswa was se man geset.
 1.5.8. Þæt þur þara smeagunga and þare endbirnesse.
 1.5.9. Vtan nu nymen æryst gewislice þane fruman of þan
heafde.
 2.5.11. Wið oman; Þus man sceal wyrcen þa sealfe wið oman,
and þus he sceal beon gehaled: Nim litargio twentige scillinga gewyht and
niwes limes twentiga scillinga gewihte and anne healfne sester ecedes and

ætsomne mid þan ecede, and þanne nima man oððer ele and meng

 3.5.19. <foreign>Ad scabiosos</foreign> Wid þæt heafod, þe byð toswollen,
þæt Grecas ulcerosus hatað, þæt is heafodsar, þa bula, þe
betwyx/ felle and flæsce arisað and on mannes anwlytan utbersteþ swa
grete swa beane.
 3.5.23. Þus he scel beon gehaled: Nim wingeardes sæt and gnid
on wæte and lege uppan þar sar, and he byð sona hæl.
 4.5.25. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsona wid þat ylca: Nim swearte beanen and
cnuca hy swiðe smale and bynd hy to þare wunda, and selest heo hit
gehaleð.
 5.5.29. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsona nim mintan and cnuca hy smale and lege
uppan þa wunda, and ealle þa wæten, ðe þarut gað of þan sare,
eall heo hit adrigh, and gehælð þæt sare.
 6.7.1. <foreign>Item</foreign> Eftsona wið þæt ylca, gif þeo ylca adle

 9.7.14. <foreign>De cefalaponia</foreign> Cefalaponia, ðæt ys heafodsar, and

 9.7.16. And þis synda þa tacnu þæs sares.

eal þat heafod byð hefi, and swogað þa earan and þa sinan on þan

 9.7.19. Þis sceal to botan þan sare: Do þane mann innan to
ana huse, þe be no to leoht no to þustre, and begyte man hym rudan, swa
mycel swa he mæge mid hys hand byfon, and eorðiui ealswa micel and

byð sona hæl.
 10.7.25. <foreign>Ad dolorem capitis</foreign> To þan mann, þæt hys heafod
æcþ, oððer wurmas on þan heafedon rixiad: Nim senepsæd and
næpsæd and meng eced and cned hyt mid þam ecede, þæt hit si swa
þicce swa doh, and smyre þæt heafoð foreweard mid; and þis his
anredest/ læcecræft.
 11.9.1. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Wið þæt ylca; Eft nim ladsar, þæt ys

wlacan ecede and nim þanne þa sealfe and geot on þæs seocys mannes
eare and læt hyne liggen swa lange fortþan eara hit habben eal gedruncan,
and he byð wunderlice hraþe hal.
 12.9.7. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eft nim ellenes piþan and ecede and wull eall
togadere and geot þa sealfan in þat eare, gif se wyrme ys þarinnan; sona
he sceal hutgan of þan earen, gif he þarinna hys.
 13.9.11. <foreign>Ad tornionem capitis</foreign> Þis ys se lacecræft be þan
manne, þat hym þingþ, þæt hyt turnge abotan hys heafod and farþ
furwendun brachenum: Nim man rudan and ceruellan and enneleac and cnuca þa
wurtan togadere.
 13.9.15. Nim þanne eale and buteran and ecede and hunig and meng
togadere þa sealfe mid þare wulle, þe ne com næfre awæxan, and do
inna þa sealfen and wæte þa sealfen inne ane panne mid wulle and mid

byð sona bet.
 14.9.21. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsane nim renwæter oððer wullewæter,
þa upwærd wylld and clæne byð; do hyt in an fæt, nim þann anne
linnenne clað and do hine eal wate on þan wætere and bynd hine
syðþan twyfeald uppe þan heafode, of se claþ drige beon, and hym byð
sone bet.
 15.9.27. <foreign>Item</foreign> Eftsona nim balsmeðan and ele and cnuca þane
balsmeþan and menge syððe wið hlutre ele and cnuca; nim þann ane
panne/ and wyrme þa sealfe innan; nim þann þa sealfe swa wearme and
bebind/ þæt heafed mid.
 15.9.31. And nim eftsona plantaginem, þæt ys webrædan, and
cnuca þa wurt togadere, and meng hecede þarto; wyrce syðan anne cliþan
þarof/; nim þann þane clyðan and bynd to þan sare.
 15.11.2. Þanne scealt þu wyrcen ðus þone dreng þarto: Nim
sauinam and ambrotena and cnuca hi and do hi syþþan on win and meng piper
þarto and sum dal huniges and þige þarof anne cuppan felle on ærne
morge and oþerne an niht, þann he gad to bedde.
 16.11.7. <foreign>De capitis purgatione</foreign> Wið þat þæt mannes
heafod clþppitað and to ealre þare clansunge þas heafodes.
 16.11.9. And hit ys nidþearf wið ælc yfel, þæt man
ærest hys heafod clænsige.
 16.11.10. Þæt ys: Nim ærest twegen sestres sapan and twege
hunies and þre sestres ecedes; and se sester sceal wegan twa pund be
sylfyrgewyht; and nin hwytne stor and senep and gingiber, æl þissa twelf
peniga gewihte; and nim rudan ane handfulle and organe ane handfulle and ane
gelare pinahnutte and do eal þys innan anne niwne croccan, and amorgen
þann seoð þu hyt swa swiðe, þat se þriddana dæl beo besodan.
 16.11.17. Nim hit þanne and do in an glæsfat and man machiæ
stufbæþ and baþege hine þaron and smyrige þann þæt heafod mid
þare scealfe.
 17.11.20. <foreign>Ad aures</foreign> Þis sceal to þan earan, þe wind
oþþer wæter forclyst.
 17.11.22. Þus man hy læcnian sceal: Gif þar sy sweg
oþþer sar innan þan heafedan, on fruman do þas scealfe: Nim twegen
styccan fulle godes eles and grene diles twa handfulle and rudan ealswa micel
and wyl on an niwen crocen næs to swiðe, ðe læsse þe ele his
mægn/ forleosen.
 17.11.26. Wryng þann þur linne clæþ and do hyt on an
glæsfæt; wyrme þanne mann þæt heafod and smyre mid þare sealfe,
and he binde þanne þæt heafod mid ane clæþe ane niht; wring þanne
garleyc inne þa eare alche dæg; after þat he byd hæl.
 18.11.31. <foreign>Ad parotidas: Ad parotidas</foreign> þæt ys to ðan sare,
þe abutan sa earan wycst, þæt man nemneð on ure geðeode healsgund.
 18.11.33. And þe healsgund ys twera cunna; and he becum
oþerhwylum/ an man, þur þa awergeda adle, and þam mannan swyðest, se
on sara seocnesse cealdne wætan drincaþ.
 18.13.3. And þa healsgunda syndan twa cunna: Þe oþer byd
eaðe to halene, and þæge non dolh ne wyrces; and oþer syndun, þe
Grecas <foreign>cacote</foreign> hateð, þæt synde awyrgede, and þæge syndan to
agytene ealswa hit her beforen segð, forþan þe færunga hy atyweþ and
færinga aweg gewiteþ buta ælce læcecrafte and swa þeah micele
frecnysse getacnæð, forþan þe hi beoð acennede of þan swertan
wætan, and hy reade atywþ.
 18.13.10. Þus hy man sceal hælen: Nim webradeleaf ar sunne
upgange; nym þanne hlaf and sealt and swamm and cnuca hyt eal togadere and
wyrce/ to clyðan and lege to þan sare; þanne sceal hit bersten and
hælige sona after.
 19.13.15. <foreign>Ad cecitatem oculorum</foreign> Þis scal wyð þare eagene
tyddernesse, heallswa Hypcras þe læce hyt cydde.
 19.13.17. Þæt ys ærest, þæt ðæt sar becymþ on
ða eagen mid mycelre hætan; hwilum hit cymð on mid wæten, þæt hi
beoð toþundene, and hwilum buton ælce sore, þat hi ablindiað, and
hwilum of þan flewsan, þe of þan eagean yrnaþ.
 19.13.21. Þanne sceal hy man þus lacnian: Gif seo unhælþe
cymþ of þare drigan hætan, þanne niman man ane clæþ and waxen
þa eagan mid þan claðe, dyppe hine on watere and gnide þa eagean mid;
and gif hi beoþ toswollene oððer blodes fulle, ðanne scel mann settan
horn þ þunwangan.
 19.13.25. And gif hy ablindiaþ butan ælcon sare, sylle hym
drincan catarcum, and he byð gehaled; and eftsona, gif ani þing innan þa
eagen byfulþ, þanne sceal man nime mede oððer wyfes meolc and do innan
þa eagen, and hym byð sona bet.
 20.13.30. Wið totore egean; Þis sceal to þan eagen, se
geslegen byð oððer toregan: Nim berbeneleaf and cnuca hy swyþe, wyrc
anne cliðan swylc an litel cicel and lege uppan þa eagan anne dæge and
ana niht.
 20.15.1. Eftsona nim attrumu and hunig and þæt hwita of
æge, meng togadere, lage to þan eagean; hym byð sona sel.
 21.15.3. Eftsona wið þan ylcan; Nim niwne cysan and screda hyne
on weallendan wætere and nim þanne cyse and maca elswa litles cicles and
bynd/ to þan eagean ane niht.
 22.15.7. <foreign>Contra glaucomata</foreign> Þis sceal wyð eagena dymnysse,
þæt Grecas nemniað glaucomata, þæt ys eagena dymnesse.
 22.15.9. Þus me hyne sceal læcnige: Nim wifes meolce þry
sticcæs fulla and cyleþena, id est celidonia wos, anne sticce fulne and
alewan and croh, safran gallice, and meng æl þas togadere and wring ðurh
linnenne claþ and do þanne þa sealfan inna þa eagen.
 23.15.14. <foreign>Item contra cecitatem</foreign> Þis sceal wyð eagen
tyddernyssa, þe beoþ on þan ægmoran sara: Nim myrta and lege hy on
hunige and nym þanne ða myrta and lege to þan eagean, þæt þa eagen
toðinden, and nim þanne rudan and cnuca hy and meng axan to and lege
sydþan to þan eagen; þanne ærest byt heo, swyle þa brewas, and after
þan heo hyt glewylce gehælð.
 24.15.21. <foreign>Ad eos, qui non possunt uidere a sole donec ad occasum:
Ad nectalopas</foreign> þæt ys on ure þeodum þe man, þe ne mæge nenig
geseo after sunna upgange, ær sunna eft on setl ga.
 24.15.24. Þanne is þis ðe læcecræft, þe þe
þærto gebyreþ: Nim buccan hwurfban and bræde hit, and þanne þeo
bræde geswate, nim þanne ðæt swot and smyre mid þa eagen, and after
þan ete þa ylcan braden; and nim þanne niwe assan tord and wrynge hit;
nime ðanne þæt wos and smyrege þa eagen mid, and hym byð sone bet.
 25.17.1. <foreign>Ad ordiolum</foreign> Þis sceal wyð þat, þe on eagen
beoþ, þæt Grecas hatað ordiolum.
 25.17.2. Þæt ys þe læcecræft, ðe þarto gebyreð:
Nim beremele and cned hyt mid hunige, lege to þan eagen; þes
læcecræft/ hys fram manigum mannum afanded.
 26.17.6. <foreign>Item ad idem</foreign> Eftsana nim beana melu and sapan, meng
togadere and lege to þan eagen.
 27.17.9. <foreign>Item</foreign> Þis man sceal don þan mane, þe ne mæg
slapan: Nim wermod and gnid on wine oððer on wearme wætere and drinca,
and hym byð sona bet.
 28.17.13. <foreign>Ad sternutationem</foreign> Þis ys þa tylung to þan manne,
þe wel gefnesan ne mæge and micel nearnesse on þa heafedan habbaþ.
 28.17.15. Þis ys þe læcecraft, þe þarto gebyreð: Nim
castorium oððer elleborum and wyrc to duste and do hyt innan þa nosan,
and hyt bringð forð þane fnæst.
 29.17.19. <foreign>Ad infirmitatem labiorum et lingue</foreign> Eftsona þes
læcedom sceal þan manne, ða hyra lippa beoð sare, oððer hyra tunga
and seo ceola swa sær byþ, þæt he hearfoðlice hys spatel forswelgan
mæg.
 29.17.22. Þus hym man sceal tiligan: Nim fifleafan and drige to
duste and meng hunige þanne þarto; nim ðanne se sealfe and smire mid þa
lippa and ða geaglas innan, and hym byð sona bet.
 30.17.26. <foreign>Eis, qui sobito obmutescunt</foreign> Þisne læcecræft man
sceal don þan manne, ða færinga adumbiaþ: Nim dworgedwostlan, hoc est
pollegia, and do hi on ecede and nim þanne anne linnenne clæð and do
þa dworgedwostlan on innan and do þanne benyþan his nosu, and he mæg
specan sona.
 31.19.1. <foreign>Item ad infirmitatem lingue</foreign> Wið þam, þe se streng
under þare tunga toswollen byð; Þisne læcecræft mæn sceal don
þan mannum, þe se streng under þare tunge toswollen byð; and þurh
þanne streng ærest ælc untrumnesse on þane man becumð.
 31.19.5. Þanne nim þu ærest þane cyrnel, þe byð innan
þan persogge, and cyrfetan cyrnel and cawelstelan, cnuca togædere, and
ceorf þane streng under þara tunga and do þat dust on innan, and hym byd
sona bet.
 32.19.9. Wyð þæt flæsc, ðe abute þe teþ wuxt; <foreign>Ad
ginciuas</foreign> þe Grecas hæteð, þæt ys on ure þeodum þæt
flæsc, ðe abute þa teþ wuxt and þa teþ awegð and astyreþ: Nim
forcorfen leac and cnuca hyt and wring þæt wos of anne sticcan fulne and
ecede anne sticcan fulne and huniges þry sticcan fulle and do, þæt hyt
welle þrywa.
 32.19.14. Nim þanne swa hætte swa he hattest forbere mæge,
and habban an dæl on hys muþe, forte acoled beo; þanne eftsona oðer
dæl eallswa; þane þæt þriddan dæl eallswa.
 33.19.18. <foreign>Ad dentes</foreign> Þes lacecraft ys to ðan menniscan
toþan, ðat Grecas nemneþ organum, þæt ys on ure geþeodan bysse
genemned, forþan þurh þa teþ seo blissa sceal uppspringan and manna
arwyrþnys and ealle nydþearfnys on þan toþan ys, ælc man wyte
mæg, and þan toþa þa tunga to spæce gesteal ys.
 33.19.23. Þanne, þæt Greccas nemnes, ys ærest tritumes,
þæt synden þa fyrst teþ, þe ærest þane mete underfoð.
 33.19.25. Oþre Greccas nemneð eumotici, þæt sindon þe
teþ, þe þane mete brecaþ, syþþe þa forme hyne underfangene
habbæt.
 33.19.27. Þann Grecces nemneþ sume molides, þæt we
hæteð grindingteþ, fore hy grindeþ æl, þæt man bygleofaþ.
 33.19.29. Anð oft mann smeaþ, hwæþer teþ bænene beon,
forþan þe ælc ban mearh hæfþ and hy nan mearh nabbaþ.
 33.19.31. Anð oþre bæn, þeah hi beon tobrocene, mid suman
læcecræfte hy man mai hælen, and nafre þane toþ, gif he tobrocen
beoþ.
 33.21.2. Oft of þan heuede se wyrsta wate cumþ to þan toþan
on þare gelicnesse, þe hyt of huse dropað on stan, þan hyt vinð, and
þane stan þurhþurleþ and þurhþreawþ, ealswa þa ufe wæte of
þan heafod fylþ uppan þa teþ and hy þane þurhþreawþ and deþ,
þæt hy rotigeþ and toþinddaþ, þat þa teþ þoligean ne mæge
ne hæte ne ceald and swyþest þa grindingeþ, þe alc mid feower
wyrtrume/ gefæstned byð; and þane hy hero wurtruma forleataþ, þanne
sweratiged hy and fealled.
 33.21.10. Þanne ys se læcecræft þarto: Nim sumne dæl
of heortes hyde and anne niwne croccan and do wæter on and seoþ swa
swyþe, þæt hit þriwa wylle, swa swyðe swa wæterflæsc.
 33.21.13. Nim þanne þat wæter, and habbe on hys muþe, swa
wearm swa he forbere mæge, fort hyt acoled beon, and þanne hyt si col,
wyrpe hyt ut of hys muþe and nime eft wearmre and do yt eft col ut, and byð
sona bet.
 34.21.17. <foreign>Item ad idem</foreign> Eftsona nim piper and alewen and sealt and
leaces sæd and hunig and meng eal togadere.
 34.21.19. Nim þanne se sealfe and gnid þa teþ mid, and þa
sealfe aflymþ fram þa toþa eall þæt yfel.
 35.21.22. <foreign>Item ad idem</foreign> Eftsona nim hwitne stor and laurberigie
and ecede, meng heal togadere, nym þanne ane panne and wlece hyt eall
togadere, þæt hyt wlæc beo, and habbe on hys muþe swa wlac.
 36.21.26. <foreign>Ad yfam</foreign> Þes lacecræft deah wyð þone huf: Nim
piper and cumyn and rudan þreora scyllinga gewyht, and do þarto anne
sticcan fulne huniges.
 36.21.29. Nimm þanne ane clæne panne and seod þa scealfe,
þæt heo wel wealle. and styre hy swyþe, gemang þan þe heo welle; nim
an/ clæne fæt and do hy on; and syle hym etan þanne twegen sticcan
fulle a æfen, twegen a morgen, and byþ sona hæl.
 37.23.1. <foreign>Pro inflatione gutturis</foreign> For mannes þrote, þe byð
toswolle; Þes lacecræft deaþ, gif þæs mannes þrota toswollen
byð and þa ceola, þæt Greccas brahmas hataþ.
 37.23.4. Þis ys þe læcecræft: Sule hym supan gebræddan
hrere ægeran and hunig to and do hym bryð of meolce gemaced, and syle hym
ceruillan etan and fæt flæsc, þæt beo wel gesoden, etan, and he byd
sona hal.
 38.23.8. <foreign>Ad strictum pectus</foreign> Þes lacecraft sceal þan manne,
þe nerwnysse byð æt þare heortan and æt ðare þrotu, þæt he
uneþe specan mægan.
 38.23.10. Þæt scealt þu hym þus don: Nim leac and cnuca
hit and wring þat wos of, syle hym supan, and hym byð sona bet.
 39.23.13. <foreign>Item ad idem</foreign> Eft nim beana and ele and seoð þa
beana on eala and syle hym etan, and hy doþ þa nearwnysse aweg.
 40.23.16. <foreign>Ad vocem perditam recuperandam</foreign> Þisne læcecraft man
sceal don þan manne, þe hura stemna offylþ, ðæt Greccas nemneþ
catulemsis.
 40.23.18. Þus þu hine scealt lacnian: Do hym
forhæfædnysse on mete and læt hine beo on stille stowe; nim þanne
godre butere twegen sticcan fulle and anne sticcan fulne huniges and wyll
togadere and læt hine swelgan þa sealfe leohtlice; and sile hym þanne
leohtne/ mete, and drinca win, and hym cymþ bote.
 41.23.24. <foreign>Ad inflationem gutturis</foreign> Wid mannes ceola, þe byð
sær; Þisne læcecræft man sceal don manne, þe byd þe ceola sar,
þæt Greccas hæteþ gargarisis: Nim niwe beane and puna, nim þanne
eced oþþer win and seoð se beanna and nim ele and meng þarto, oþþer
spic, gif man ele nabbe, and do þarto; wille on ana panna.
 41.25.3. Nim þanne wylle and dype on þare scealfe and bind þa
wulle to þare ceolan.
 42.25.5. <foreign>Ad colli infirmitatem</foreign> Wyð hneccan sar; Þes
læcedon/ is god manne, þe hyra hnecca sær byd and eal se swyra
sargiað swa swiðe, þæt he þane muþ uneaþe to don mæg;
þæt sar Greccas nemneþ spasmus, þæt ys on ure leodene hneccasar.
 42.25.10. Þis ys se læcedom þarto: Nim ane handfulle mintan
and cnuca hy and nim þanne anne sester fulne wines and ane pundes gewyht
eles; meng þane eall togadere and seoð hit swa swyðe, þæt þæs
wines and þæs eles ne sy na mære, þane ær wæs þæs eles,
þa hit drige wæs: wring þanne þurh claþ and wurp aweg þa mintan
and nim wulle and wyrc twegen cliðan of þare wulle.
 42.25.16. Duppe þanne ðonne cliþan on þare sealfe and lege
to þan hneccan, þanne eftsona þane oþþerne and do þanne oþþerne
aweg; do þus fiftine syþun; nim þanne oþþre wulle and wyrm to
heorþe, þæt heo beo swyþe wearm, and bynd to þan hneccan; þanne
byn twan tide do þa wylle aweg and nim þa ylcan clyþan, þe þar ær
wæran: do þarto on þa ylcan wisan, þe þu ær dydest.
 43.25.23. Wið þan yfelan on mannes swure; Þisne
læcecræft man sceal don mannum, þe hyra swyran mid þan sinum fortogen
beoþ, þæt he hys næn geweald nah, þæt Greccas hætað
tetanicus.
 43.25.26. Þys adle ys þreora cynna: Þæt an cynn Greccas
hætað tetanicas, þat syndan þa menn, þa rihte gað wið
uppaþenedan swyran and ne magan abugan fora untrumnesse.
 43.25.29. Anð þa oþer adle sit þus on þan swuran,
þæt sa syna teoð fram þan cynne to þan breostan, þæt he þane
muþ atyne ne mæg fore syna getoge; and þæge adle Greccas nemneð
brostenus.
 43.25.32. And þe þrydde adle sitt þus on þa swyran,
þæt sa syna teoþ fram þan cynnbane to þan sculdre and þane muþ
awoh breddad.
 43.27.2. Do hym ærest þanne þisne læcecræft: Wyrce
hym arest hnesce bedd and maca wearm fyr; þanne sceal hym man læten blod
on þan earme on þan middemyste ædra.
 43.27.5. And gif þan gehæled ne byd, þanne teo hym man blod
ut betweoxan þan sculdran mid horne: nim þanne eald wyn and ealde rusel;
nim þanne ane panne and seoð þane rusel and þat wyn swa swyþe, fort
se rusel habbe bedruncan þat wyn; nim þanne wulle and tæs hy and maca
hy swylce anne clyþa and lege þa scealfe on uppan and bynd þanne to
þan sare myd ane clæþe.
 44.27.12. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsona nym buteran and ele and meng
togædere; nim þanne winberian coddes and galpania and anan and cnuca eall
togadere and wyl in ðare buteran and on þan ele and do to þan sare,
ealswa hyt beforan seið; do hym þanne hnesce mettas and godne drincan,
healswa hit beforen seið, swylce wile, swa hym he beþurfe.
 45.27.19. <foreign>Ad pormones, id est ad infirmitatem manuum</foreign> Þes
læcecræft is god wyð sare handum and þara fingra sare, þæt
Greccas hataþ pormones, and on leden perniciam man hyt hæt: Nim hwitne
stor and seolferun syndrun and swefel and meng togadere, nim þanne ele and
meng þarto; wurm þanna sa handa and smyra þarmid: bewynd þanne þa
handan mid linnen claþe.
 46.27.26. <foreign>Item ad infirmitatem mannum</foreign> Wyð sare handa; Wyð
þa handa, þe þæt fell of gað; Þis hys to þan handan, þæt
þat fel of gæþ and þæt flæsc tospringad: Nym winberian, þe
beoþ acende æfter oþþre berigian, and cnuca ahy swyþe smale and do
hy on buteran swyþe and smure þæt sar gelomelice mid; bærne þanne
streuw and nime þa axan and strewe þaruppe.
 47.29.1. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eft nim dracentan wyrtrume and puna hy smale and
wyll hy on hunige and lege þanne uppan hændan.
 48.29.4. <foreign>Ad infirmitatem mannum</foreign> To handum; Þis lacecræft
sceal to þan handan, þe þæt fell of pyleþ: Nim betan ane handfulle
and lactucan ane handfulle and coliandrone ane handfulle and cnuca eall
togadere; nim þanne cruman and do on wæter and þa wyrt mid and wurme
þanne wel þa wurtan on þan wæter and þa cruman mid; wyrc þanne
clyþan þarof and bind uppan þa handan ane niht and do þus þa lange,
þe hit beþurfe.
 49.29.13. <foreign>Item ad vnguem scabiosam</foreign> Þis sceal to scurfedan
næglum: Nim plumsewes anes scyllinges gewyht and swegles æpples twegean
scyllenges gewyht and cnuca hy togadere; smyre þa næglas mid and læt hy
beon swa gesmyrede.
 50.29.18. <foreign>Ad eos, qui non habent appetitum ad cibum</foreign> Þis hys god
ta þan mann, þe hura metes ne lyst, þæt Greccas hataþ blaffesis, and
Ypocras seggeþ, þæt seo untrunyss cymþ of þrim þingum, oþþer
of cyle, oþþer of miclum hæte and drince, oþþer of lytte þte and
drince, oþþer of miclum wernesse.
 50.29.23. Gif hyt cumeþ of þan cyle, þanne scealt þu hym
helpan mid baþe; gif hyt cymet of mycele drence, þanne scel he habba
forhæfdnysse; gif hyt cymeþ of mycle swynce oþþer of earfodnysse,
þanne scealt þu hym don eced wyd hunige gemenged oþþer drinccan ecede
wyd leac gemenged.
 50.31.1. Gif þa untrumnysse cumþ of þan cyle, þanne nim
þu beferes herþan and barne to duste and grind piper and meng piper and
þæt dust togadere and nim sticcan fulne þas gemengede dustes and do in
ane cuppefulle wynes and wlece þanne þæt win mid þan duste and sile
hym drinca.
 50.31.6. Oþþer nim peretrum wyð mede gemenged, swa micel swa
gemenged wæs þæs oþþeres, and sile hym drince.
 51.31.9. <foreign>Ad strictum pectus, siue ad asmaticos</foreign> Þisne læcedon
do þan manne, þa hym beoð on hyra brosten nearuwe, þat Greccas
hæteð asmaticos, þæt ys nearunyss; and uneaþe mæg þane
fnæst to do and utabringan and hæfd hæte breost and byd innen mid
micle nearnysse; and hwilan he blod hræcþ and hwylum mid blode gemenged,
and hwile he riþaþ, swylce he on dueorge sy; and micel spatel on ceola
wyxeþ and syhþ adun on þara lungane.
 51.31.16. And þus byð þat yfel acenned: Ærest þur mycele
æteþ and drincas þæt yfel hym on innan wyxt and rixað swa swyþe,
þæt hym næþer ne meteþ ne ealaþ ne lyst.
 51.31.19. Þus þu scealt hine halan: Do hyne into þan huse,
þe beo næþer ne to hæt ne to ceald, and læt hym læce blod on
þan wynstran earme, gef he þare ylde hafeþ; gif þu þanne on þan
earme ne mæge, þanne sceal þu hym læten blod mid cyrfetum betwex
þan scoldrum on þa ylcan wysa, þe mann mid horne deð.
 51.31.24. Gyf wyntra sy, þanne scealt þu niman pollegian and
seoð hy on watere, nim þanne þa wyrta and wyrce togadere swa micel swa
celrus; þacc yt þanne gelomelice mid þan wermum wætere betwex þan
sculdrun/ oþþer mid harehunan, gif þu dueorgeduostle næbbe.
 51.31.29. And gif þur þis hæl ne beon, nim uentuosam and
lege under þa earmes and anbutan þane mægen and nim þane fele cyne
wyrta and wyrc to sealfe and smeri abotan þan mæge mid sare selfe; nim
þane hnesce wulle and dupe on ele, þe beo of cypressan, and smyre anne
clæþ mid þan ele and wrið þane clæþ abutan þan mægan and
smyre abutan þane swyran mid þan ele and abutan þa hrigbræde
geloemelice/.
 51.33.3. Wyrc þanne clydan of eorþan, þa mann nemneþ nitro,
þa byþ fundan on Ytalia, and do þar piper to and lege to þan sare, fort
þe man wearmie; nym þanne narð and pintreowes sæp and panic and wyrc
þær drenc and syle hym drince.
 51.33.7. Nim þanne eft cicenamete ane handfulle and þry
æpple of celidonia; nim þanne ane healfne sester wynes and seoþ hi, fort
hy beon wel gesodene; syle hym þanne drincan þry dæges, ælce dæg

 52.33.11. <foreign>Item ad pectus</foreign> Þes læcedom sceal to þan mann,
þe byð yfele on þan breostam.
 52.33.13. Þur þa breost fela freccenysse synden, þe on þe
manne becumeþ.
 52.33.14. And soþ hys, þæt ælc wæte cymd ærest ut
of þan magan, and þur þane wæten þa breost beoþ geheafugede and
þa heorte ge sydu byð gefullede mid yfele blode; and æfter þan ealle
