and þa eaxle særgeaþ and sa sculdraþ teoþ togadere, and hyt pricaþ
innan þan sculdru and on þan hrigge swilce þar þornas on sy, and hys
andwlita byð eall awend.
 52.33.21. Þanne þu þas tacnunge seo on þan manna, þanne
scealt þu hym blod lætan; and gif þu ne dest, hit cym hym to mucele and
stranga adle, forþan þa æddra and þa lime beoþ gefullede myd
mucellere fulnesse.
 52.33.24. Forþan we byddaþ æræst, þæt mann hym
wyrce/ speaudrenc, forþan eal þæt yfel, þe byð on þare heorta and
on þan breoste, eall yt sceal þanne ut and beo þa heorta and þa breost
and þæt heafod swa wel geclansæd.
 52.33.28. And gif he þanne þa spatl swyþe utspæte, þanne
hys þat þe hyfela wæte, þe on þan heafode rixaþ; and eall se
lichama geswæred byþ and gehefeguþ, eal swylc he of mycele swynce come,
and ealle he byþ geswenced and, bute he þe hraþar gehæled beo, hyt cum
hym to mycele yfele.
 52.35.1. Þus man hine sceal læcnie: He hine forhabban wyð
feala cunna metas and drencas and wyð gebræd flæsc and wið ælces
orffes flæsc, þe cudu ceowe, and drince leoht wyn, þæt hym ne
þyrste.
 52.35.4. Ac ceowe hwytes cuduwys sæd and fiffingran ælce
dæg, ær he etan; and wite þu gewyslice, gif he mid earfodnysse hwest
and yt uthræcþ, þanne hys þæt clænsunga þara breosta.
 52.35.7. Þanne sceal he etan drigne hlaf and cyse, and ne cume he
on nane cyle, þe hwile þe he seoc beo, ac beo on wermum huse, and hæte
hym man bæþ swa hraþa, swa hys wisa godige.
 52.35.10. Nim þanne earixena wyrtruman and glædene more and
swearte mintan and mucgwurt and drige to duste and do þær æcern to,
oþþer hwætena flysma; mengc togædera, meng þar þanne hunig to and
wynberigea/ coddes and pices sum dæl and hwyttre gosu smere; seoð þanne
eall togadera on anu niwe croccan; nim þanne wulle, þe ne com næfre
awaxen, wyrc cliþan þærof, lege þæruppa þa sealfe wel þicce.
 52.35.17. Wyrð þanne to þan breostan, swa hæt swa he
hattest forberan mæge; þanne þeo beo acoled, lege oþerne wearme
þarto, and do þus ðe hwyle hym þearf sy; wyrce hym drenc gode, þe
ægþer clænsige ge þa breost ge þane innoþ; and bace hym man
þanne wearmen hlaf be heorþe, and ete þane manige dæges þane hlaf
þe wyrm.
 52.35.22. Nim eft cicenemete and wermod and lauberigan and do hwyt

þane þa breost to heorþan and smyre hy þanne mid þare scealfe.
 53.35.27. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eft nim cicenemete and seoþ on wine; do
þanne ele to, þe beo of frencissen hnutu, and drince þæt.
 54.35.30. Wyð þan scearpan bane, þe betweox þan breostan
byþ; Þus man sceal wyrcean þane cliþan to þan scearpan bane, þe
betweox þan breostum byð, gif hyt sar sig: Nim ealdne swynes risel twegea
punda gewiht and wexas syx scyllinga gewyht and eles swa mycel and þæt
sæpp of cypresso swa micel and fearres smere fif scillinga wyht and panecis

smere anes sceallinges wyht and euforbeo swa micel, and pyne æl togadere and
do in ane boxs, and nime syþþan swa oft swa he beþurfe.
 55.37.10. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsona to þan ylcan: Nim niwe butera twegen
dæles and þane þriddan dæl nifes huniges and ane gode cuppan fulle

byð, do þæt hunig and þa butera þærto and syle hym þanne drinca
fæstende ane cuppan fulle.
 56.37.16. <foreign>Ad vmbilicum</foreign> Þisne læcedon man sceal do þan
manne, se his nafulsceaft intyhþ.
 56.37.18. Nim eormeleaf and seoþ and wyrð þanne swa hæt
uppan þane nafelon.
 57.37.20. <foreign>Ad idem</foreign> Eftsona to þan ylcan: Nim hwit cudu and

streuwa uppa ane clæþe and bynd swa hate uppa þane nafelan.
 58.35.24. Wið heortan and sidane sore <foreign>Ad morbum cordis et
lateris</foreign> Wyð heortan ge sydu unhæle; Þisne læcedom mann sceal do
þan mann, þeo beo on heora heortan ge sidu unhale.
 58.37.28. Þus þu scealt þat yfel ongyta on þan manne: Hym
byd hynnene eall swylce he si eall tobrocen, and he hwest swyþe hefelice and
micelne hefe gefret æt hys heortan, and þat he uthræcþ, byþ swyþe
þicce and hæfet hwyt hyw.
 58.39.1. Þan scealt þu hine þus læcnigean: Nim grene helda
and cnuca hy swyþe smale and nim ane æg and þa wrut and swyng togadere;
nim þanne swynes smere and ana clæna panne, wylle þanne þa wurt mid
þan æge on þan swunes smere innan þare panne, fort hyt genoh beo, and
sile him fæstenda eta; and æfter þan he sceal fæsten seofan tide,
ær he ænigne oþerne mete etan.
 58.39.7. And gif nabbe grene helda, nime þat dust and mæcige
mid þan æge and bruce þysses læcecræft, fort he byð hæl.
 59.39.10. <foreign>Ad eos, qui nimis saliuam conspuunt</foreign> Þis sceal þan
manna to læcecræfte, þe swyþe hyra spatl utspiwaþ, and hy habbaþ
swyþe/ heue magan.
 59.39.12. Þanne ys god, þæt mann foresceawie, hwanne seo
seocnysse sig, forþan þeos ædle ne eglad ælce manne gelice.
 59.39.14. Sume men hyt eagles hof þas heafedes wæten, and
sume men hyt eagles, þanne hi fæstende beoþ, and hy swyþust hyre spatl
utspiwaþ, of hy fulle beoþ, and næfre hy ne swycaþ, ac þanne hi
hungrie beoþ.
 59.39.18. Þu miht þa adle gecnawa, forþan of þara hæten
byþ þæt spatl tolysed, and þa micele spatl of þara mycele hæte,
ealswa þæt treow, þæt man on heorþe leges; for þare mycele
hæten, þe þæt treow barned beoþ, þare wylþ ut of þan ende
water.
 59.39.22. Þus þu hyne scealt læcgnie: Nim gingyfran twelf
penega wyht and piperes feower and twentiga penega gewhyt and hunige heahta and
feorwertig penega gewyht; meng þanne eal þas togadere and sille hym

 60.39.27. <foreign>Ad acidiua</foreign> Wyþ þæt hæte wæter, þe scyt
upp of þan breosten; <foreign>Ad acidiua</foreign> þæt hys þæt hæte wæter,
þe scet upp of þan breostan and hwylan of þa mæge.
 60.39.30. Þanne sceal he drinca fif handfulle scealtes

 60.41.1. And nim eftsona wermodes sæd and seoþ hyt on watere
and menge þærto wyn and drince hyt þanne.
 60.41.3. Eallswa nim þro pipercorn oþþer fif and hete hyt.

 60.41.7. Eftsona nim lufestices sæd ane handfulle and ete hyt.
 61.41.8. <foreign>Potus prouocans vomitum</foreign> Þes lacecræft sceal þan

 61.41.9. Wyte þu gewyslice, þæt se speaudrenc deaþ hym

 61.41.14. Eall þe drenc afyrsaþ and aclænsaþ þa hylc
þing, swa þar weaxan, þe byð to yfele in þan mann; þur þane drenc

 61.41.17. Þe spæudrenc ys god ær mete and betra æfter

þæs yfeles wætan on þan heafede and þæt oferflawende yfel on

gellan byð eac astired; þanne þur þane dreng he byd afeormud and ne
geþafaþ, þæt þær ænig yfel wæta beo gesamnad innan þan

 61.41.23. Þus þu scealt þane spæawdrenc wyrcean: Nim smale
napes and lege hy on eced and do þar hunig to and læt hy licgean ane niht
þæron ofgotene; ete þanne a morgen, fort he full sy, drince þanne

 61.41.27. Nim þanne an feðere and dyppe on ele and stynge on
hys muþe, oþþer his fingers do on hys muþ, þæt he þane
spæudrenc astyrie.
 61.41.29. And eftsona: Nim cuppan fulle wæteres and sealtes and
meng swyþe togadere, of þæt sealt moltan sy; do hyt þanne on ane
croccan an nyht, nim hyt a morgen and dreahne hit þurh linnen clæþ and
syle him drinca.
 61.41.32. Þanne se drenc hyne styrge, þanne sile him drince
gelomlice wearm wæter, þæt he þa bet spiwe.
 62.43.1. <foreign>Item: Potus leuior ad vomitum</foreign> And eft, gyf þu wylle,
sile hym leohtran dreng.
 62.43.2. Nim þanne wearm wæter and syle hym drincan, duppe
þanne a feþer on ele and do on hys muþ, oþþer hys fingres, and he
spiþ sona.
 62.43.5. Eftsona nim endlufun leaf of bulgagine, ofgeot hy ane

 62.43.8. Nim eft eallan wyrte wos swa wearm twegea dæles and

 62.43.11. And nim eftsana grene cyrfætan an handfulle and do hy

 62.43.13. And eftsona nim curfettan wyrtruman and cnuca hy and

 63.43.19. <foreign>Contra nimium vomitum</foreign> Þisne lacecræft mann sceal
don manne, þæt swyþe spywaþ, gif wullaþ, þat hit astonden,
þæt Greccas hateþ apoxerrisis; þæt sinden þa menn, þa after

hwylan ær hy etan, hy spiwaþ, and þe mæga sargað, and þe innoþ

se ansine and þa fet beoþ toswollen, and his anwlita byþ blac, and his
migga byþ hwit, and he sceal gelomelice migan.
 63.43.27. Þus þu scealt hine hrædlice læcnige: Gif þa
ylda habbe, læt hym blod of bam þa foten byneoþan ancleowe; swa si
þæt blod forlæte, þæt eallunga se seocca ne getorige, and þa
þing, þe þane magen healdeþ, þæt hy næfre forþan forwyrþan,
and þeo oþru blodlæse ys, þe þu þane seoccan læcnige scealt,
þæt ys, þæt þu hym scealt lætan blod under þare tuncgan,
þæt þeo blodlæse þane mann alihte: and æfter þæt seo
blodlæse si gefylled, þu hine scealt scearpigean.
 63.43.35. Nim þann sealt and gnid þa wunda mid; nim þanne
cicenamete and wyllecærsen and eorme leafes sæd and seoþ hy on watere;
hwonlice meng þarto ele and hunige and wyrc þanne clyþan þerof and lege

 63.45.4. Eftsona nim gladenan and hlutter pic and meng togadere and

cnuca þanne eall þas togadere and magce togadere, meng þarto þanne

 63.45.8. Eftsona nim alewen and myrra and hwit cudu and ægra

 63.45.12. Nim þanne ele, seoð þa wyrta, wyrma þanne þa

 63.45.24. Wyð þan ylcan: Nym betonican swa grene and gnid hy on

 63.45.26. Nim eft bettonican þreora scyllange gewyht and seoð

 63.45.30. Eft nim saluian ane handfulle and cnuca hy swyþe smale

 63.47.3. Nim eft dyles sædes twelf penega gewiht and piperes

 63.47.7. Eftsona, gif se man spiwan, and he ne mage etan: Syle him

 63.47.9. Eftsona, gif man sy gewunulic, þæt hyne þyrete:

 63.47.12. Eftsona nim elenam and spelter and seoþ on wine and

 63.47.13. Þis ys seo selesta drenc wyð þæt broc.
 63.47.14. And wyð þan ylcan: Genym hwit cude and alewan and

 63.47.16. Nim þann linnenne clæð and lege þa sealfe uppan,
bynð/ þann ofer þane mægen.
 63.47.18. Þann clansaþ þa scealfe þane innoþ and þa
werinysse aweg gedeð and þann magan gewyrmþ.
 63.47.19. Wyþ þan ylcan: Nim swefles ehta penega gewyhta and
cnuca hine smale; nim þann an hrere bræd æg and do hyt on innan and
sile hym etan.
 63.47.22. Eftsona, gif þu wylt þe werinyssa aweg don of þan
mann, þann þat yfel hyne geþreadne hæfð, of ðe þurft aweg adon:
Nim hwyt cudu and gyngyfere and recels and lauwinberigean and cost, ælces
þissa emfela; nim þann of oþþrum pyhmentum ane sticcan fulne and gnid
hy eal togadere; nim þann wateres twegen dales and wines þann þriddan
dal, meng þann eall togadere and syle him drincan.
 64.47.29. <foreign>Ad emoptoycos, latine dicitur reiectatio: Ad emoptoycos</foreign>
þæt Greccas hateð amatostax, þæt ys on ledene genemned reiectatio,
and on englisc ys haten blodrine.
 64.49.1. Þus him egleþ se blodrine: Hwilum þurh þa nosa hym
yrnþ þæt blod, hwilum þane on arsganga sitt, hyt hym fram yrnaþ.
 64.49.3. Ac þa ealde læces sædan, þæt þeos þrowung
ys geset of feofer þingum, þæt ys of þan breoste and of þan magan
and of ædran and of þan þearman.
 64.49.5. Galwenus se læce hyt of hys snotornysse þus wrat: Gif
hyt on þan breoste byð oþþer on þan magan, þanne þurh þann
spiþan þu hyt miht gecnawen; gif hyt byþ on þan ædran oþþer of
þare bladre, þu miht þurh þane miggan hyt gecnawan.
 65.49.10. <foreign>Si dolor et infirmitas sit in visceribus</foreign> Gif hit byð
of þan þerman, þanne myht þu þurh þane arsgang hyt gecnawan.
 65.49.12. Hit byþ ongyton on sume manne, þæt þæt blod
hym ut of þan heafode utwylþ, and on suma hwilum, þæt hyt utsprinþ
þur þa twa litlan þurlu, þa innan þara ceolan beoþ, forþan þa
ædran beoþ tobrocone, þa inna þa þurlu beoþ.
 65.49.16. And hwilun of þare ceolan þæt blod utwylþ,
hwilum of goman, hwylum of þan scearpan banum, þe bytweox þan breostan
byþ, and hwylum of þare lungone, hwylum of þan magen, hwylum of þan
innoþe, hwilum of þan lendune.
 65.49.20. Þis ys þæt gescead þara lacnunge: Gif þat blod
oþ þan heafode wyll, þus þu scealt hyt agytan: He hwest hefelice, and
sindrig blod he utracþ.
 65.49.22. Þane, gif þa adra byþ tobrocen innan þan þurlu,
of/ þan uue dropaþ uppan þa tunga, and of þara tungan hyt ingehwyrfþ
and he agynþ to brecanne, þane to spiwanne.
 65.49.25. Þann gif hyt cumþ of þare þrotan, þus þu hyt
scealt agitan: Þann he hwest, þann smyit hys tunge, and he uthræþ
wurmsig blod, and þeo þrutu byþ mid sare gemenged, swa swiþe, þæt
he hyt utan gefret.
 65.49.28. Gif hyt of þan goman byþ butan blode, and swiðe
uthreæcþ, þann todo þu hys muþ, and hawa, hwæþer hys ceaflas
sin toswollene, and he eaþelic nan þing forswoligon ne mæg.
 65.49.31. Þann, gif hyt of þan scearpe bane byþ, þæt he
sarlice hwest, and blod utspiuwþ and micel blod astyreþ and gif gæd, hys
breost beoð gesargude, þann wite þu gewyslice, þæt þa adran synd
tobrocene, þe on þa þurlun synd gesette.
 65.51.4. Þann, gif þat blod of þa lungune cymþ, þæt
agyt þu hyt þus, gif þat blod beo swyþe read and clane ut to spiwanne,
and he mid hwostan hyt uthræcþ butun alcum sare.
 65.51.7. Gif þat blod of þan innoþe flowe, þæt wyte
þu, þæt sindon wunda on þan þearmum, and þann he to arsganga
gæþ, þanne þæt hym fram gæþ, byþ swyþe wyþ blode
gemenged.
 65.51.10. And þann, gif hyt byþ of renys, oþþer þan
lendene, þane cumþ þæt blod of þara blæddran; and þæt he
myhþ, byþ sweart oþþer hwyt oþþer read, forþan of yfelre adle
becymþ þis þing on þan mann.
 65.51.13. Þus þu hyne scealt lacnige: Do hyne on wearme huse
and on beorht and bedde hys bed myd morsecge oppan þara eorþa.
 65.51.15. And he hyne sceal forhabban wyþ fela þingas: þis ys
ærest wyþ micele spæce; and wyþ yrsunga and wyþ hamed þing and
fram alce furwerfetum flæsce and fram smyce and fram alce ungeþilde,
forþan þa addran berstað hwyla for þan miceles blodes þinge, þe on
þan/ lichama and on addra byþ.
 66.51.21. <foreign>Ipocras dicit quod quidam plures venas quam alii
habeant</foreign> Ipocras se læce atwuwde, þæt on sumum lichama beoþ ma addra,
þane on sume, and þe lichama byþ wearmra, þann se þe smalran addran
and þa swa feawa ann beoþ.
 66.51.26. Þane þe lichama and þa addran beoþ þæs
yfelan blodes fulle, þann scealt þu hym læten blod on þan earme, gif
he þara hulde habban; and wyrc hym siþþan twegen firesce clyþan and
bind oþerne betwex þa sculdru, oþerne betweox þa breoste and syle hym
ealra ærest etan gebrædne swam.
 66.51.30. And gif þæt blod utwealle oþan heafode, þann
cnuca þu swam and nim wæter and hunig and meng togadere and sile hym
drincan.
 66.51.32. Nym þann ecede and hunig and meng togadere.
 66.53.1. Nim þane an feþere and dyppe þaron and smyra þann
þa stowe mid.
 66.53.2. Loca, hwær þæt blod utwealle, gif þu þa stowe
geracen mægen.
 66.53.3. Gif þat blod of þara ceolan utwealle, nym cole,
spongiam/ and swam and sealt and cnuca eall togadere and bynd þann þane
clyþan uppa þa þrotan and sile hym ærest drincan finul on hluttrun
wine and sile hym etan nywe beoblæd; and hym byd sona bet.
 66.53.8. And gif þat blod on þara lungane si, þane nim
wegbrædan and cnuca hig and wring þarof þæt wos and drinc.
 66.53.10. Gif hyt byþ of þan scearpan bane, þa betwex þa
breosta/ byþ, þann nym þu cealde swam and scealt and cnuca togadere; nym
þane spongyam and lege þa scealfe on uppan and bynd to þan breostan;
cnuca þann swam and do hine on watere and drinca hyne butan sealt, and gif he
þare ylde habban, þann læt þu hym blod and bynd þa scealfe to þan
breostan þane.
 67.53.17. Gif þæt blod of þan innoþe cumþ. vii.
